Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa

# Khuddakanikāye

## Theragāthāpāḷi

#### Nidānagāthā

```
Sīhānaṃva <pb ed="T" n="0.0260" /><pb ed="M" n="0.0019" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0161" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0001" /> nadantānaṃ, dāṭhīnaṃ girigabbhare;
```

```
Suṇātha bhāvitattānaṃ, gāthā atthūpanāyikā <note>attūpanāyikā (sī. ka.)</note>.
```

```
Yathānāmā yathāgottā, yathādhammavihārino;
```

```
Yathādhimuttā sappaññā, vihariṃsu atanditā.
```

```
Tattha tattha vipassitvā, phusitvā accutaṃ padaṃ;
```

```
Katantaṃ paccavekkhantā, imamatthamabhāsisuṃ.
```

### 1. Ekakanipāto

#### 1. Paṭhamavaggo

#### 1. Subhūtittheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Channā <pb ed="V" n="0.0162" /> me kuṭikā sukhā nivātā, vassa deva yathāsukhaṃ;
```

```
Cittaṃ me susamāhitaṃ vimuttaṃ, ātāpī viharāmi vassa devā’’ti.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ <note>itthaṃ sumaṃ (ka. aṭṭha.)</note> āyasmā subhūtitthero gāthaṃ abhāsitthāti.

#### 2. Mahākoṭṭhikattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Upasanto <pb ed="M" n="0.0220" /> uparato, mantabhāṇī anuddhato;
```

```
Dhunāti pāpake dhamme, dumapattaṃva māluto’’ti.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mahākoṭṭhiko <note>mahākoṭṭhito (sī. syā.)</note> thero gāthaṃ abhāsitthāti.

#### 3. Kaṅkhārevatattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Paññaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0261" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0002" /> imaṃ passa tathāgatānaṃ, aggi yathā pajjalito nisīthe;
```

```
Ālokadā cakkhudadā bhavanti, ye āgatānaṃ vinayanti kaṅkha’’nti.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kaṅkhārevato thero gāthaṃ abhāsitthāti.

#### 4. Puṇṇattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Sambhireva samāsetha, paṇḍitehatthadassibhi;
```

```
Atthaṃ mahantaṃ gambhīraṃ, duddasaṃ nipuṇaṃ aṇuṃ;
```

```
Dhīrā samadhigacchanti, appamattā vicakkhaṇā’’ti.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā puṇṇo mantāṇiputto <note>mantāniputto (syā. ka.)</note> thero gāthaṃ abhāsitthāti.

#### 5. Dabbattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Yo <pb ed="V" n="0.0163" /> duddamiyo damena danto, dabbo santusito vitiṇṇakaṅkho;
```

```
Vijitāvī apetabheravo hi, dabbo so parinibbuto ṭhitatto’’ti.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā dabbo thero gāthaṃ abhāsitthāti.

#### 6. Sītavaniyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Yo <pb ed="M" n="0.0221" /> sītavanaṃ upagā bhikkhu, eko santusito samāhitatto;
```

```
Vijitāvī apetalomahaṃso, rakkhaṃ kāyagatāsatiṃ dhitimā’’ti.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sītavaniyo thero gāthaṃ abhāsitthāti.

#### 7. Bhalliyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Yopānudī <pb ed="T" n="0.0262" /> maccurājassa senaṃ, naḷasetuṃva sudubbalaṃ mahogho;
```

```
Vijitāvī apetabheravo hi, danto so parinibbuto ṭhitatto’’ti.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bhalliyo thero gāthaṃ abhāsitthāti.

#### 8. Vīrattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Yo duddamiyo damena danto, vīro santusito vitiṇṇakaṅkho;
```

```
Vijitāvī apetalomahaṃso, vīro so parinibbuto ṭhitatto’’ti.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vīro thero gāthaṃ abhāsitthāti.

#### 9. Pilindavacchattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ na durāgataṃ <note>nāpagataṃ (sī. syā.)</note>, nayidaṃ dumantitaṃ mama;
```

```
Saṃvibhattesu dhammesu, yaṃ seṭṭhaṃ tadupāgami’’nti.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pilindavaccho <note>pilindivaccho (sī.)</note> thero gāthaṃ abhāsitthāti.

#### 10. Puṇṇamāsattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Vihari <pb ed="M" n="0.0222" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0164" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0003" /> apekkhaṃ idha vā huraṃ vā, yo vedagū samito yatatto;
```

```
Sabbesu dhammesu anūpalitto, lokassa jaññā udayabbayañcā’’ti.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā puṇṇamāso thero gāthaṃ abhāsitthāti.

Vaggo paṭhamo niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Subhūti <pb ed="T" n="0.0263" /> koṭṭhiko thero, kaṅkhārevatasammato;
```

```
Mantāṇiputto dabbo ca, sītavaniyo ca bhalliyo;
```

```
Vīro pilindavaccho ca, puṇṇamāso tamonudoti.
```

#### 2. Dutiyavaggo

#### 1. Cūḷavacchattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Pāmojjabahulo bhikkhu, dhamme buddhappavedite;
```

```
Adhigacche padaṃ santaṃ, saṅkhārūpasamaṃ sukha’’nti.
```

… Cūḷavaccho <note>cūlagavaccho (sī.)</note> thero….

#### 2. Mahāvacchattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Paññābalī sīlavatūpapanno, samāhito jhānarato satīmā;
```

```
Yadatthiyaṃ bhojanaṃ bhuñjamāno, kaṅkhetha kālaṃ idha vītarāgo’’ti.
```

… Mahāvaccho <note>mahāgavaccho (sī.)</note> thero….

#### 3. Vanavacchattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Nīlabbhavaṇṇā <pb ed="M" n="0.0223" /> rucirā, sītavārī sucindharā;
```

```
Indagopakasañchannā, te selā ramayanti ma’’nti.
```

… Vanavaccho thero….

#### 4. Sivakasāmaṇeragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Upajjhāyo <pb ed="V" n="0.0165" /> maṃ avaca, ito gacchāma sīvaka;
```

```
Gāme <pb ed="T" n="0.0264" /> me vasati kāyo, araññaṃ me gato mano;
```

```
Semānakopi gacchāmi, natthi saṅgo vijānata’’nti.
```

… Sivako sāmaṇero….

#### 5. Kuṇḍadhānattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Pañca chinde pañca jahe, pañca cuttari bhāvaye;
```

```
Pañcasaṅgātigo bhikkhu, oghatiṇṇoti vuccatī’’ti.
```

… Kuṇḍadhāno thero….

#### 6. Belaṭṭhasīsattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāpi bhaddo ājañño, naṅgalāvattanī sikhī;
```

```
Gacchati appakasirena, evaṃ rattindivā mama;
```

```
Gacchanti appakasirena, sukhe laddhe nirāmise’’ti.
```

… Belaṭṭhasīso thero….

#### 7. Dāsakattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Middhī <pb ed="P" n="0.0004" /> yadā hoti mahagghaso ca, niddāyitā samparivattasāyī;
```

```
Mahāvarāhova nivāpapuṭṭho, punappunaṃ gabbhamupeti mando’’ti.
```

… Dāsako thero….

#### 8. Siṅgālapituttheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Ahu <pb ed="M" n="0.0224" /> buddhassa dāyādo, bhikkhu bhesakaḷāvane;
```

```
Kevalaṃ aṭṭhisaññāya, apharī pathaviṃ <note>paṭhaviṃ (sī. syā.)</note> imaṃ;
```

```
Maññehaṃ kāmarāgaṃ so, khippameva pahissatī’’ti <note>pahīyabhi (sabbattha pāḷiyaṃ)</note>.
```

… Siṅgālapitā <note>sīgālapitā (sī.)</note> thero….

#### 9. Kulattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
<note>dha. pa. 80, 145 dhammapadepi</note> ‘‘Udakaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0166" /> hi nayanti nettikā, usukārā namayanti <note>damayanti (ka.)</note> tejanaṃ;
```

```
Dāruṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0265" /> namayanti tacchakā, attānaṃ damayanti subbatā’’ti.
```

… Kulo <note>kuṇḍalo (sī.), kuḷo (syā. ka.)</note> thero….

#### 10. Ajitattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Maraṇe me bhayaṃ natthi, nikanti natthi jīvite;
```

```
Sandehaṃ nikkhipissāmi, **sampajāno** paṭissato’’ti <note>patissatoti (sī. syā.)</note>.
```

… Ajito thero ….

Vaggo dutiyo niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Cūḷavaccho mahāvaccho, vanavaccho ca sīvako;
```

```
Kuṇḍadhāno ca belaṭṭhi, dāsako ca tatopari;
```

```
Siṅgālapitiko thero, kulo ca ajito dasāti.
```

#### 3. Tatiyavaggo

#### 1. Nigrodhattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Nāhaṃ bhayassa bhāyāmi, satthā no amatassa kovido;
```

```
Yattha bhayaṃ nāvatiṭṭhati, tena maggena vajanti bhikkhavo’’ti.
```

… Nigrodho thero….

#### 2. Cittakattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Nīlā <pb ed="M" n="0.0225" /> sugīvā sikhino, morā kārambhiyaṃ <note>kāraṃviyaṃ (sī.), kāraviyaṃ (syā.)</note> abhinadanti;
```

```
Te sītavātakīḷitā <note>sītavātakadditakalitā (sī.), sītavātakalitā (syā.)</note>, suttaṃ jhāyaṃ <note>jhānaṃ (syā.), jhāyiṃ (?)</note> nibodhentī’’ti.
```

… Cittako thero….

#### 3. Gosālattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0266" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0167" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0005" /> kho veḷugumbasmiṃ, bhutvāna madhupāyasaṃ;
```

```
Padakkhiṇaṃ sammasanto, **khandhānaṃ udayabbayaṃ;**
```

```
Sānuṃ paṭigamissāmi, vivekamanubrūhaya’’nti.
```

… Gosālo thero….

#### 4. Sugandhattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Anuvassiko pabbajito, **passa dhammasudhammataṃ;**
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsana’’nti.
```

… Sugandho thero….

#### 5. Nandiyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Obhāsajātaṃ phalagaṃ, cittaṃ yassa abhiṇhaso;
```

```
Tādisaṃ bhikkhumāsajja, kaṇha dukkhaṃ nigacchasī’’ti.
```

… Nandiyo thero….

#### 6. Abhayattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Sutvā subhāsitaṃ vācaṃ, buddhassādiccabandhuno;
```

```
Paccabyadhiṃ hi nipuṇaṃ, vālaggaṃ usunā yathā’’ti.
```

… Abhayo thero….

#### 7. Lomasakaṅgiyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Dabbaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0226" /> kusaṃ poṭakilaṃ, usīraṃ muñjapabbajaṃ;
```

```
Urasā panudissāmi, vivekamanubrūhaya’’nti.
```

… Lomasakaṅgiyo thero….

#### 8. Jambugāmikaputtattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Kacci <pb ed="V" n="0.0168" /> no vatthapasuto, kacci no bhūsanārato;
```

```
Kacci sīlamayaṃ gandhaṃ, kiṃ tvaṃ vāyasi <note>kacci sīlamayaṃ gandhaṃ, tvaṃ vāsi (syā.)</note> netarā pajā’’ti.
```

… Jambugāmikaputto thero….

#### 9. Hāritattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Samunnamayamattānaṃ, usukārova tejanaṃ;
```

```
Cittaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0267" /> ujuṃ karitvāna, avijjaṃ bhinda hāritā’’ti.
```

… Hārito thero….

#### 10. Uttiyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Ābādhe me samuppanne, sati me udapajjatha;
```

```
Ābādho me samuppanno, kālo me nappamajjitu’’nti.
```

… Uttiyo thero….

Vaggo tatiyo niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Nigrodho cittako thero, gosālathero sugandho;
```

```
Nandiyo abhayo thero, thero lomasakaṅgiyo;
```

```
Jambugāmikaputto ca, hārito uttiyo isīti.
```

#### 4. Catutthavaggo

#### 1. Gahvaratīriyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Phuṭṭho <pb ed="M" n="0.0227" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0006" /> ḍaṃsehi makasehi, araññasmiṃ brahāvane;
```

```
Nāgo saṃgāmasīseva, **sato tatrādhivāsaye’’ti**.
```

… Gahvaratīriyo thero….

#### 2. Suppiyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Ajaraṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0169" /> jīramānena, tappamānena nibbutiṃ;
```

```
Nimiyaṃ <note>nimmissaṃ (sī.), nirāmisaṃ (syā.), nimineyyaṃ (?)</note> paramaṃ santiṃ, yogakkhemaṃ anuttara’’nti.
```

… Suppiyo thero….

#### 3. Sopākattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāpi <pb ed="T" n="0.0268" /> ekaputtasmiṃ, piyasmiṃ kusalī siyā;
```

```
Evaṃ sabbesu pāṇesu, sabbattha kusalo siyā’’ti.
```

… Sopāko thero….

#### 4. Posiyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Anāsannavarā etā, niccameva vijānatā;
```

```
Gāmā araññamāgamma, tato gehaṃ upāvisi <note>upāvisiṃ (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Tato uṭṭhāya pakkāmi, anāmantetvā <note>anāmantiya (sī.)</note> posiyo’’ti.
```

… Posiyo thero….

#### 5. Sāmaññakānittheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Sukhaṃ sukhattho labhate tadācaraṃ, kittiñca pappoti yasassa vaḍḍhati;
```

```
Yo ariyamaṭṭhaṅgikamañjasaṃ ujuṃ, bhāveti maggaṃ amatassa pattiyā’’ti.
```

… Sāmaññakānitthero….

#### 6. Kumāputtattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Sādhu <pb ed="M" n="0.0228" /> sutaṃ sādhu caritakaṃ, sādhu sadā aniketavihāro;
```

```
Atthapucchanaṃ padakkhiṇakammaṃ, etaṃ sāmaññamakiñcanassā’’ti.
```

… Kumāputto thero….

#### 7. Kumāputtasahāyakattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Nānājanapadaṃ yanti, vicarantā asaññatā;
```

```
Samādhiñca virādhenti, kiṃsu raṭṭhacariyā karissati;
```

```
Tasmā vineyya sārambhaṃ, jhāyeyya apurakkhato’’ti.
```

… Kumāputtattherassa sahāyako thero….

#### 8. Gavampatittheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Yo <pb ed="T" n="0.0269" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0170" /> iddhiyā sarabhuṃ aṭṭhapesi, so gavampati asito anejo;
```

```
Taṃ sabbasaṅgātigataṃ mahāmuniṃ, devā namassanti bhavassa pāragu’’nti.
```

… Gavampatitthero….

#### 9. Tissattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
<note>saṃ. ni. 1.21, 97</note>‘‘Sattiyā viya omaṭṭho, ḍayhamānova <note>ḍayhamāneva (sabbattha)</note> matthake;
```

```
Kāmarāgappahānāya, sato bhikkhu paribbaje’’ti.
```

… Tisso thero….

#### 10. Vaḍḍhamānattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Sattiyā <pb ed="P" n="0.0007" /> viya omaṭṭho, ḍayhamānova matthake;
```

```
Bhavarāgappahānāya, sato bhikkhu paribbaje’’ti.
```

… Vaḍḍhamāno thero….

Vaggo catuttho niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Gahvaratīriyo <pb ed="M" n="0.0229" /> suppiyo, sopāko ceva posiyo;
```

```
Sāmaññakāni kumāputto, kumāputtasahāyako;
```

```
Gavampati tissatthero, vaḍḍhamāno mahāyasoti.
```

#### 5. Pañcamavaggo

#### 1. Sirivaḍḍhattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘Vivaramanupatanti <pb ed="T" n="0.0270" /> vijjutā, vebhārassa ca paṇḍavassa ca;
```

```
Nagavivaragato ca jhāyati, putto appaṭimassa tādino’’ti.
```

… Sirivaḍḍho thero….

#### 2. Khadiravaniyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘Cāle <pb ed="V" n="0.0171" /> upacāle sīsūpacāle ( ) <note>(cālā upacālā, sīsūpacālā) (ka.)</note> patissatā <note>paṭissatikā (syā. ka.)</note> nu kho viharatha;
```

```
Āgato vo vālaṃ viya vedhī’’ti.
```

… Khadiravaniyo thero….

#### 3. Sumaṅgalattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘Sumuttiko sumuttiko sāhu, sumuttikomhi tīhi khujjakehi;
```

```
Asitāsu mayā naṅgalāsu, mayā khuddakuddālāsu mayā.
```

```
Yadipi idhameva idhameva, atha vāpi alameva alameva;
```

```
Jhāya sumaṅgala jhāya sumaṅgala, appamatto vihara sumaṅgalā’’ti.
```

… Sumaṅgalo thero….

#### 4. Sānuttheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
<note>saṃ. ni. 1.239</note> ‘‘Mataṃ vā amma rodanti, yo vā jīvaṃ na dissati;
```

```
Jīvantaṃ maṃ amma passantī, kasmā maṃ amma rodasī’’ti.
```

… Sānutthero….

#### 5. Ramaṇīyavihārittheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāpi <pb ed="M" n="0.0230" /> bhaddo ājañño, khalitvā patitiṭṭhati;
```

```
Evaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0271" /> dassanasampannaṃ, sammāsambuddhasāvaka’’nti.
```

… Ramaṇīyavihāritthero….

#### 6. Samiddhittheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Saddhāyāhaṃ pabbajito, agārasmānagāriyaṃ;
```

```
**Sati paññā** ca me vuḍḍhā, cittañca susamāhitaṃ;
```

```
Kāmaṃ karassu rūpāni, neva maṃ byādhayissasī’’ti <note>bādhayissasīti (sī.), byāthayissasīti (?)</note>.
```

… Samiddhitthero….

#### 7. Ujjayattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Namo <pb ed="V" n="0.0172" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0008" /> te buddha vīratthu, vippamuttosi sabbadhi;
```

```
Tuyhāpadāne viharaṃ, viharāmi anāsavo’’ti.
```

… Ujjayo thero….

#### 8. Sañjayattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Yato ahaṃ pabbajito, agārasmānagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Nābhijānāmi saṅkappaṃ, anariyaṃ dosasaṃhita’’nti.
```

… Sañjayo thero….

#### 9. Rāmaṇeyyakattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Cihacihābhinadite <note>vihavihābhinadite (sī. syā.)</note>, sippikābhirutehi ca;
```

```
Na me taṃ phandati cittaṃ, ekattanirataṃ hi me’’ti.
```

… Rāmaṇeyyako thero….

#### 10. Vimalattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Dharaṇī <pb ed="M" n="0.0231" /> ca siñcati vāti, māluto vijjutā carati nabhe;
```

```
Upasamanti vitakkā, cittaṃ susamāhitaṃ mamā’’ti.
```

… Vimalo thero….

Vaggo pañcamo niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Sirīvaḍḍho revato thero, sumaṅgalo sānusavhayo<pb ed="T" n="0.0272" />;
```

```
Ramaṇīyavihārī ca, samiddhiujjayasañjayā;
```

```
Rāmaṇeyyo ca so thero, vimalo ca raṇañjahoti.
```

#### 6. Chaṭṭhavaggo

#### 1. Godhikattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Vassati <pb ed="V" n="0.0173" /> devo yathā sugītaṃ, channā me kuṭikā sukhā nivātā;
```

```
Cittaṃ susamāhitañca mayhaṃ, atha ce patthayasi pavassa devā’’ti.
```

… Godhiko thero….

#### 2. Subāhuttheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Vassati devo yathā sugītaṃ, channā me kuṭikā sukhā nivātā;
```

```
**Cittaṃ susamāhitañca kāye,** atha ce patthayasi pavassa devā’’ti.
```

… Subāhutthero….

#### 3. Valliyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Vassati devo yathā sugītaṃ, channā me kuṭikā sukhā nivātā;
```

```
Tassaṃ viharāmi appamatto, atha ce patthayasi pavassa devā’’ti.
```

… Valliyo thero….

#### 4. Uttiyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Vassati <pb ed="M" n="0.0232" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0009" /> devo yathā sugītaṃ, channā me kuṭikā sukhā nivātā;
```

```
Tassaṃ viharāmi adutiyo, atha ce patthayasi pavassa devā’’ti.
```

… Uttiyo thero….

#### 5. Añjanavaniyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Āsandiṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0273" /> kuṭikaṃ katvā, ogayha añjanaṃ vanaṃ;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsana’’nti.
```

… Añjanavaniyo thero….

#### 6. Kuṭivihārittheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Ko <pb ed="V" n="0.0174" /> kuṭikāyaṃ bhikkhu kuṭikāyaṃ, vītarāgo susamāhitacitto;
```

```
Evaṃ jānāhi āvuso, amoghā te kuṭikā katā’’ti.
```

… Kuṭivihāritthero….

#### 7. Dutiyakuṭivihārittheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Ayamāhu purāṇiyā kuṭi, aññaṃ patthayase navaṃ kuṭiṃ;
```

```
Āsaṃ kuṭiyā virājaya, dukkhā bhikkhu puna navā kuṭī’’ti.
```

… Dutiyakuṭivihāritthero….

#### 8. Ramaṇīyakuṭikattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Ramaṇīyā me kuṭikā, saddhādeyyā manoramā;
```

```
Na me attho kumārīhi, yesaṃ attho tahiṃ gacchatha nāriyo’’ti.
```

… Ramaṇīyakuṭiko thero….

#### 9. Kosalavihārittheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Saddhāyāhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0233" /> pabbajito, araññe me kuṭikā katā;
```

```
Appamatto ca ātāpī, sampajāno patissato’’ti <note>paṭissatoti (ka.)</note>.
```

… Kosalavihāritthero….

#### 10. Sīvalittheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Te me ijjhiṃsu saṅkappā, yadattho pāvisiṃ kuṭiṃ;
```

```
Vijjāvimuttiṃ paccesaṃ, mānānusayamujjaha’’nti.
```

… Sīvalitthero….

Vaggo chaṭṭho niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Godhiko <pb ed="T" n="0.0274" /> ca subāhu ca, valliyo uttiyo isi;
```

```
Añjanavaniyo thero, duve kuṭivihārino;
```

```
Ramaṇīyakuṭiko ca, kosalavhayasīvalīti.
```

#### 7. Sattamavaggo

#### 1. Vappattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘Passati <pb ed="V" n="0.0175" /> passo passantaṃ, apassantañca passati;
```

```
Apassanto apassantaṃ, passantañca na passatī’’ti.
```

… Vappo thero….

#### 2. Vajjiputtattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘Ekakā <pb ed="P" n="0.0010" /> mayaṃ araññe viharāma, apaviddhaṃva vanasmiṃ dārukaṃ;
```

```
Tassa me bahukā pihayanti, nerayikā viya saggagāmina’’nti.
```

… Vajjiputto thero….

#### 3. Pakkhattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘Cutā <pb ed="M" n="0.0234" /> patanti patitā, giddhā ca punarāgatā;
```

```
Kataṃ kiccaṃ rataṃ rammaṃ, sukhenanvāgataṃ sukha’’nti.
```

… Pakkho thero….

#### 4. Vimalakoṇḍaññattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘Dumavhayāya uppanno, jāto paṇḍaraketunā;
```

```
Ketuhā <pb ed="T" n="0.0275" /> ketunāyeva, mahāketuṃ padhaṃsayī’’ti.
```

… Vimalakoṇḍañño thero….

#### 5. Ukkhepakatavacchattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Ukkhepakatavacchassa, saṅkalitaṃ bahūhi vassehi;
```

```
Taṃ bhāsati gahaṭṭhānaṃ, sunisinno uḷārapāmojjo’’ti.
```

… Ukkhepakatavaccho thero….

#### 6. Meghiyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Anusāsi <pb ed="V" n="0.0176" /> mahāvīro, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
```

```
Tassāhaṃ dhammaṃ sutvāna, vihāsiṃ santike sato;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsana’’nti.
```

… Meghiyo thero….

#### 7. Ekadhammasavanīyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Vikkhīṇo jātisaṃsāro, natthi dāni punabbhavo’’ti.
```

… Ekadhammasavanīyo thero….

#### 8. Ekudāniyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
<note>udā. 37; pāci. 153</note> ‘‘Adhicetaso appamajjato, munino monapathesu sikkhato;
```

```
Sokā na bhavanti tādino, upasantassa sadā satīmato’’ti.
```

… Ekudāniyo thero….

#### 9. Channattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Sutvāna <pb ed="M" n="0.0235" /> dhammaṃ mahato mahārasaṃ, sabbaññutaññāṇavarena desitaṃ;
```

```
Maggaṃ papajjiṃ <note>papajjaṃ (ka.)</note> amatassa pattiyā, so yogakkhemassa pathassa kovido’’ti.
```

… Channo thero….

#### 10. Puṇṇattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Sīlameva <pb ed="T" n="0.0276" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0011" /> idha aggaṃ, paññavā pana uttamo;
```

```
Manussesu ca devesu, sīlapaññāṇato jaya’’nti.
```

… Puṇṇo thero….

Vaggo sattamo niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0177" /> –

```
Vappo ca vajjiputto ca, pakkho vimalakoṇḍañño;
```

```
Ukkhepakatavaccho ca, meghiyo ekadhammiko;
```

```
Ekudāniyachannā ca, puṇṇatthero mahabbaloti.
```

#### 8. Aṭṭhamavaggo

#### 1. Vacchapālattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Susukhumanipuṇatthadassinā, matikusalena nivātavuttinā;
```

```
Saṃsevitavuddhasīlinā <note>saṃsevitabuddhasīlinā (ka.)</note>, nibbānaṃ na hi tena dullabha’’nti.
```

… Vacchapālo thero….

#### 2. Ātumattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Yathā <pb ed="M" n="0.0236" /> kaḷīro susu vaḍḍhitaggo, dunnikkhamo hoti pasākhajāto;
```

```
Evaṃ ahaṃ bhariyāyānitāya, anumaññaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0277" /> maṃ pabbajitomhi dānī’’ti.
```

… Ātumo thero….

#### 3. Māṇavattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘Jiṇṇañca disvā dukhitañca byādhitaṃ, matañca disvā gatamāyusaṅkhayaṃ;
```

```
Tato ahaṃ nikkhamitūna pabbajiṃ, pahāya kāmāni manoramānī’’ti.
```

… Māṇavo thero….

#### 4. Suyāmanattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘Kāmacchando ca byāpādo, thinamiddhañca <note>thīnamiddhañca (sī. syā.)</note> bhikkhuno;
```

```
Uddhaccaṃ vicikicchā ca, sabbasova na vijjatī’’ti.
```

… Suyāmano thero….

#### 5. Susāradattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
‘‘Sādhu suvihitāna dassanaṃ, kaṅkhā chijjati buddhi vaḍḍhati;
```

```
Bālampi karonti paṇḍitaṃ, tasmā sādhu sataṃ samāgamo’’ti.
```

… Susārado thero….

#### 6. Piyañjahattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
‘‘Uppatantesu <pb ed="V" n="0.0178" /> nipate, nipatantesu uppate;
```

```
Vase avasamānesu, ramamānesu no rame’’ti.
```

… Piyañjaho thero….

#### 7. Hatthārohaputtattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
‘‘Idaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0237" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0012" /> pure cittamacāri cārikaṃ, yenicchakaṃ yatthakāmaṃ yathāsukhaṃ;
```

```
Tadajjahaṃ niggahessāmi yoniso, hatthippabhinnaṃ viya aṅkusaggaho’’ti.
```

… Hatthārohaputto thero….

#### 8. Meṇḍasirattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
‘‘Anekajātisaṃsāraṃ<pb ed="T" n="0.0278" />, sandhāvissaṃ anibbisaṃ;
```

```
Tassa me dukkhajātassa, dukkhakkhandho aparaddho’’ti.
```

… Meṇḍasiro thero….

#### 9. Rakkhitattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbo rāgo pahīno me, sabbo doso samūhato;
```

```
Sabbo me vigato moho, sītibhūtosmi nibbuto’’ti.
```

… Rakkhito thero….

#### 10. Uggattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0238" /> mayā pakataṃ kammaṃ, appaṃ vā yadi vā bahuṃ;
```

```
Sabbametaṃ parikkhīṇaṃ, natthi dāni punabbhavo’’ti.
```

… Uggo thero….

Vaggo aṭṭhamo niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Vacchapālo ca yo thero, ātumo māṇavo isi;
```

```
Suyāmano susārado, thero yo ca piyañjaho;
```

```
Ārohaputto meṇḍasiro, rakkhito uggasavhayoti.
```

#### 9. Navamavaggo

#### 1. Samitiguttattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0179" /> mayā pakataṃ pāpaṃ, pubbe aññāsu jātisu;
```

```
Idheva taṃ vedanīyaṃ, vatthu aññaṃ na vijjatī’’ti.
```

… Samitigutto thero….

#### 2. Kassapattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
‘‘Yena <pb ed="T" n="0.0279" /> yena subhikkhāni, sivāni abhayāni ca;
```

```
Tena puttaka gacchassu, mā sokāpahato bhavā’’ti.
```

… Kassapo thero….

#### 3. Sīhattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
‘‘Sīhappamatto vihara, rattindivamatandito;
```

```
Bhāvehi kusalaṃ dhammaṃ, jaha sīghaṃ samussaya’’nti.
```

… Sīho thero….

#### 4. Nītattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbarattiṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0013" /> supitvāna, divā saṅgaṇike rato;
```

```
Kudāssu nāma dummedho, dukkhassantaṃ karissatī’’ti.
```

… Nīto thero….

#### 5. Sunāgattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
‘‘Cittanimittassa kovido, pavivekarasaṃ vijāniya;
```

```
Jhāyaṃ nipako patissato, adhigaccheyya sukhaṃ nirāmisa’’nti.
```

… Sunāgo thero….

#### 6. Nāgitattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
‘‘Ito <pb ed="V" n="0.0180" /> bahiddhā puthu aññavādinaṃ, maggo na nibbānagamo yathā ayaṃ;
```

```
Itissu saṅghaṃ bhagavānusāsati, satthā sayaṃ pāṇitaleva dassaya’’nti.
```

… Nāgito thero….

#### 7. Paviṭṭhattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
‘‘Khandhā <pb ed="M" n="0.0239" /> diṭṭhā yathābhūtaṃ, bhavā sabbe padālitā;
```

```
Vikkhīṇo jātisaṃsāro, natthi dāni punabbhavo’’ti.
```

… Paviṭṭho thero….

#### 8. Ajjunattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
‘‘Asakkhiṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0280" /> vata attānaṃ, uddhātuṃ udakā thalaṃ;
```

```
Vuyhamāno mahogheva, saccāni paṭivijjhaha’’nti.
```

… Ajjuno thero….

#### 9. (Paṭhama)-devasabhattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
‘‘Uttiṇṇā paṅkapalipā, pātālā parivajjitā;
```

```
Mutto oghā ca ganthā ca, sabbe mānā visaṃhatā’’ti.
```

… Devasabho thero….

#### 10. Sāmidattattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
‘‘Pañcakkhandhā pariññātā, tiṭṭhanti chinnamūlakā;
```

```
Vikkhīṇo jātisaṃsāro, natthi dāni punabbhavo’’ti.
```

… Sāmidatto thero….

Vaggo navamo niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Thero samitigutto ca, kassapo sīhasavhayo;
```

```
Nīto sunāgo nāgito, paviṭṭho ajjuno isi;
```

```
Devasabho ca yo thero, sāmidatto mahabbaloti.
```

#### 10. Dasamavaggo

#### 1. Paripuṇṇakattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
‘‘Na <pb ed="V" n="0.0181" /> tathā mataṃ satarasaṃ, sudhannaṃ yaṃ mayajja paribhuttaṃ;
```

```
Aparimitadassinā gotamena, buddhena desito dhammo’’ti.
```

… Paripuṇṇako thero….

#### 2. Vijayattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
‘‘Yassāsavā <pb ed="T" n="0.0281" /><pb ed="M" n="0.0240" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0014" /> parikkhīṇā, āhāre ca anissito;
```

```
Suññatā animitto ca, vimokkho yassa gocaro;
```

```
Ākāseva sakuntānaṃ, padaṃ tassa durannaya’’nti.
```

… Vijayo thero….

#### 3. Erakattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
‘‘Dukkhā kāmā eraka, na sukhā kāmā eraka;
```

```
Yo kāme kāmayati, dukkhaṃ so kāmayati eraka;
```

```
Yo kāme na kāmayati, dukkhaṃ so na kāmayati erakā’’ti.
```

… Erako thero….

#### 4. Mettajittheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
‘‘Namo hi tassa bhagavato, sakyaputtassa sirīmato;
```

```
Tenāyaṃ aggappattena, aggadhammo <note>aggo dhammo (sī.)</note> sudesito’’ti.
```

… Mettaji thero….

#### 5. Cakkhupālattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
‘‘Andhohaṃ hatanettosmi, kantāraddhānapakkhando <note>pakkhanno (sī.), pakkanto (syā. sī. aṭṭha.)</note>;
```

```
Sayamānopi gacchissaṃ, na sahāyena pāpenā’’ti.
```

… Cakkhupālo thero….

#### 6. Khaṇḍasumanattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
‘‘Ekapupphaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0182" /> cajitvāna, asīti <note>asītiṃ (sī.)</note> vassakoṭiyo;
```

```
Saggesu paricāretvā, sesakenamhi nibbuto’’ti.
```

… Khaṇḍasumano thero….

#### 7. Tissattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
‘‘Hitvā satapalaṃ kaṃsaṃ, sovaṇṇaṃ satarājikaṃ;
```

```
Aggahiṃ mattikāpattaṃ, idaṃ dutiyābhisecana’’nti.
```

… Tisso thero….

#### 8. Abhayattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
‘‘Rūpaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0282" /><pb ed="M" n="0.0241" /> disvā sati muṭṭhā, piyaṃ nimittaṃ manasikaroto;
```

```
Sārattacitto vedeti, tañca ajjhosa tiṭṭhati;
```

```
Tassa vaḍḍhanti āsavā, bhavamūlopagāmino’’ti <note>bhavamūlā bhavagāminoti (sī. ka.)</note>.
```

… Abhayo thero….

#### 9. Uttiyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
‘‘Saddaṃ sutvā sati muṭṭhā, piyaṃ nimittaṃ manasikaroto;
```

```
Sārattacitto vedeti, tañca ajjhosa tiṭṭhati;
```

```
Tassa vaḍḍhanti āsavā, saṃsāraṃ upagāmino’’ti.
```

… Uttiyo thero….

#### 10. (Dutiya)-devasabhattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
‘‘Sammappadhānasampanno, satipaṭṭhānagocaro;
```

```
Vimuttikusumasañchanno, parinibbissatyanāsavo’’ti.
```

… Devasabho thero….

Vaggo dasamo niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Paripuṇṇako ca vijayo, erako mettajī muni;
```

```
Cakkhupālo khaṇḍasumano, tisso ca abhayo tathā;
```

```
Uttiyo ca mahāpañño, thero devasabhopi cāti.
```

#### 11. Ekādasamavaggo

#### 1. Belaṭṭhānikattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
‘‘Hitvā <pb ed="V" n="0.0183" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0015" /> gihittaṃ anavositatto, mukhanaṅgalī odariko kusīto;
```

```
Mahāvarāhova <pb ed="T" n="0.0283" /> nivāpapuṭṭho, punappunaṃ gabbhamupeti mando’’ti.
```

… Belaṭṭhāniko thero….

#### 2. Setucchattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
‘‘Mānena <pb ed="M" n="0.0242" /> vañcitāse, saṅkhāresu saṃkilissamānāse;
```

```
Lābhālābhena mathitā, samādhiṃ nādhigacchantī’’ti.
```

… Setuccho thero….

#### 3. Bandhurattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
‘‘Nāhaṃ etena atthiko, sukhito dhammarasena tappito;
```

```
Pitvā <note>pītvāna (sī. syā.)</note> rasaggamuttamaṃ, na ca kāhāmi visena santhava’’nti.
```

… Bandhuro <note>bandhano (ka.)</note> thero….

#### 4. Khitakattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
‘‘Lahuko vata me kāyo, phuṭṭho ca pītisukhena vipulena;
```

```
Tūlamiva eritaṃ mālutena, pilavatīva me kāyo’’ti.
```

… Khitako thero….

#### 5. Malitavambhattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
‘‘Ukkaṇṭhitopi na vase, ramamānopi pakkame;
```

```
Na tvevānatthasaṃhitaṃ, vase vāsaṃ vicakkhaṇo’’ti.
```

… Malitavambho thero….

#### 6. Suhemantattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
‘‘Sataliṅgassa <pb ed="V" n="0.0184" /> atthassa, satalakkhaṇadhārino;
```

```
Ekaṅgadassī dummedho, satadassī ca paṇḍito’’ti.
```

… Suhemanto thero….

#### 7. Dhammasavattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbajiṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0243" /> tulayitvāna, agārasmānagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Tisso <pb ed="T" n="0.0284" /> vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsana’’nti.
```

… Dhammasavo thero….

#### 8. Dhammasavapituttheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
‘‘Sa vīsavassasatiko, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsana’’nti.
```

… Dhammasavapitu thero….

#### 9. Saṅgharakkhitattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
‘‘Na <pb ed="P" n="0.0016" /> nūnāyaṃ paramahitānukampino, rahogato anuvigaṇeti sāsanaṃ;
```

```
Tathāhayaṃ viharati pākatindriyo, migī yathā taruṇajātikā vane’’ti.
```

… Saṅgharakkhito thero….

#### 10. Usabhattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
‘‘Nagā nagaggesu susaṃvirūḷhā, udaggameghena navena sittā;
```

```
Vivekakāmassa araññasaññino, janeti bhiyyo usabhassa kalyata’’nti.
```

… Usabho thero….

Vaggo ekādasamo niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Belaṭṭhāniko setuccho, bandhuro khitako isi;
```

```
Malitavambho suhemanto, dhammasavo dhammasavapitā;
```

```
Saṅgharakkhitatthero <pb ed="T" n="0.0285" /> ca, usabho ca mahāmunīti.
```

#### 12. Dvādasamavaggo

#### 1. Jentattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
‘‘Duppabbajjaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0244" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0185" /> ve duradhivāsā gehā, dhammo gambhīro duradhigamā bhogā;
```

```
Kicchā vutti no itarītareneva, yuttaṃ cintetuṃ satatamaniccata’’nti.
```

… Jento thero….

#### 2. Vacchagottattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
‘‘Tevijjohaṃ mahājhāyī, cetosamathakovido;
```

```
Sadattho me anuppatto, kataṃ buddhassa sāsana’’nti.
```

… Vacchagotto thero….

#### 3. Vanavacchattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
‘‘Acchodikā puthusilā,gonaṅgulamigāyutā;
```

```
Ambusevālasañchannā, te selā ramayanti ma’’nti.
```

… Vanavaccho thero….

#### 4. Adhimuttattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
‘‘Kāyaduṭṭhullagaruno, hiyyamānamhi <note>hīyamānamhi (sī.)</note> jīvite;
```

```
Sarīrasukhagiddhassa, kuto samaṇasādhutā’’ti.
```

… Adhimutto thero….

#### 5. Mahānāmattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
‘‘Esāvahiyyase pabbatena, bahukuṭajasallakikena <note>sallakitena (sī.), sallarikena (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Nesādakena <pb ed="T" n="0.0286" /> girinā, yasassinā paricchadenā’’ti.
```

… Mahānāmo thero….

#### 6. Pārāpariyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
‘‘Chaphassāyatane <pb ed="M" n="0.0245" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0186" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0017" /> hitvā, guttadvāro susaṃvuto;
```

```
Aghamūlaṃ vamitvāna, patto me āsavakkhayo’’ti.
```

… Pārāpariyo <note>pārāsariyo (sī.), pāraṃpariyo (ka.)</note> thero ….

#### 7. Yasattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
‘‘Suvilitto suvasano,sabbābharaṇabhūsito;
```

```
Tisso vijjā ajjhagamiṃ, kataṃ buddhassa sāsana’’nti.
```

… Yaso thero….

#### 8. Kimilattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
‘‘Abhisattova nipatati, vayo rūpaṃ aññamiva tatheva santaṃ;
```

```
Tasseva sato avippavasato, aññasseva sarāmi attāna’’nti.
```

… Kimilo <note>kimbilo (sī. syā.)</note> thero….

#### 9. Vajjiputtattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
‘‘Rukkhamūlagahanaṃ pasakkiya, nibbānaṃ hadayasmiṃ opiya;
```

```
Jhāya gotama mā ca pamādo, kiṃ te biḷibiḷikā karissatī’’ti.
```

… Vajjiputto thero….

#### 10. Isidattattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
‘‘Pañcakkhandhā pariññātā, tiṭṭhanti chinnamūlakā;
```

```
Dukkhakkhayo <pb ed="T" n="0.0287" /> anuppatto,patto me āsavakkhayo’’ti.
```

… Isidatto thero….

Vaggo dvādasamo niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0187" /> –

```
Jento <pb ed="M" n="0.0246" /> ca vacchagotto ca, vaccho ca vanasavhayo;
```

```
Adhimutto mahānāmo, pārāpariyo yasopi ca;
```

```
Kimilo vajjiputto ca, isidatto mahāyasoti.
```

<trailer rend="centre">Ekakanipāto niṭṭhito.</trailer>

Tatruddānaṃ –

```
Vīsuttarasataṃ therā, katakiccā anāsavā;
```

```
Ekakeva nipātamhi, susaṅgītā mahesibhīti.
```

### 2. Dukanipāto

#### 1. Paṭhamavaggo

#### 1. Uttarattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
‘‘Natthi <pb ed="M" n="0.0247" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0188" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0018" /> koci bhavo nicco, saṅkhārā vāpi sassatā;
```

```
Uppajjanti ca te khandhā, cavanti aparāparaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
‘‘Etamādīnaṃ ñatvā, bhavenamhi anatthiko;
```

```
Nissaṭo sabbakāmehi, patto me āsavakkhayo’’ti.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā uttaro thero gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

#### 2. Piṇḍolabhāradvājattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§123.</p>

```
‘‘Nayidaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0288" /> anayena jīvitaṃ, nāhāro hadayassa santiko;
```

```
Āhāraṭṭhitiko samussayo, iti disvāna carāmi esanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
‘‘Paṅkoti hi naṃ pavedayuṃ, yāyaṃ vandanapūjanā kulesu;
```

```
Sukhumaṃ sallaṃ durubbahaṃ, sakkāro kāpurisena dujjaho’’ti.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā piṇḍolabhāradvājo thero gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

#### 3. Valliyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
‘‘Makkaṭo pañcadvārāyaṃ, kuṭikāyaṃ pasakkiya;
```

```
Dvārena anupariyeti, ghaṭṭayanto muhuṃ muhuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṭṭha makkaṭa mā dhāvi, na hi te taṃ yathā pure;
```

```
Niggahītosi paññāya, neva dūraṃ gamissatī’’ti.
```

… Valliyo thero….

#### 4. Gaṅgātīriyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṇṇaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0248" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0189" /> me tālapattānaṃ, gaṅgātīre kuṭī katā;
```

```
Chavasittova me patto, paṃsukūlañca cīvaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
‘‘Dvinnaṃ antaravassānaṃ, ekā vācā me bhāsitā;
```

```
Tatiye antaravassamhi, tamokhandho <note>tamokkhandho (sī. syā.)</note> padālito’’ti.
```

… Gaṅgātīriyo thero….

#### 5. Ajinattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
‘‘Api ce hoti tevijjo, maccuhāyī anāsavo;
```

```
Appaññātoti naṃ bālā, avajānanti ajānatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
‘‘Yo <pb ed="P" n="0.0019" /> ca kho annapānassa, lābhī hotīdha puggalo;
```

```
Pāpadhammopi ce hoti, so nesaṃ hoti sakkato’’ti.
```

… Ajino thero….

#### 6. Meḷajinattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§131.</p>

```
‘‘Yadāhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0289" /> dhammamassosiṃ, bhāsamānassa satthuno;
```

```
Na kaṅkhamabhijānāmi, sabbaññūaparājite.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§132.</p>

```
‘‘Satthavāhe mahāvīre, sārathīnaṃ varuttame;
```

```
Magge paṭipadāyaṃ vā, kaṅkhā mayhaṃ na vijjatī’’ti.
```

… Meḷajino thero….

#### 7. Rādhattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§133.</p>

```
<note>dha. pa. 13 dhammapade</note> ‘‘Yathā agāraṃ ducchannaṃ, vuṭṭhī samativijjhati;
```

```
Evaṃ abhāvitaṃ cittaṃ, rāgo samativijjhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§134.</p>

```
<note>dha. pa. 14 dhammapade</note> ‘‘Yathā agāraṃ succhannaṃ, vuḍḍhī na samativijjhati;
```

```
Evaṃ subhāvitaṃ cittaṃ, rāgo na samativijjhatī’’ti.
```

… Rādho thero….

#### 8. Surādhattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§135.</p>

```
‘‘Khīṇā <pb ed="M" n="0.0249" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0190" /> hi mayhaṃ jāti, vusitaṃ jinasāsanaṃ;
```

```
Pahīno jālasaṅkhāto, bhavanetti samūhatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§136.</p>

```
‘‘Yassatthāya pabbajito, agārasmānagāriyaṃ;
```

```
So me attho anuppatto, sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo’’ti.
```

… Surādho thero….

#### 9. Gotamattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§137.</p>

```
‘‘Sukhaṃ supanti munayo, ye itthīsu na bajjhare;
```

```
Sadā ve rakkhitabbāsu, yāsu saccaṃ sudullabhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§138.</p>

```
‘‘Vadhaṃ carimha te kāma, anaṇā dāni te mayaṃ;
```

```
Gacchāma dāni nibbānaṃ, yattha gantvā na socatī’’ti.
```

… Gotamo thero….

#### 10. Vasabhattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§139.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbe <pb ed="T" n="0.0290" /> hanati attānaṃ, pacchā hanati so pare;
```

```
Suhataṃ hanti attānaṃ, vītaṃseneva pakkhimā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§140.</p>

```
‘‘Na brāhmaṇo bahivaṇṇo, anto vaṇṇo hi brāhmaṇo;
```

```
Yasmiṃ pāpāni kammāni, sa ve kaṇho sujampatī’’ti.
```

… Vasabho thero….

Vaggo paṭhamo niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Uttaro ceva piṇḍolo, valliyo tīriyo isi;
```

```
Ajino ca meḷajino, rādho surādho gotamo;
```

```
Vasabhena ime honti, dasa therā mahiddhikāti.
```

#### 2. Dutiyavaggo

#### 1. Mahācundattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§141.</p>

```
‘‘Sussūsā <pb ed="M" n="0.0250" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0191" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0020" /> sutavaddhanī, sutaṃ paññāya vaddhanaṃ;
```

```
Paññāya atthaṃ jānāti, ñāto attho sukhāvaho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§142.</p>

```
‘‘Sevetha pantāni senāsanāni, careyya saṃyojanavippamokkhaṃ;
```

```
Sace ratiṃ nādhigaccheyya tattha, saṅghe vase rakkhitatto satimā’’ti.
```

… Mahācundo thero….

#### 2. Jotidāsattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§143.</p>

```
‘‘Ye kho te veṭhamissena <note>veghamissena (sī. syā.), ve gamissena, vekhamissena (ka.)</note>, nānattena ca kammunā;
```

```
Manusse uparundhanti, pharusūpakkamā janā;
```

```
Tepi <pb ed="T" n="0.0291" /> tattheva kīranti, na hi kammaṃ panassati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§144.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ karoti naro kammaṃ, kalyāṇaṃ yadi pāpakaṃ;
```

```
Tassa tasseva dāyādo, yaṃ yaṃ kammaṃ pakubbatī’’ti.
```

… Jotidāso thero….

#### 3. Heraññakānittheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§145.</p>

```
‘‘Accayanti ahorattā, jīvitaṃ uparujjhati;
```

```
Āyu khīyati maccānaṃ, kunnadīnaṃva odakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§146.</p>

```
‘‘Atha pāpāni kammāni, karaṃ bālo na bujjhati;
```

```
Pacchāssa kaṭukaṃ hoti, vipāko hissa pāpako’’ti.
```

… Heraññakānitthero….

#### 4. Somamittattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§147.</p>

```
‘‘Parittaṃ dārumāruyha, yathā sīde mahaṇṇave;
```

```
Evaṃ kusītamāgamma, sādhujīvīpi sīdati;
```

```
Tasmā taṃ parivajjeyya, kusītaṃ hīnavīriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§148.</p>

```
‘‘Pavivittehi <pb ed="M" n="0.0251" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0192" /> ariyehi, pahitattehi jhāyibhi;
```

```
Niccaṃ āraddhavīriyehi, paṇḍitehi sahāvase’’ti.
```

… Somamitto thero….

#### 5. Sabbamittattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§149.</p>

```
‘‘Jano janamhi sambaddho <note>sambaddho (syā. ka.)</note>, janamevassito jano;
```

```
Jano janena heṭhīyati, heṭheti ca <note>bodhiyati, bādheti ca (ka.)</note> jano janaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§150.</p>

```
‘‘Ko <pb ed="P" n="0.0021" /> hi tassa janenattho, janena janitena vā;
```

```
Janaṃ ohāya gacchaṃ taṃ, heṭhayitvā <note>bādhayitvā (ka.)</note> bahuṃ jana’’nti.
```

… Sabbamitto thero….

#### 6. Mahākāḷattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§151.</p>

```
‘‘Kāḷī <pb ed="T" n="0.0292" /> itthī brahatī dhaṅkarūpā, satthiñca bhetvā aparañca satthiṃ;
```

```
Bāhañca bhetvā aparañca bāhaṃ, sīsañca bhetvā dadhithālakaṃva;
```

```
Esā nisinnā abhisandahitvā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§152.</p>

```
‘‘Yo ve avidvā upadhiṃ karoti, punappunaṃ dukkhamupeti mando;
```

```
Tasmā pajānaṃ upadhiṃ na kayirā, māhaṃ puna bhinnasiro sayissa’’nti <note>passissanti (ka.)</note>.
```

… Mahākāḷo thero….

#### 7. Tissattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§153.</p>

```
‘‘Bahū sapatte labhati, muṇḍo saṅghāṭipāruto;
```

```
Lābhī annassa pānassa, vatthassa sayanassa ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§154.</p>

```
‘‘Etamādīnavaṃ ñatvā, sakkāresu mahabbhayaṃ;
```

```
Appalābho anavassuto, sato bhikkhu paribbaje’’ti.
```

… Tisso thero….

#### 8. Kimilattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§155.</p>

```
‘‘Pācīnavaṃsadāyamhi<pb ed="M" n="0.0252" />, sakyaputtā sahāyakā;
```

```
Pahāyānappake bhoge, uñchāpattāgate ratā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§156.</p>

```
‘‘Āraddhavīriyā <pb ed="V" n="0.0193" /> pahitattā, niccaṃ daḷhaparakkamā;
```

```
Ramanti dhammaratiyā, hitvāna lokiyaṃ rati’’nti.
```

… Kimilo <note>kimbilo (sī. syā. pī.)</note> thero….

#### 9. Nandattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§157.</p>

```
‘‘Ayoniso <pb ed="T" n="0.0293" /> manasikārā, maṇḍanaṃ anuyuñjisaṃ;
```

```
Uddhato capalo cāsiṃ, kāmarāgena aṭṭito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§158.</p>

```
‘‘Upāyakusalenāhaṃ, buddhenādiccabandhunā;
```

```
Yoniso paṭipajjitvā, bhave cittaṃ udabbahi’’nti.
```

… Nando thero….

#### 10. Sirimattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§159.</p>

```
‘‘Pare ca naṃ pasaṃsanti, attā ce asamāhito;
```

```
Moghaṃ pare pasaṃsanti, attā hi asamāhito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§160.</p>

```
‘‘Pare ca naṃ garahanti, attā ce susamāhito;
```

```
Moghaṃ pare garahanti, attā hi susamāhito’’ti.
```

… Sirimā thero….

Vaggo dutiyo niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Cundo <pb ed="P" n="0.0022" /> ca jotidāso ca, thero heraññakāni ca;
```

```
Somamitto sabbamitto, kālo tisso ca kimilo <note>kimbilo (sī. syā. pī.), chandalakkhaṇānulomaṃ</note>;
```

```
Nando ca sirimā ceva, dasa therā mahiddhikāti.
```

#### 3. Tatiyavaggo

#### 1. Uttarattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§161.</p>

```
‘‘Khandhā <pb ed="M" n="0.0253" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0194" /> mayā pariññātā, taṇhā me susamūhatā;
```

```
Bhāvitā mama bojjhaṅgā, patto me āsavakkhayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§162.</p>

```
‘‘Sohaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0294" /> khandhe pariññāya, abbahitvāna <note>abbuhitvāna (ka.)</note> jāliniṃ;
```

```
Bhāvayitvāna bojjhaṅge, nibbāyissaṃ anāsavo’’ti.
```

… Uttaro thero….

#### 2. Bhaddajittheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§163.</p>

```
‘‘Panādo nāma so rājā, yassa yūpo suvaṇṇayo;
```

```
Tiriyaṃ soḷasubbedho <note>soḷasapabbedho (sī. aṭṭha.), soḷasabbāṇo (?)</note>, ubbhamāhu <note>uddhamāhu (sī.), uccamāhu (syā.)</note> sahassadhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§164.</p>

```
‘‘Sahassakaṇḍo satageṇḍu, dhajālu haritāmayo;
```

```
Anaccuṃ tattha gandhabbā, chasahassāni sattadhā’’ti.
```

… Bhaddajitthero….

#### 3. Sobhitattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§165.</p>

```
**‘‘Satimā paññavā** bhikkhu, āraddhabalavīriyo;
```

```
Pañca kappasatānāhaṃ, ekarattiṃ anussariṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§166.</p>

```
‘‘Cattāro satipaṭṭhāne, satta aṭṭha ca bhāvayaṃ;
```

```
Pañca kappasatānāhaṃ, ekarattiṃ anussari’’nti.
```

… Sobhito thero….

#### 4. Valliyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§167.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ kiccaṃ daḷhavīriyena, yaṃ kiccaṃ boddhumicchatā;
```

```
Karissaṃ nāvarajjhissaṃ <note>nāvarujjhissaṃ (ka. sī. ka.)</note>, passa vīriyaṃ parakkama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§168.</p>

```
‘‘Tvañca me maggamakkhāhi, añjasaṃ amatogadhaṃ;
```

```
Ahaṃ monena monissaṃ, gaṅgāsotova sāgara’’nti.
```

… Valliyo thero….

#### 5. Vītasokattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§169.</p>

```
‘‘Kese <pb ed="M" n="0.0254" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0195" /> me olikhissanti, kappako upasaṅkami;
```

```
Tato <pb ed="T" n="0.0295" /> ādāsamādāya, sarīraṃ paccavekkhisaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§170.</p>

```
‘‘Tuccho <pb ed="P" n="0.0023" /> kāyo adissittha, andhakāro tamo byagā;
```

```
Sabbe coḷā samucchinnā, natthi dāni punabbhavo’’ti.
```

… Vītasoko thero….

#### 6. Puṇṇamāsattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§171.</p>

```
‘‘Pañca nīvaraṇe hitvā, yogakkhemassa pattiyā;
```

```
Dhammādāsaṃ gahetvāna, ñāṇadassanamattano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§172.</p>

```
‘‘Paccavekkhiṃ imaṃ kāyaṃ, sabbaṃ santarabāhiraṃ;
```

```
Ajjhattañca bahiddhā ca, tuccho kāyo adissathā’’ti.
```

… Puṇṇamāso thero….

#### 7. Nandakattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§173.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāpi bhaddo ājañño, khalitvā patitiṭṭhati;
```

```
Bhiyyo laddāna saṃvegaṃ, adīno vahate dhuraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§174.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ dassanasampannaṃ, sammāsambuddhasāvakaṃ;
```

```
Ājānīyaṃ maṃ dhāretha, puttaṃ buddhassa orasa’’nti.
```

… Nandako thero….

#### 8. Bharatattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§175.</p>

```
‘‘Ehi nandaka gacchāma, upajjhāyassa santikaṃ;
```

```
Sīhanādaṃ nadissāma, buddhaseṭṭhassa sammukhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§176.</p>

```
‘‘Yāya no anukampāya, amhe pabbājayī muni;
```

```
So no attho anuppatto, sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo’’ti.
```

… Bharato thero….

#### 9. Bhāradvājattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§177.</p>

```
‘‘Nadanti <pb ed="T" n="0.0296" /><pb ed="M" n="0.0255" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0196" /> evaṃ sappaññā, sīhāva girigabbhare;
```

```
Vīrā vijitasaṅgāmā, jetvā māraṃ savāhaniṃ <note>savāhanaṃ (bahūsu)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§178.</p>

```
‘‘Satthā ca pariciṇṇo me, dhammo saṅgho ca pūjito;
```

```
Ahañca vitto sumano, puttaṃ disvā anāsava’’nti.
```

… Bhāradvājo thero….

#### 10. Kaṇhadinnattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§179.</p>

```
‘‘Upāsitā sappurisā, sutā dhammā abhiṇhaso;
```

```
Sutvāna paṭipajjissaṃ, añjasaṃ amatogadhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§180.</p>

```
‘‘Bhavarāgahatassa me sato, bhavarāgo puna me na vijjati;
```

```
Na cāhu na ca me bhavissati, na ca me etarahi vijjatī’’ti.
```

… Kaṇhadinno thero….

Vaggo tatiyo niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Uttaro bhaddajitthero, sobhito valliyo isi;
```

```
Vītasoko ca yo thero, puṇṇamāso ca nandako;
```

```
Bharato bhāradvājo ca, kaṇhadinno mahāmunīti.
```

#### 4. Catutthavaggo

#### 1. Migasirattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§181.</p>

```
‘‘Yato <pb ed="P" n="0.0024" /> ahaṃ pabbajito, sammāsambuddhasāsane;
```

```
Vimuccamāno uggacchiṃ, kāmadhātuṃ upaccagaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§182.</p>

```
‘‘Brahmuno <pb ed="T" n="0.0297" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0197" /> pekkhamānassa, tato cittaṃ vimucci me;
```

```
Akuppā me vimuttīti, sabbasaṃyojanakkhayā’’ti.
```

… Migasiro thero….

#### 2. Sivakattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§183.</p>

```
‘‘Aniccāni <pb ed="M" n="0.0256" /> gahakāni, tattha tattha punappunaṃ;
```

```
Gahakāraṃ <note>gahakārakaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> gavesanto, dukkhā jāti punappunaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§184.</p>

```
‘‘Gahakāraka diṭṭhosi, puna gehaṃ na kāhasi;
```

```
Sabbā te phāsukā bhaggā, thūṇikā <note>thūṇirā (pī. ka.), dhuṇirā (syā.)</note> ca vidālitā <note>padālitā (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Vimariyādikataṃ cittaṃ, idheva vidhamissatī’’ti.
```

… Sivako <note>sīvako (sī.)</note> thero….

#### 3. Upavāṇattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§185.</p>

```
‘‘Arahaṃ sugato loke, vātehābādhito <note>… bādhito (ka.)</note> muni;
```

```
Sace uṇhodakaṃ atthi, munino dehi brāhmaṇa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§186.</p>

```
‘‘Pūjito pūjaneyyānaṃ <note>pūjanīyānaṃ (sī.)</note>, sakkareyyāna sakkato;
```

```
Apacitopaceyyānaṃ <note>apacanīyānaṃ (sī.), apacineyyānaṃ (syā.)</note>, tassa icchāmi hātave’’ti.
```

… Upavāṇo thero….

#### 4. Isidinnattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§187.</p>

```
‘‘Diṭṭhā mayā dhammadharā upāsakā, kāmā aniccā iti bhāsamānā;
```

```
Sārattarattā maṇikuṇḍalesu, puttesu dāresu ca te apekkhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§188.</p>

```
‘‘Addhā na jānanti yatodha dhammaṃ, kāmā <pb ed="T" n="0.0298" /> aniccā iti cāpi āhu;
```

```
Rāgañca tesaṃ na balatthi chettuṃ, tasmā sitā puttadāraṃ dhanañcā’’ti.
```

… Isidinno thero….

#### 5. Sambulakaccānattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§189.</p>

```
‘‘Devo <pb ed="M" n="0.0257" /> ca vassati devo ca gaḷagaḷāyati,
```

```
Ekako cāhaṃ bherave bile viharāmi;
```

```
Tassa mayhaṃ ekakassa bherave bile viharato,
```

```
Natthi bhayaṃ vā chambhitattaṃ vā lomahaṃso vā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§190.</p>

```
‘‘Dhammatā <pb ed="V" n="0.0198" /> mamasā yassa me, ekakassa bherave bile;
```

```
Viharato natthi bhayaṃ vā, chambhitattaṃ vā lomahaṃso vā’’ti.
```

… Sambulakaccāno <note>sambahulakaccāno (ka.)</note> thero….

#### 6. Nitakattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§191.</p>

```
<note>udā. 34 udānepi</note> ‘‘Kassa <pb ed="P" n="0.0025" /> selūpamaṃ cittaṃ, ṭhitaṃ nānupakampati;
```

```
Virattaṃ rajanīyesu, kuppanīye na kuppati;
```

```
Yassevaṃ bhāvitaṃ cittaṃ, kuto taṃ dukkhamessati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§192.</p>

```
‘‘Mama selūpamaṃ cittaṃ, ṭhitaṃ nānupakampati;
```

```
Virattaṃ rajanīyesu, kuppanīye na kuppati;
```

```
Mamevaṃ bhāvitaṃ cittaṃ, kuto maṃ dukkhamessatī’’ti.
```

… Nitako <note>khitako (sī. syā.)</note> thero….

#### 7. Soṇapoṭiriyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§193.</p>

```
‘‘Na tāva supituṃ hoti, ratti nakkhattamālinī;
```

```
Paṭijaggitumevesā, ratti hoti vijānatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§194.</p>

```
‘‘Hatthikkhandhāvapatitaṃ<pb ed="T" n="0.0299" />, kuñjaro ce anukkame;
```

```
Saṅgāme me mataṃ seyyo, yañce jīve parājito’’ti.
```

… Soṇo poṭiriyo <note>selissariyo (sī.), poṭṭiriyaputto (syā.)</note> thero ….

```
‘‘Nābhinandāmi maraṇaṃ, nābhinandāmi jīvitaṃ;

```

#### 9. Usabhattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§197.</p>

```
‘‘Ambapallavasaṅkāsaṃ, aṃse katvāna cīvaraṃ;
```

```
Nisinno hatthigīvāyaṃ, gāmaṃ piṇḍāya pāvisiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§198.</p>

```
‘‘Hatthikkhandhato <pb ed="V" n="0.0199" /> oruyha, saṃvegaṃ alabhiṃ tadā;
```

```
Sohaṃ ditto tadā santo, patto me āsavakkhayo’’ti.
```

… Usabho thero….

#### 10. Kappaṭakurattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§199.</p>

```
‘‘Ayamiti kappaṭo kappaṭakuro, acchāya atibharitāya <note>atibhariyāya (sī. ka.), accaṃ bharāya (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Amataghaṭikāyaṃ dhammakaṭamatto <note>dhammakaṭapatto (syā. ka. aṭṭha.), dhammakaṭamaggo (sī. aṭṭha.)</note>, katapadaṃ jhānāni ocetuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§200.</p>

```
‘‘Mā <pb ed="P" n="0.0026" /> kho tvaṃ kappaṭa pacālesi, mā tvaṃ upakaṇṇamhi tāḷessaṃ;
```

```
Na <pb ed="T" n="0.0300" /> hi <note>na vā (ka.)</note> tvaṃ kappaṭa mattamaññāsi, saṅghamajjhamhi pacalāyamānoti.
```

… Kappaṭakuro thero….

Vaggo catuttho niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Migasiro <pb ed="M" n="0.0259" /> sivako ca, upavāno ca paṇḍito;
```

```
Isidinno ca kaccāno, nitako ca mahāvasī;
```

```
Poṭiriyaputto nisabho, usabho kappaṭakuroti.
```

#### 5. Pañcamavaggo

#### 1. Kumārakassapattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§201.</p>

```
‘‘Aho buddhā aho dhammā, aho no satthu sampadā;
```

```
Yattha etādisaṃ dhammaṃ, sāvako sacchikāhi’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§202.</p>

```
‘‘Asaṅkheyyesu kappesu, sakkāyādhigatā ahū;
```

```
Tesamayaṃ pacchimako, carimoyaṃ samussayo;
```

```
Jātimaraṇasaṃsāro, natthi dāni punabbhavo’’ti.
```

… Kumārakassapo thero….

#### 2. Dhammapālattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§203.</p>

```
‘‘Yo <pb ed="V" n="0.0200" /> have daharo bhikkhu, yuñjati buddhasāsane;
```

```
Jāgaro sa hi suttesu <note>patisuttesu (sī. ka.)</note>, amoghaṃ tassa jīvitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§204.</p>

```
‘‘Tasmā <pb ed="T" n="0.0301" /> saddhañca sīlañca, pasādaṃ dhammadassanaṃ;
```

```
Anuyuñjetha medhāvī, saraṃ buddhāna sāsana’’nti.
```

… Dhammapālo thero….

#### 3. Brahmālittheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§205.</p>

```
‘‘Kassindriyāni samathaṅgatāni, assā yathā sārathinā sudantā;
```

Pahīnamānassa anāsavassa, devāpi kassa <note>tassa (bahūsu)</note> pihayanti tādino’’ti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§206.</p>

Pahīnamānassa anāsavassa, devāpi mayhaṃ pihayanti tādino’’ti.
```

… Brahmāli thero….

#### 4. Mogharājattheragāthā

```

Hemantikasītakālarattiyo <note>hemantikakālarattiyo (ka.)</note>, bhikkhu tvaṃsi kathaṃ karissasi’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§208.</p>

```
‘‘Sampannasassā magadhā, kevalā iti me sutaṃ;
```

```
Palālacchannako seyyaṃ, yathaññe sukhajīvino’’ti.
```

… Mogharājā thero….

#### 5. Visākhapañcālaputtattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§209.</p>

```
‘‘Na ukkhipe no ca parikkhipe pare, okkhipe pāragataṃ na eraye;
```

```
Na <pb ed="T" n="0.0302" /> cattavaṇṇaṃ parisāsu byāhare, anuddhato sammitabhāṇi subbato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§210.</p>

```
‘‘Susukhumanipuṇatthadassinā, matikusalena nivātavuttinā;
```

```
Saṃsevitavuddhasīlinā, nibbānaṃ na hi tena dullabha’’nti.
```

… Visākho pañcālaputto thero ….

#### 6. Cūḷakattheragāthā

```

<p rend="hangnum">§212.</p>

```
‘‘Sukallarūpo <pb ed="M" n="0.0261" /> sumanassa jhāyataṃ <note>jhāyitaṃ (syā. ka.)</note>, sunikkamo sādhu subuddhasāsane;
```

```
Susukkasukkaṃ nipuṇaṃ sududdasaṃ, phusāhi taṃ uttamamaccutaṃ pada’’nti.
```

… Cūḷako <note>cūlako (sī. aṭṭha.)</note> thero….

#### 7. Anūpamattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§213.</p>

```
‘‘Nandamānāgataṃ cittaṃ, sūlamāropamānakaṃ;

Tena teneva vajasi, yena sūlaṃ kaliṅgaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§214.</p>

```
‘‘Tāhaṃ cittakaliṃ brūmi, taṃ brūmi cittadubbhakaṃ;
```

```
Satthā te dullabho laddho, mānatthe maṃ niyojayī’’ti.
```

… Anūpamo thero….

#### 8. Vajjitattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§215.</p>

```
‘‘Saṃsaraṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0303" /> dīghamaddhānaṃ, gatīsu parivattisaṃ;
```

```
Apassaṃ ariyasaccāni, andhabhūto <note>andhībhūto (ka.)</note> puthujjano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§216.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa <pb ed="P" n="0.0028" /> me appamattassa, saṃsārā vinaḷīkatā;
```

```
Sabbā gatī samucchinnā, natthi dāni punabbhavo’’ti.
```

… Vajjito thero….

#### 9. Sandhitattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§217.</p>

```
‘‘Assatthe haritobhāse, saṃvirūḷhamhi pādape;
```

```
Ekaṃ buddhagataṃ saññaṃ, alabhitthaṃ <note>alabhiṃ haṃ (ka.)</note> patissato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§218.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā;
```

```
Tassā saññāya vāhasā, patto me āsavakkhayo’’ti.
```

… Sandhito thero….

Vaggo pañcamo niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0202" /> –

```
Kumārakassapo <pb ed="M" n="0.0262" /> thero, dhammapālo ca brahmāli;
```

```
Mogharājā visākho ca, cūḷako ca anūpamo;
```

```
Vajjito sandhito thero, kilesarajavāhanoti.
```

<trailer rend="centre">Dukanipāto niṭṭhito.</trailer>

Tatruddānaṃ –

```
Gāthādukanipātamhi, navuti ceva aṭṭha ca;
```

```
Therā ekūnapaññāsaṃ, bhāsitā nayakovidāti.
```

### 3. Tikanipāto

#### 1. Aṅgaṇikabhāradvājattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§219.</p>

```
‘‘Ayoni <pb ed="T" n="0.0304" /><pb ed="M" n="0.0263" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0203" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0029" /> suddhimanvesaṃ, aggiṃ paricariṃ vane;
```

```
Suddhimaggaṃ ajānanto, akāsiṃ amaraṃ tapaṃ <note>akāsiṃ aparaṃ tapaṃ (syā.), akāsiṃ amataṃ tapaṃ (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§220.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ sukhena sukhaṃ laddhaṃ, passa dhammasudhammataṃ;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§221.</p>

```
‘‘Brahmabandhu pure āsiṃ, idāni khomhi brāhmaṇo;
```

```
Tevijjo nhātako <note>nahātako (sī. aṭṭha.)</note> camhi, sottiyo camhi vedagū’’ti.
```

… Aṅgaṇikabhāradvājo thero….

#### 2. Paccayattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§222.</p>

```
‘‘Pañcāhāhaṃ pabbajito, sekho appattamānaso,
```

```
Vihāraṃ me paviṭṭhassa, cetaso paṇidhī ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§223.</p>

```
‘‘Nāsissaṃ na pivissāmi, vihārato na nikkhame;
```

```
Napi passaṃ nipātessaṃ, taṇhāsalle anūhate.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§224.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa mevaṃ viharato, passa vīriyaparakkamaṃ;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsana’’nti.
```

… Paccayo thero….

#### 3. Bākulattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§225.</p>

```
‘‘Yo pubbe karaṇīyāni, pacchā so kātumicchati;
```

```
Sukhā so dhaṃsate ṭhānā, pacchā ca manutappati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§226.</p>

```
‘‘Yañhi kayirā tañhi vade, yaṃ na kayirā na taṃ vade;
```

```
Akarontaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0305" /> bhāsamānaṃ, parijānanti paṇḍitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§227.</p>

```
‘‘Susukhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0264" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0204" /> vata nibbānaṃ, sammāsambuddhadesitaṃ;
```

```
Asokaṃ virajaṃ khemaṃ, yattha dukkhaṃ nirujjhatī’’ti.
```

… Bākulo <note>bākkulo (sī.)</note> thero….

#### 4. Dhaniyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§228.</p>

```
‘‘Sukhaṃ ce jīvituṃ icche, sāmaññasmiṃ apekkhavā;
```

```
Saṅghikaṃ nātimaññeyya, cīvaraṃ pānabhojanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§229.</p>

```
‘‘Sukhaṃ ce jīvituṃ icche, sāmaññasmiṃ apekkhavā;
```

```
Ahi mūsikasobbhaṃva, sevetha sayanāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§230.</p>

```
‘‘Sukhaṃ ce <pb ed="P" n="0.0030" /> jīvituṃ icche, sāmaññasmiṃ apekkhavā;
```

```
Itarītarena tusseyya, ekadhammañca bhāvaye’’ti.
```

… Dhaniyo thero….

#### 5. Mātaṅgaputtattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§231.</p>

```
‘‘Atisītaṃ atiuṇhaṃ, atisāyamidaṃ ahu;
```

```
Iti vissaṭṭhakammante, khaṇā accenti māṇave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§232.</p>

```
‘‘Yo ca sītañca uṇhañca, tiṇā bhiyyo na maññati;
```

```
Karaṃ purisakiccāni, so sukhā na vihāyati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§233.</p>

```
‘‘Dabbaṃ kusaṃ poṭakilaṃ, usīraṃ muñjapabbajaṃ;
```

```
Urasā panudissāmi, vivekamanubrūhaya’’nti.
```

… Mātaṅgaputto thero….

#### 6. Khujjasobhitattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§234.</p>

```

```

```

```

<p rend="hangnum">§235.</p>

```
‘‘Ye <pb ed="T" n="0.0306" /><pb ed="M" n="0.0265" /> cittakathī bahussutā, samaṇā pāṭaliputtavāsino;
```

```
Tesaññataroyamāyuvā, dvāre tiṭṭhati māluterito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§236.</p>

```
‘‘Suyuddhena suyiṭṭhena, saṅgāmavijayena ca;
```

```
Brahmacariyānuciṇṇena, evāyaṃ sukhamedhatī’’ti.
```

… Khujjasobhito thero….

#### 7. Vāraṇattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§237.</p>

```
‘‘Yodha <pb ed="V" n="0.0205" /> koci manussesu, parapāṇāni hiṃsati;
```

```
Asmā lokā paramhā ca, ubhayā dhaṃsate naro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§238.</p>

```
‘‘Yo ca mettena cittena, sabbapāṇānukampati;
```

```
Bahuñhi so pasavati, puññaṃ tādisako naro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§239.</p>

```
‘‘Subhāsitassa sikkhetha, samaṇūpāsanassa ca;
```

```
Ekāsanassa ca raho, cittavūpasamassa cā’’ti.
```

… Vāraṇo thero….

#### 8. Vassikattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§240.</p>

```
‘‘Ekopi saddho medhāvī, assaddhānīdha ñātinaṃ;
```

```
Dhammaṭṭho sīlasampanno, hoti atthāya bandhunaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§241.</p>

```
‘‘Niggayha anukampāya, coditā ñātayo mayā;
```

```
Ñātibandhavapemena, kāraṃ katvāna bhikkhusu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§242.</p>

```
‘‘Te abbhatītā kālaṅkatā, pattā te tidivaṃ sukhaṃ;
```

```
Bhātaro mayhaṃ mātā ca, modanti kāmakāmino’’ti.
```

… Vassiko <note>passiko (sī. syā. pī.)</note> thero….

#### 9. Yasojattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§243.</p>

```
‘‘Kālapabbaṅgasaṅkāso, kiso dhamanisanthato;
```

```
Mattaññū <pb ed="T" n="0.0307" /> annapānamhi, adīnamanaso naro’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§244.</p>

```
‘‘Phuṭṭho <pb ed="M" n="0.0266" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0031" /> ḍaṃsehi makasehi, araññasmiṃ brahāvane;
```

```
Nāgo saṅgāmasīseva, sato tatrādhivāsaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§245.</p>

```
‘‘Yathā brahmā tathā eko, yathā devo tathā duve;
```

```
Yathā gāmo tathā tayo, kolāhalaṃ tatuttari’’nti.
```

… Yasojo thero….

#### 10. Sāṭimattiyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§246.</p>

```
‘‘Ahu <pb ed="V" n="0.0206" /> tuyhaṃ pure saddhā, sā te ajja na vijjati;
```

```
Yaṃ tuyhaṃ tuyhamevetaṃ, natthi duccaritaṃ mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§247.</p>

```
‘‘Aniccā hi calā saddā, evaṃ diṭṭhā hi sā mayā;
```

```
Rajjantipi virajjanti, tattha kiṃ jiyyate muni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§248.</p>

```
‘‘Paccati munino bhattaṃ, thokaṃ thokaṃ kule kule;
```

```
Piṇḍikāya carissāmi, atthi jaṅghabalaṃ <note>jaṅghābalaṃ (sī.)</note> mamā’’ti.
```

… Sāṭimattiyo thero….

#### 11. Upālittheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§249.</p>

```
‘‘Saddhāya abhinikkhamma, navapabbajito navo;
```

```
Mitte bhajeyya kalyāṇe, suddhājīve atandite.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§250.</p>

```
‘‘Saddhāya abhinikkhamma, navapabbajito navo;
```

```
Saṅghasmiṃ viharaṃ bhikkhu, sikkhetha vinayaṃ budho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§251.</p>

```
‘‘Saddhāya abhinikkhamma, navapabbajito navo;
```

```
Kappākappesu kusalo, careyya apurakkhato’’ti.
```

… Upālitthero….

#### 12. Uttarapālattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§252.</p>

```
‘‘Paṇḍitaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0308" /> vata maṃ santaṃ, alamatthavicintakaṃ;
```

```
Pañca kāmaguṇā loke, sammohā pātayiṃsu maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§253.</p>

```
‘‘Pakkhando māravisaye, daḷhasallasamappito;
```

```
Asakkhiṃ maccurājassa, ahaṃ pāsā pamuccituṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§254.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbe <pb ed="M" n="0.0267" /> kāmā pahīnā me, bhavā sabbe padālitā <note>vidālitā (sī. pī. aṭṭha.)</note>;
```

```
Vikkhīṇo jātisaṃsāro, natthi dāni punabbhavo’’ti.
```

… Uttarapālo thero….

#### 13. Abhibhūtattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§255.</p>

```
‘‘Suṇātha ñātayo sabbe, yāvantettha samāgatā;
```

```
Dhammaṃ vo desayissāmi, dukkhā jāti punappunaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§256.</p>

```
<note>saṃ. ni. 1.185</note> ‘‘Ārambhatha <note>ārabhatha (sī. syā.), ārabbhatha (ka.)</note> nikkamatha, yuñjatha buddhasāsane;
```

```
Dhunātha maccuno senaṃ, naḷāgāraṃva kuñjaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§257.</p>

```
‘‘Yo <pb ed="V" n="0.0207" /> imasmiṃ dhammavinaye, **appamatto** vihassati <note>vihessati (syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Pahāya jātisaṃsāraṃ, dukkhassantaṃ karissatī’’ti.
```

… Abhibhūto thero….

#### 14. Gotamattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§258.</p>

```
‘‘Saṃsaraṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0032" /> hi nirayaṃ agacchissaṃ, petalokamagamaṃ punappunaṃ;
```

```
Dukkhamamhipi tiracchānayoniyaṃ, nekadhā hi vusitaṃ ciraṃ mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§259.</p>

```
‘‘Mānusopi ca bhavobhirādhito, saggakāyamagamaṃ sakiṃ sakiṃ;
```

```
Rūpadhātusu <pb ed="T" n="0.0309" /> arūpadhātusu, nevasaññisu asaññisuṭṭhitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§260.</p>

```
‘‘Sambhavā suviditā asārakā, saṅkhatā pacalitā saderitā;
```

```
Taṃ viditvā mahamattasambhavaṃ, santimeva satimā samajjhaga’’nti.
```

… Gotamo thero….

#### 15. Hāritattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§261.</p>

```
‘‘Yo pubbe karaṇīyāni, pacchā so kātumicchati;
```

```
Sukhā so dhaṃsate ṭhānā, pacchā ca manutappati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§262.</p>

```
‘‘Yañhi <pb ed="M" n="0.0268" /> kayirā tañhi vade, yaṃ na kayirā na taṃ vade;
```

```
Akarontaṃ bhāsamānaṃ, parijānanti paṇḍitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§263.</p>

```
‘‘Susukhaṃ vata nibbānaṃ, sammāsambuddhadesitaṃ;
```

```
Asokaṃ virajaṃ khemaṃ, yattha dukkhaṃ nirujjhatī’’ti.
```

… Hārito thero….

#### 16. Vimalattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§264.</p>

```
‘‘Pāpamitte vivajjetvā, bhajeyyuttamapuggalaṃ;
```

```
Ovāde cassa tiṭṭheyya, patthento acalaṃ sukhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§265.</p>

```
‘‘Parittaṃ dārumāruyha, yathā sīde mahaṇṇave;
```

```
Evaṃ kusītamāgamma, sādhujīvīpi sīdati;
```

```
Tasmā taṃ parivajjeyya, kusītaṃ hīnavīriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§266.</p>

```
‘‘Pavivittehi <pb ed="V" n="0.0208" /> ariyehi, pahitattehi jhāyibhi;
```

```
Niccaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0310" /> āraddhavīriyehi, paṇḍitehi sahāvase’’ti.
```

… Vimalo thero….

<trailer rend="centre">Tikanipāto niṭṭhito.</trailer>

Tatruddānaṃ –

```
Aṅgaṇiko bhāradvājo, paccayo bākulo isi;
```

```
Dhaniyo mātaṅgaputto, sobhito vāraṇo isi.
```

```
Vassiko ca yasojo ca, sāṭimattiyupāli ca;
```

```
Uttarapālo abhibhūto, gotamo hāritopi ca.
```

```
Thero tikanipātamhi, nibbāne vimalo kato;
```

```
Aṭṭhatālīsa gāthāyo, therā soḷasa kittitāti.
```

### 4. Catukanipāto

#### 1. Nāgasamālattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§267.</p>

```
‘‘Alaṅkatā <pb ed="M" n="0.0269" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0209" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0033" /> suvasanā, mālinī candanussadā;
```

```
Majjhe mahāpathe nārī, turiye naccati naṭṭakī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§268.</p>

```
‘‘Piṇḍikāya paviṭṭhohaṃ, gacchanto naṃ udikkhisaṃ;
```

```
Alaṅkataṃ suvasanaṃ, maccupāsaṃva oḍḍitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§269.</p>

```
‘‘Tato me manasīkāro, yoniso udapajjatha;
```

```
Ādīnavo pāturahu, nibbidā samatiṭṭhatha <note>sampatiṭṭhatha (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§270.</p>

```
‘‘Tato cittaṃ vimucci me, passa dhammasudhammataṃ;
```

```
Tisso <pb ed="T" n="0.0311" /> vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsana’’nti.
```

… Nāgasamālo thero….

#### 2. Bhaguttheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§271.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ middhena pakato, vihārā upanikkhamiṃ;
```

```
Caṅkamaṃ abhiruhanto, tattheva papatiṃ chamā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§272.</p>

```
‘‘Gattāni parimajjitvā, punapāruyha caṅkamaṃ;
```

```
Caṅkame caṅkamiṃ sohaṃ, ajjhattaṃ susamāhito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§273.</p>

```
‘‘Tato me manasīkāro, yoniso udapajjatha;
```

```
Ādīnavo pāturahu, nibbidā samatiṭṭhatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§274.</p>

```
‘‘Tato cittaṃ vimucci me, passa dhammasudhammataṃ;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsana’’nti.
```

… Bhagutthero….

#### 3. Sabhiyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§275.</p>

```
<note>dha. pa. 6 dhammapadepi</note> ‘‘Pare ca na vijānanti, mayamettha yamāmase;
```

```
Ye ca tattha vijānanti, tato sammanti medhagā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§276.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā <pb ed="V" n="0.0210" /> ca avijānantā, iriyantyamarā viya;
```

```
Vijānanti ca ye dhammaṃ, āturesu anāturā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§277.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0270" /> kiñci sithilaṃ kammaṃ, saṃkiliṭṭhañca yaṃ vataṃ;
```

```
Saṅkassaraṃ brahmacariyaṃ, na taṃ hoti mahapphalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§278.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa sabrahmacārīsu, gāravo nūpalabbhati;
```

```
Ārakā hoti saddhammā, nabhaṃ puthaviyā yathā’’ti.
```

… Sabhiyo thero….

#### 4. Nandakattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§279.</p>

```
‘‘Dhiratthu <pb ed="T" n="0.0312" /> pūre duggandhe, mārapakkhe avassute;
```

```
Navasotāni te kāye, yāni sandanti sabbadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§280.</p>

```
‘‘Mā <pb ed="P" n="0.0034" /> purāṇaṃ amaññittho, māsādesi tathāgate;
```

```
Saggepi te na rajjanti, kimaṅgaṃ pana <note>kimaṅga pana (sī.)</note> mānuse.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§281.</p>

```
‘‘Ye ca kho bālā dummedhā, dummantī mohapārutā;
```

```
Tādisā tattha rajjanti, mārakhittamhi bandhane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§282.</p>

```
‘‘Yesaṃ rāgo ca doso ca, avijjā ca virājitā;
```

```
Tādī tattha na rajjanti, chinnasuttā abandhanā’’ti.
```

… Nandako thero….

#### 5. Jambukattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§283.</p>

```
‘‘Pañcapaññāsavassāni, rajojallamadhārayiṃ;
```

```
Bhuñjanto māsikaṃ bhattaṃ, kesamassuṃ alocayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§284.</p>

```
‘‘Ekapādena aṭṭhāsiṃ, āsanaṃ parivajjayiṃ;
```

```
Sukkhagūthāni ca khādiṃ, uddesañca na sādiyiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§285.</p>

```
‘‘Etādisaṃ karitvāna, bahuṃ duggatigāminaṃ;
```

```
Vuyhamāno mahoghena, buddhaṃ saraṇamāgamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§286.</p>

```
‘‘Saraṇagamanaṃ passa, passa dhammasudhammataṃ;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsana’’nti.
```

… Jambuko thero….

#### 6. Senakattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§287.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0271" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0211" /> vata me āsi, gayāyaṃ gayaphagguyā;
```

```
Yaṃ addasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ, desentaṃ dhammamuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§288.</p>

```
‘‘Mahappabhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0313" /> gaṇācariyaṃ, aggapattaṃ vināyakaṃ;
```

```
Sadevakassa lokassa, jinaṃ atuladassanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§289.</p>

```
‘‘Mahānāgaṃ mahāvīraṃ, mahājutimanāsavaṃ;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇaṃ, satthāramakutobhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§290.</p>

```
‘‘Cirasaṃkiliṭṭhaṃ vata maṃ, diṭṭhisandānabandhitaṃ <note>sandhitaṃ (sī. syā.), sanditaṃ (pī. sī. aṭṭha.)</note>;
```

```
Vimocayi so bhagavā, sabbaganthehi senaka’’nti.
```

… Senako thero….

#### 7. Sambhūtattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§291.</p>

```
‘‘Yo dandhakāle tarati, taraṇīye ca dandhaye;
```

```
Ayoni <note>ayoniso (syā.)</note> saṃvidhānena, bālo dukkhaṃ nigacchati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§292.</p>

```
‘‘Tassatthā parihāyanti, kāḷapakkheva candimā;
```

```
Āyasakyañca <note>āyasasyañca (sī.)</note> pappoti, mittehi ca virujjhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§293.</p>

```
‘‘Yo dandhakāle dandheti, taraṇīye ca tāraye;
```

```
Yoniso saṃvidhānena, sukhaṃ pappoti paṇḍito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§294.</p>

```
‘‘Tassatthā paripūrenti, sukkapakkheva candimā;
```

```
Yaso kittiñca pappoti, mittehi na virujjhatī’’ti.
```

… Sambhūto thero….

#### 8. Rāhulattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§295.</p>

```
‘‘Ubhayeneva <pb ed="P" n="0.0035" /> sampanno, rāhulabhaddoti maṃ vidū;
```

```
Yañcamhi putto buddhassa, yañca dhammesu cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§296.</p>

```
‘‘Yañca me āsavā khīṇā, yañca natthi punabbhavo;
```

```
Arahā <pb ed="T" n="0.0314" /> dakkhiṇeyyomhi, tevijjo amataddaso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§297.</p>

```
‘‘Kāmandhā <pb ed="M" n="0.0272" /> jālapacchannā, taṇhāchādanachāditā;
```

```
Pamattabandhunā baddhā, macchāva kumināmukhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§298.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0212" /> kāmaṃ ahamujjhitvā, chetvā mārassa bandhanaṃ;
```

```
Samūlaṃ taṇhamabbuyha, sītibhūtosmi nibbuto’’ti.
```

… Rāhulo thero….

#### 9. Candanattheragāthā

```

Aṅkena puttamādāya, bhariyā maṃ upāgami.

```
‘‘Tañca disvāna āyantiṃ, sakaputtassa mātaraṃ;

… Candano thero….

#### 10. Dhammikattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§303.</p>

```
<note>jā. 1.10.102 jātakepi</note> ‘‘Dhammo have rakkhati dhammacāriṃ, dhammo suciṇṇo sukhamāvahati;
```

```
Esānisaṃso dhamme suciṇṇe, na duggatiṃ gacchati dhammacārī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§304.</p>

```
<note>jā. 1.15.385</note> ‘‘Nahi dhammo adhammo ca, ubho samavipākino;
```

```
Adhammo <pb ed="T" n="0.0315" /> nirayaṃ neti, dhammo pāpeti suggatiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§305.</p>

```
‘‘Tasmā hi dhammesu kareyya chandaṃ, iti modamāno sugatena tādinā;
```

```
Dhamme ṭhitā sugatavarassa sāvakā, nīyanti dhīrā saraṇavaraggagāmino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§306.</p>

```
‘‘Vipphoṭito <pb ed="M" n="0.0273" /> gaṇḍamūlo, taṇhājālo samūhato;
```

```
So khīṇasaṃsāro na catthi kiñcanaṃ,
```

```
Cando yathā dosinā puṇṇamāsiya’’nti.
```

… Dhammiko thero….

#### 11. Sappakattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§307.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā balākā sucipaṇḍaracchadā, kāḷassa meghassa bhayena tajjitā;
```

```
Palehiti ālayamālayesinī, tadā nadī ajakaraṇī rameti maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§308.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā <pb ed="V" n="0.0213" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0036" /> balākā suvisuddhapaṇḍarā, kāḷassa meghassa bhayena tajjitā;
```

```
Pariyesati leṇamaleṇadassinī, tadā nadī ajakaraṇī rameti maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§309.</p>

```
‘‘Kaṃ nu tattha na ramenti, jambuyo ubhato tahiṃ;
```

```
Sobhenti āpagākūlaṃ, mama leṇassa <note>mahāleṇassa (syā. ka.)</note> pacchato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§310.</p>

```
‘‘Tā matamadasaṅghasuppahīnā,
```

```
Bhekā <pb ed="T" n="0.0316" /> mandavatī panādayanti;
```

```
‘Nājja girinadīhi vippavāsasamayo,
```

```
Khemā ajakaraṇī sivā surammā’’’ti.
```

… Sappako thero….

#### 12. Muditattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§311.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbajiṃ jīvikatthohaṃ, laddhāna upasampadaṃ;
```

```
Tato saddhaṃ paṭilabhiṃ, daḷhavīriyo parakkamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§312.</p>

```
‘‘Kāmaṃ bhijjatuyaṃ kāyo, maṃsapesī visīyaruṃ <note>visiyantu (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Ubho jaṇṇukasandhīhi, jaṅghāyo papatantu me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§313.</p>

```
‘‘Nāsissaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0274" /> na pivissāmi, vihārā ca na nikkhame;
```

```
Napi passaṃ nipātessaṃ, taṇhāsalle anūhate.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§314.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa mevaṃ viharato, passa vīriyaparakkamaṃ;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsana’’nti.
```

… Mudito thero….

<trailer rend="centre">Catukkanipāto niṭṭhito.</trailer>

Tatruddānaṃ –

```
Nāgasamālo bhagu ca, sabhiyo nandakopi ca;
```

```
Jambuko senako thero, sambhūto rāhulopi ca.
```

```
Bhavati candano thero, dasete <note>idāni naveva therā dissanti</note> buddhasāvakā;
```

```
Dhammiko sappako thero, mudito cāpi te tayo;
```

```
Gāthāyo dve ca paññāsa, therā sabbepi terasāti <note>idāni dvādaseva therā dissanti</note>.
```

### 5. Pañcakanipāto

#### 1. Rājadattattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§315.</p>

```
‘‘Bhikkhu <pb ed="T" n="0.0317" /><pb ed="M" n="0.0275" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0214" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0037" /> sivathikaṃ <note>sīvathikaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> gantvā, addasa itthimujjhitaṃ;
```

```
Apaviddhaṃ susānasmiṃ, khajjantiṃ kimihī phuṭaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§316.</p>

```
‘‘Yañhi eke jigucchanti, mataṃ disvāna pāpakaṃ;
```

```
Kāmarāgo pāturahu, andhova savatī <note>vasatī (sī.)</note> ahuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§317.</p>

```
‘‘Oraṃ odanapākamhā, tamhā ṭhānā apakkamiṃ;
```

```
Satimā sampajānohaṃ, ekamantaṃ upāvisiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§318.</p>

```
‘‘Tato me manasīkāro, yoniso udapajjatha;
```

```
Ādīnavo pāturahu, nibbidā samatiṭṭhatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§319.</p>

```
‘‘Tato cittaṃ vimucci me, passa dhammasudhammataṃ;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsana’’nti.
```

… Rājadatto thero….

#### 2. Subhūtattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§320.</p>

```
‘‘Ayoge yuñjamattānaṃ, puriso kiccamicchako <note>kiccamicchato (sī.), kiccamicchayaṃ (katthaci)</note>;
```

```
Caraṃ ce nādhigaccheyya, ‘taṃ me dubbhagalakkhaṇaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§321.</p>

```
‘‘Abbūḷhaṃ aghagataṃ vijitaṃ, ekañce ossajeyya kalīva siyā;
```

```
Sabbānipi ce ossajeyya andhova siyā, samavisamassa adassanato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§322.</p>

```
‘‘Yañhi <pb ed="T" n="0.0318" /> kayirā tañhi vade, yaṃ na kayirā na taṃ vade;
```

```
Akarontaṃ bhāsamānaṃ, parijānanti paṇḍitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§323.</p>

```
<note>dha. pa. 51 dhammapadepi</note> ‘‘Yathāpi ruciraṃ pupphaṃ, vaṇṇavantaṃ agandhakaṃ;
```

```
Evaṃ subhāsitā vācā, aphalā hoti akubbato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§324.</p>

```
<note>dha. pa. 52</note> ‘‘Yathāpi <pb ed="M" n="0.0276" /> ruciraṃ pupphaṃ, vaṇṇavantaṃ sugandhakaṃ <note>sagandhakaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Evaṃ subhāsitā vācā, saphalā hoti kubbato’’ti <note>sakubbato (sī. pī.), sukubbato (syā.)</note>.
```

… Subhūto thero….

#### 3. Girimānandattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§325.</p>

```
‘‘Vassati <pb ed="V" n="0.0215" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0038" /> devo yathā sugītaṃ, channā me kuṭikā sukhā nivātā;
```

```
Tassaṃ viharāmi vūpasanto, atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§326.</p>

```
‘‘Vassati devo yathā sugītaṃ, channā me kuṭikā sukhā nivātā;
```

```
Tassaṃ viharāmi santacitto, atha ce patthayasī pavassa deva.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§327.</p>

```
‘‘Vassati devo…pe… tassaṃ viharāmi vītarāgo…pe….
```

<p rend="hangnum">§328.</p>

```
‘‘Vassati devo…pe… tassaṃ viharāmi vītadoso…pe….
```

<p rend="hangnum">§329.</p>

```
‘‘Vassati devo…pe… tassaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0319" /> viharāmi vītamoho;
```

```
Atha ce patthayasī pavassa devā’’ti.
```

… Girimānando thero….

#### 4. Sumanattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§330.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ patthayāno dhammesu, upajjhāyo anuggahi;
```

```
Amataṃ abhikaṅkhantaṃ, kataṃ kattabbakaṃ mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§331.</p>

```
‘‘Anuppatto sacchikato, sayaṃ dhammo anītiho;
```

```
Visuddhiñāṇo nikkaṅkho, byākaromi tavantike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§332.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
```

```
Sadattho me anuppatto, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§333.</p>

```
‘‘Appamattassa me sikkhā, sussutā tava sāsane;
```

```
Sabbe me āsavā khīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§334.</p>

```
‘‘Anusāsi <pb ed="M" n="0.0277" /> maṃ ariyavatā, anukampi anuggahi;
```

```
Amogho tuyhamovādo, antevāsimhi sikkhito’’ti.
```

… Sumano thero….

#### 5. Vaḍḍhattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§335.</p>

```
‘‘Sādhū hi kira me mātā, patodaṃ upadaṃsayi;
```

```
Yassāhaṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, anusiṭṭho janettiyā;
```

```
Āraddhavīriyo pahitatto, patto sambodhimuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§336.</p>

```
‘‘Arahā <pb ed="V" n="0.0216" /> dakkhiṇeyyomhi, tevijjo amataddaso;
```

```
Jetvā namucino senaṃ, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§337.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjhattañca <pb ed="T" n="0.0320" /> bahiddhā ca, ye me vijjiṃsu āsavā;
```

```
Sabbe asesā ucchinnā, na ca uppajjare puna.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§338.</p>

```
‘‘Visāradā kho bhaginī, etamatthaṃ abhāsayi;
```

```
‘Apihā nūna mayipi, vanatho te na vijjati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§339.</p>

```
‘‘Pariyantakataṃ dukkhaṃ, antimoyaṃ samussayo;
```

```
Jātimaraṇasaṃsāro, natthi dāni punabbhavo’’ti.
```

… Vaḍḍho thero….

#### 6. Nadīkassapattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§340.</p>

```
‘‘Atthāya vata me buddho, nadiṃ nerañjaraṃ agā;
```

```
Yassāhaṃ dhammaṃ sutvāna, micchādiṭṭhiṃ vivajjayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§341.</p>

```
‘‘Yajiṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0039" /> uccāvace yaññe, aggihuttaṃ juhiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
‘Esā suddhī’ti maññanto, andhabhūto <note>andhībhūto (ka.)</note> puthujjano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§342.</p>

```
‘‘Diṭṭhigahanapakkhando <note>pakkhanto (sī.), pakkhanno (syā. pī.)</note>, parāmāsena mohito;
```

```
Asuddhiṃ maññisaṃ suddhiṃ, andhabhūto aviddasu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§343.</p>

```
‘‘Micchādiṭṭhi pahīnā me, bhavā sabbe padālitā <note>vidālitā (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Juhāmi dakkhiṇeyyaggiṃ, namassāmi tathāgataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§344.</p>

```
‘‘Mohā <pb ed="M" n="0.0278" /> sabbe pahīnā me, bhavataṇhā padālitā;
```

```
Vikkhīṇo jātisaṃsāro, natthi dāni punabbhavo’’ti.
```

… Nadīkassapo thero….

#### 7. Gayākassapattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§345.</p>

```
‘‘Pāto majjhanhikaṃ sāyaṃ, tikkhattuṃ divasassahaṃ;
```

```
Otariṃ udakaṃ sohaṃ, gayāya gayaphagguyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§346.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0321" /> mayā pakataṃ pāpaṃ, pubbe aññāsu jātisu;
```

```
Taṃ dānīdha pavāhemi’, evaṃdiṭṭhi pure ahuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§347.</p>

```
‘‘Sutvā <pb ed="V" n="0.0217" /> subhāsitaṃ vācaṃ, dhammatthasahitaṃ padaṃ;
```

```
Tathaṃ yāthāvakaṃ atthaṃ, yoniso paccavekkhisaṃ;
```

<p rend="hangnum">§348.</p>

```
‘‘Ninhātasabbapāpomhi, nimmalo payato suci;
```

```
Suddho suddhassa dāyādo, putto buddhassa oraso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§349.</p>

```
‘‘Ogayhaṭṭhaṅgikaṃ sotaṃ, sabbapāpaṃ pavāhayiṃ;
```

```
Tisso vijjā ajjhagamiṃ, kataṃ buddhassa sāsana’’nti.
```

… Gayākassapo thero….

#### 8. Vakkalittheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§350.</p>

```
‘‘Vātarogābhinīto tvaṃ, viharaṃ kānane vane;
```

```
Paviṭṭhagocare lūkhe, kathaṃ bhikkhu karissasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§351.</p>

```
‘‘Pītisukhena vipulena, pharamāno samussayaṃ;
```

```
Lūkhampi abhisambhonto, viharissāmi kānane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§352.</p>

```
‘‘Bhāvento satipaṭṭhāne, indriyāni balāni ca;
```

```
Bojjhaṅgāni ca bhāvento, viharissāmi kānane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§353.</p>

```
‘‘Āraddhavīriye pahitatte, niccaṃ daḷhaparakkame <note>āraddhavīriyo pahitatto, niccaṃ daḷhaparakkamo (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Samagge sahite disvā, viharissāmi kānane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§354.</p>

```
‘‘Anussaranto sambuddhaṃ, aggaṃ dantaṃ samāhitaṃ;
```

```
Atandito <pb ed="T" n="0.0322" /> rattindivaṃ, viharissāmi kānane’’ti.
```

… Vakkalitthero….

#### 9. Vijitasenattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§355.</p>

```
‘‘Olaggessāmi <pb ed="M" n="0.0279" /> te citta, āṇidvāreva hatthinaṃ;
```

```
Na taṃ pāpe niyojessaṃ, kāmajāla <note>kāmajālaṃ (syā.)</note> sarīraja <note>sarīrajaṃ (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§356.</p>

```
‘‘Tvaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0040" /> olaggo na gacchasi <note>na gañchisi (pī)</note>, dvāravivaraṃ gajova alabhanto;
```

```
Na ca cittakali punappunaṃ, pasakka <note>pasahaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> pāparato carissasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§357.</p>

```
‘‘Yathā kuñjaraṃ adantaṃ, navaggahamaṅkusaggaho;
```

```
Balavā āvatteti akāmaṃ, evaṃ āvattayissaṃ taṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§358.</p>

```
‘‘Yathā varahayadamakusalo, sārathi pavaro dameti ājaññaṃ;
```

```
Evaṃ damayissaṃ taṃ, patiṭṭhito pañcasu balesu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§359.</p>

```
‘‘Satiyā <pb ed="V" n="0.0218" /> taṃ nibandhissaṃ, payutto te damessāmi <note>payatatto vodapessāmi (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Vīriyadhuraniggahito, na yito dūraṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0323" /> gamissase cittā’’ti.
```

… Vijitaseno thero….

#### 10. Yasadattattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§360.</p>

```
‘‘Upārambhacitto dummedho, suṇāti jinasāsanaṃ;
```

```
Ārakā hoti saddhammā, nabhaso pathavī yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§361.</p>

```
‘‘Upārambhacitto dummedho, suṇāti jinasāsanaṃ;
```

```
Parihāyati saddhammā, kāḷapakkheva candimā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§362.</p>

```
‘‘Upārambhacitto dummedho, suṇāti jinasāsanaṃ;
```

```
Parisussati saddhamme, maccho appodake yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§363.</p>

```
‘‘Upārambhacitto dummedho, suṇāti jinasāsanaṃ;
```

```
Na virūhati saddhamme, khette bījaṃva pūtikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§364.</p>

```
‘‘Yo ca tuṭṭhena cittena, suṇāti jinasāsanaṃ;
```

```
Khepetvā āsave sabbe, sacchikatvā akuppataṃ;
```

```
Pappuyya paramaṃ santiṃ, parinibbātināsavo’’ti.
```

… Yasadatto thero….

#### 11. Soṇakuṭikaṇṇattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§365.</p>

```
‘‘Upasampadā <pb ed="M" n="0.0280" /> ca me laddhā, vimutto camhi anāsavo;
```

```
