So ca me bhagavā diṭṭho, vihāre ca sahāvasiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§366.</p>

```
‘‘Bahudeva rattiṃ bhagavā, abbhokāsetināmayi;
```

```
Vihārakusalo satthā, vihāraṃ pāvisī tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§367.</p>

```
‘‘Santharitvāna saṅghāṭiṃ, seyyaṃ kappesi gotamo;
```

```
Sīho <pb ed="T" n="0.0324" /> selaguhāyaṃva, pahīnabhayabheravo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§368.</p>

```
‘‘Tato kalyāṇavākkaraṇo, sammāsambuddhasāvako;
```

```
Soṇo abhāsi saddhammaṃ, buddhaseṭṭhassa sammukhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§369.</p>

```
‘‘Pañcakkhandhe pariññāya, bhāvayitvāna añjasaṃ;
```

```
Pappuyya paramaṃ santiṃ, parinibbissatyanāsavo’’ti.
```

… Soṇo kuṭikaṇṇathero….

#### 12. Kosiyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§370.</p>

```
‘‘Yo <pb ed="V" n="0.0219" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0041" /> ve garūnaṃ vacanaññu dhīro, vase ca tamhi janayetha pemaṃ;
```

```
So bhattimā nāma ca hoti paṇḍito, ñatvā ca dhammesu visesi assa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§371.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ āpadā uppatitā uḷārā, nakkhambhayante paṭisaṅkhayantaṃ;
```

```
So thāmavā nāma ca hoti paṇḍito, ñatvā ca dhammesu visesi assa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§372.</p>

```
‘‘Yo ve samuddova ṭhito anejo, gambhīrapañño nipuṇatthadassī;
```

```
Asaṃhāriyo nāma ca hoti paṇḍito, ñatvā ca dhammesu visesi assa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§373.</p>

```
‘‘Bahussuto dhammadharo ca hoti, dhammassa <pb ed="T" n="0.0325" /> hoti anudhammacārī;
```

```
So tādiso nāma ca hoti paṇḍito, ñatvā ca dhammesu visesi assa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§374.</p>

```
‘‘Atthañca <pb ed="M" n="0.0281" /> yo jānāti bhāsitassa, atthañca ñatvāna tathā karoti;
```

```
Atthantaro nāma sa hoti paṇḍito, ñatvā ca dhammesu visesi assā’’ti.
```

… Kosiyo thero….

<trailer rend="centre">Pañcakanipāto niṭṭhito.</trailer>

Tatruddānaṃ –

```
Rājadatto subhūto ca, girimānandasumanā;
```

```
Vaḍḍho ca kassapo thero, gayākassapavakkalī.
```

```
Vijito yasadatto ca, soṇo kosiyasavhayo;
```

```
Saṭṭhi ca pañca gāthāyo, therā ca ettha dvādasāti.
```

### 6. Chakkanipāto

#### 1. Uruveḷakassapattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§375.</p>

```
‘‘Disvāna <pb ed="M" n="0.0282" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0220" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0042" /> pāṭihīrāni, gotamassa yasassino;
```

```
Na tāvāhaṃ paṇipatiṃ, issāmānena vañcito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§376.</p>

```
‘‘Mama saṅkappamaññāya, codesi narasārathi;
```

```
Tato <pb ed="T" n="0.0326" /> me āsi saṃvego, abbhuto lomahaṃsano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§377.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbe jaṭilabhūtassa, yā me siddhi parittikā;
```

```
Tāhaṃ tadā nirākatvā <note>niraṃkatvā (syā. ka.)</note>, pabbajiṃ jinasāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§378.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbe yaññena santuṭṭho, kāmadhātupurakkhato;
```

```
Pacchā rāgañca dosañca, mohañcāpi samūhaniṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§379.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
```

```
Iddhimā paracittaññū, dibbasotañca pāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§380.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa catthāya pabbajito, agārasmānagāriyaṃ;
```

```
So me attho anuppatto, sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo’’ti.
```

… Uruveḷakassapo thero….

#### 2. Tekicchakārittheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§381.</p>

```
‘‘Atihitā vīhi, khalagatā sālī;
```

```
Na ca labhe piṇḍaṃ, kathamahaṃ kassaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§382.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhamappameyyaṃ anussara pasanno;
```

```
Pītiyā phuṭasarīro hohisi satatamudaggo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§383.</p>

```
‘‘Dhammamappameyyaṃ anussara pasanno;
```

```
Pītiyā phuṭasarīro hohisi satatamudaggo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§384.</p>

```
‘‘Saṅghamappameyyaṃ anussara pasanno;
```

```
Pītiyā phuṭasarīro hohisi satatamudaggo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§385.</p>

```
‘‘Abbhokāse <pb ed="M" n="0.0283" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0221" /> viharasi, sītā hemantikā imā ratyo;
```

```
Mā sītena pareto vihaññittho, pavisa <pb ed="T" n="0.0327" /> tvaṃ vihāraṃ phusitaggaḷaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§386.</p>

```
‘‘Phusissaṃ catasso appamaññāyo, tāhi ca sukhito viharissaṃ;
```

```
Nāhaṃ sītena vihaññissaṃ, aniñjito viharanto’’ti.
```

… Tekicchakārī <note>tekicchakāni (sī. syā. pī.)</note> thero….

#### 3. Mahānāgattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§387.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa <pb ed="P" n="0.0043" /> sabrahmacārīsu, gāravo nūpalabbhati;
```

```
Parihāyati saddhammā, maccho appodake yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§388.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa sabrahmacārīsu, gāravo nūpalabbhati;
```

```
Na virūhati saddhamme, khette bījaṃva pūtikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§389.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa sabrahmacārīsu, gāravo nūpalabbhati;
```

```
Ārakā hoti nibbānā <note>nibbāṇā (sī.)</note>, dhammarājassa sāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§390.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa sabrahmacārīsu, gāravo upalabbhati;
```

```
Na vihāyati saddhammā, maccho bavhodake <note>bahvodake (sī.), bahodake (syā.)</note> yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§391.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa sabrahmacārīsu, gāravo upalabbhati;
```

```
So virūhati saddhamme, khette bījaṃva bhaddakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§392.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa sabrahmacārīsu, gāravo upalabbhati;
```

```
Santike hoti nibbānaṃ <note>nibbāṇaṃ (sī.)</note>, dhammarājassa sāsane’’ti.
```

… Mahānāgo thero….

#### 4. Kullattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§393.</p>

```
‘‘Kullo sivathikaṃ gantvā, addasa itthimujjhitaṃ;
```

```
Apaviddhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0328" /> susānasmiṃ, khajjantiṃ kimihī phuṭaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§394.</p>

```
‘‘Āturaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0284" /> asuciṃ pūtiṃ, passa kulla samussayaṃ;
```

```
Uggharantaṃ paggharantaṃ, bālānaṃ abhinanditaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§395.</p>

```
‘‘Dhammādāsaṃ gahetvāna, ñāṇadassanapattiyā;
```

```
Paccavekkhiṃ imaṃ kāyaṃ, tucchaṃ santarabāhiraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§396.</p>

```
‘‘Yathā idaṃ tathā etaṃ, yathā etaṃ tathā idaṃ;
```

```
Yathā adho tathā uddhaṃ, yathā uddhaṃ tathā adho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§397.</p>

```
‘‘Yathā <pb ed="V" n="0.0222" /> divā tathā rattiṃ, yathā rattiṃ tathā divā;
```

```
Yathā pure tathā pacchā, yathā pacchā tathā pure.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§398.</p>

```
‘‘Pañcaṅgikena turiyena, na ratī hoti tādisī;
```

```
Yathā ekaggacittassa, sammā dhammaṃ vipassato’’ti.
```

… Kullo thero….

#### 5. Mālukyaputtattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§399.</p>

```
‘‘Manujassa pamattacārino, taṇhā vaḍḍhati māluvā viya;
```

```
So plavatī <note>plavati (sī. pī. ka.), pariplavati (syā.)</note> hurā huraṃ, phalamicchaṃva vanasmi vānaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§400.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ esā sahate <note>sahati (pī. ka.)</note> jammī, taṇhā loke visattikā;
```

```
Sokā tassa pavaḍḍhanti, abhivaṭṭhaṃva <note>abhivuṭṭhaṃva (syā.), abhivaḍḍhaṃva (ka.)</note> bīraṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§401.</p>

```
‘‘Yo cetaṃ sahate <note>sahati (pī. ka.)</note> jammiṃ, taṇhaṃ loke duraccayaṃ;
```

```
Sokā tamhā papatanti, udabindūva pokkharā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§402.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0044" /> vo vadāmi bhaddaṃ vo, yāvantettha samāgatā;
```

```
Taṇhāya <pb ed="T" n="0.0329" /> mūlaṃ khaṇatha, usīratthova bīraṇaṃ;
```

```
Mā vo naḷaṃva sotova, māro bhañji punappunaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§403.</p>

```
‘‘Karotha buddhavacanaṃ, khaṇo vo mā upaccagā;
```

```
Khaṇātītā hi socanti, nirayamhi samappitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§404.</p>

```
‘‘Pamādo rajo pamādo <note>sabbadā (sī. ka.), suttanipātaṭṭhakathāyaṃ uṭṭhānasuttavaṇṇanā oloketabbā</note>, pamādānupatito rajo;
```

```
Appamādena vijjāya, abbahe sallamattano’’ti.
```

… Mālukyaputto <note>māluṅkyaputto (sī. syā. pī.)</note> thero….

#### 6. Sappadāsattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§405.</p>

```
‘‘Paṇṇavīsativassāni<pb ed="M" n="0.0285" />, yato pabbajito ahaṃ;
```

```
Accharāsaṅghātamattampi, cetosantimanajjhagaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§406.</p>

```
‘‘Aladdhā cittassekaggaṃ, kāmarāgena aṭṭito <note>addito (syā. sī. aṭṭha.), aḍḍito (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Bāhā paggayha kandanto, vihārā upanikkhamiṃ <note>nūpanikkhamiṃ (sabbattha), dupanikkhamiṃ (?)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§407.</p>

```
‘‘Satthaṃ vā āharissāmi, ko attho jīvitena me;
```

```
Kathaṃ hi sikkhaṃ paccakkhaṃ, kālaṃ kubbetha mādiso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§408.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0223" /> khuramādāya, mañcakamhi upāvisiṃ;
```

```
Parinīto khuro āsi, dhamaniṃ chettumattano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§409.</p>

```
‘‘Tato me manasīkāro, yoniso udapajjatha;
```

```
Ādīnavo pāturahu, nibbidā samatiṭṭhatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§410.</p>

```
‘‘Tato cittaṃ vimucci me, passa dhammasudhammataṃ;
```

```
Tisso <pb ed="T" n="0.0330" /> vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsana’’nti.
```

… Sappadāso thero….

#### 7.Kātiyānattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§411.</p>

```
‘‘Uṭṭhehi nisīda kātiyāna, mā niddābahulo ahu jāgarassu;
```

```
Mā taṃ alasaṃ pamattabandhu, kūṭeneva jinātu maccurājā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§412.</p>

```
‘‘Seyyathāpi <note>sayathāpi (sī. pī.)</note> mahāsamuddavego, evaṃ jātijarātivattate taṃ;
```

```
So karohi sudīpamattano tvaṃ, na hi tāṇaṃ tava vijjateva aññaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§413.</p>

```
‘‘Satthā hi vijesi maggametaṃ, saṅgā jātijarābhayā atītaṃ;
```

```
Pubbāpararattamappamatto, anuyuñjassu daḷhaṃ karohi yogaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§414.</p>

```
‘‘Purimāni <pb ed="M" n="0.0286" /> pamuñca bandhanāni, saṅghāṭikhuramuṇḍabhikkhabhojī;
```

```
Mā khiḍḍāratiñca mā niddaṃ, anuyuñjittha jhāya kātiyāna.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§415.</p>

```
‘‘Jhāyāhi <pb ed="P" n="0.0045" /> jināhi kātiyāna, yogakkhemapathesu <pb ed="T" n="0.0331" /> kovidosi;
```

```
Pappuyya anuttaraṃ visuddhiṃ, parinibbāhisi vārināva joti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§416.</p>

```
‘‘Pajjotakaro parittaraṃso, vātena vinamyate latāva;
```

```
Evampi tuvaṃ anādiyāno, māraṃ indasagotta niddhunāhi;
```

```
So vedayitāsu vītarāgo, kālaṃ kaṅkha idheva sītibhūto’’ti.
```

… Kātiyāno thero….

#### 8. Migajālattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§417.</p>

```
‘‘Sudesito cakkhumatā, buddhenādiccabandhunā;
```

```
Sabbasaṃyojanātīto, sabbavaṭṭavināsano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§418.</p>

```
‘‘Niyyāniko uttaraṇo, taṇhāmūlavisosano;
```

```
Visamūlaṃ āghātanaṃ, chetvā pāpeti nibbutiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§419.</p>

```
‘‘Aññāṇamūlabhedāya<pb ed="V" n="0.0224" />, kammayantavighāṭano;
```

```
Viññāṇānaṃ pariggahe, ñāṇavajiranipātano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§420.</p>

```
‘‘Vedanānaṃ viññāpano, upādānappamocano;
```

```
Bhavaṃ aṅgārakāsuṃva, ñāṇena anupassano <note>anupassako (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§421.</p>

```
‘‘Mahāraso sugambhīro, jarāmaccunivāraṇo;
```

```
Ariyo <pb ed="T" n="0.0332" /> aṭṭhaṅgiko maggo, dukkhūpasamano sivo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§422.</p>

```
‘‘Kammaṃ kammanti ñatvāna, vipākañca vipākato;
```

```
Paṭiccuppannadhammānaṃ, yathāvālokadassano;
```

```
Mahākhemaṅgamo santo, pariyosānabhaddako’’ti.
```

… Migajālo thero….

#### 9. Purohitaputtajentattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§423.</p>

```
‘‘Jātimadena <pb ed="M" n="0.0287" /> mattohaṃ, bhogaissariyena ca;
```

```
Saṇṭhānavaṇṇarūpena, madamatto acārihaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§424.</p>

```
‘‘Nāttano samakaṃ kañci, atirekaṃ ca maññisaṃ;
```

```
Atimānahato bālo, patthaddho ussitaddhajo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§425.</p>

```
‘‘Mātaraṃ pitarañcāpi, aññepi garusammate;
```

```
Na kañci abhivādesiṃ, mānatthaddho anādaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§426.</p>

```
‘‘Disvā vināyakaṃ aggaṃ, sārathīnaṃ varuttamaṃ;
```

```
Tapantamiva ādiccaṃ, bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§427.</p>

```
‘‘Mānaṃ madañca chaḍḍetvā, vippasannena cetasā;
```

```
Sirasā abhivādesiṃ, sabbasattānamuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§428.</p>

```
‘‘Atimāno <pb ed="P" n="0.0046" /> ca omāno, pahīnā susamūhatā;
```

```
Asmimāno samucchinno, sabbe mānavidhā hatā’’ti.
```

… Jento purohitaputto thero….

#### 10. Sumanattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§429.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā <pb ed="T" n="0.0333" /> navo pabbajito, jātiyā sattavassiko;
```

```
Iddhiyā abhibhotvāna, pannagindaṃ mahiddhikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§430.</p>

```
‘‘Upajjhāyassa <pb ed="V" n="0.0225" /> udakaṃ, anotattā mahāsarā;
```

```
Āharāmi tato disvā, maṃ satthā etadabravi’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§431.</p>

```
‘‘Sāriputta imaṃ passa, āgacchantaṃ kumārakaṃ;
```

```
Udakakumbhamādāya, ajjhattaṃ susamāhitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§432.</p>

```
‘‘Pāsādikena vattena, kalyāṇairiyāpatho;
```

```
Sāmaṇeronuruddhassa, iddhiyā ca visārado.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§433.</p>

```
‘‘Ājānīyena ājañño, sādhunā sādhukārito;
```

```
Vinīto anuruddhena, katakiccena sikkhito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§434.</p>

```
‘‘So patvā paramaṃ santiṃ, sacchikatvā akuppataṃ;
```

```
Sāmaṇero sa sumano, mā maṃ jaññāti icchatī’’ti.
```

… Sumano thero….

#### 11. Nhātakamunittheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§435.</p>

```
‘‘Vātarogābhinīto <pb ed="M" n="0.0288" /> tvaṃ, viharaṃ kānane vane;
```

```
Paviddhagocare lūkhe, kathaṃ bhikkhu karissasi’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§436.</p>

```
‘‘Pītisukhena vipulena, pharitvāna samussayaṃ;
```

```
Lūkhampi abhisambhonto, viharissāmi kānane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§437.</p>

```
‘‘Bhāvento satta bojjhaṅge, indriyāni balāni ca;
```

```
Jhānasokhummasampanno <note>jhānasukhumasampanno (syā. ka.)</note>, viharissaṃ anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§438.</p>

```
‘‘Vippamuttaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0334" /> kilesehi, suddhacittaṃ anāvilaṃ;
```

```
Abhiṇhaṃ paccavekkhanto, viharissaṃ anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§439.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjhattañca bahiddhā ca, ye me vijjiṃsu āsavā;
```

```
Sabbe asesā ucchinnā, na ca uppajjare puna.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§440.</p>

```
‘‘Pañcakkhandhā pariññātā, tiṭṭhanti chinnamūlakā;
```

```
Dukkhakkhayo anuppatto, natthi dāni punabbhavo’’ti.
```

… Nhātakamunitthero….

#### 12. Brahmadattattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§441.</p>

```
‘‘Akkodhassa kuto kodho, dantassa samajīvino;
```

```
Sammadaññā vimuttassa, upasantassa tādino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§442.</p>

```
‘‘Tasseva <pb ed="V" n="0.0226" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0047" /> tena pāpiyo, yo kuddhaṃ paṭikujjhati;
```

```
Kuddhaṃ appaṭikujjhanto, saṅgāmaṃ jeti dujjayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§443.</p>

```
<note>saṃ. ni. 1.188, 250</note> ‘‘Ubhinnamatthaṃ carati, attano ca parassa ca;
```

```
Paraṃ saṅkupitaṃ ñatvā, yo sato upasammati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§444.</p>

```
<note>saṃ. ni. 1.188, 250</note> ‘‘Ubhinnaṃ tikicchantaṃ taṃ, attano ca parassa ca;
```

```
Janā maññanti bāloti, ye dhammassa akovidā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§445.</p>

```
‘‘Uppajje te sace kodho, āvajja kakacūpamaṃ;
```

```
Uppajje ce rase taṇhā, puttamaṃsūpamaṃ sara.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§446.</p>

```
‘‘Sace dhāvati cittaṃ te, kāmesu ca bhavesu ca;
```

```
Khippaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0335" /> niggaṇha satiyā, kiṭṭhādaṃ viya duppasu’’nti;
```

… Brahmadatto thero….

#### 13. Sirimaṇḍattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§447.</p>

```
<note>udā. 45; cūḷava. 385; pari. 339</note> ‘‘Channamativassati<pb ed="M" n="0.0289" />, vivaṭaṃ nātivassati;
```

```
Tasmā channaṃ vivaretha, evaṃ taṃ nātivassati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§448.</p>

```
<note>saṃ. ni. 1.66; netti. 18</note> ‘‘Maccunābbhahato loko, jarāya parivārito;
```

```
Taṇhāsallena otiṇṇo, icchādhūpāyito sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§449.</p>

```
‘‘Maccunābbhahato loko, parikkhitto jarāya ca;
```

```
Haññati niccamattāṇo, pattadaṇḍova takkaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§450.</p>

```
‘‘Āgacchantaggikhandhāva, maccu byādhi jarā tayo;
```

```
Paccuggantuṃ balaṃ natthi, javo natthi palāyituṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§451.</p>

```
‘‘Amoghaṃ divasaṃ kayirā, appena bahukena vā;
```

```
Yaṃ yaṃ vijahate <note>virahate (sī. pī.), vivahate (syā.)</note> rattiṃ, tadūnaṃ tassa jīvitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§452.</p>

```
‘‘Carato tiṭṭhato vāpi, āsīnasayanassa vā;
```

```
Upeti carimā ratti, na te kālo pamajjitu’’nti.
```

… Sirimaṇḍo <note>sirimando (sī.)</note> thero….

#### 14. Sabbakāmittheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§453.</p>

```
‘‘Dvipādakoyaṃ asuci, duggandho parihīrati <note>pariharati (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Nānākuṇapaparipūro, vissavanto tato tato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§454.</p>

```
‘‘Migaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0227" /> nilīnaṃ kūṭena, baḷiseneva ambujaṃ;
```

```
Vānaraṃ viya lepena, bādhayanti puthujjanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§455.</p>

```
‘‘Rūpā <pb ed="T" n="0.0336" /> saddā rasā gandhā, phoṭṭhabbā ca manoramā;
```

```
Pañca kāmaguṇā ete, itthirūpasmi dissare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§456.</p>

```
‘‘Ye <pb ed="P" n="0.0048" /> etā upasevanti, rattacittā puthujjanā;
```

```
Vaḍḍhenti kaṭasiṃ ghoraṃ, ācinanti punabbhavaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§457.</p>

```
‘‘Yo cetā parivajjeti, sappasseva padā siro;
```

```
Somaṃ visattikaṃ loke, sato samativattati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§458.</p>

```
‘‘Kāmesvādīnavaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0290" /> disvā, nekkhammaṃ daṭṭhu khemato;
```

```
Nissaṭo sabbakāmehi, patto me āsavakkhayo’’ti.
```

… Sabbakāmitthero….

<trailer rend="centre">Chakkanipāto niṭṭhito.</trailer>

Tatruddānaṃ –

```
Uruveḷakassapo ca, thero tekicchakāri ca;
```

```
Mahānāgo ca kullo ca, mālukyo <note>māluto (sī. ka.), māluṅkyo (syā.)</note> sappadāsako.
```

```
Kātiyāno migajālo, jento sumanasavhayo;
```

```
Nhātamuni brahmadatto, sirimaṇḍo sabbakāmī ca;
```

```
Gāthāyo caturāsīti, therā cettha catuddasāti.
```

### 7. Sattakanipāto

#### 1. Sundarasamuddattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§459.</p>

```
‘‘Alaṅkatā <pb ed="T" n="0.0337" /><pb ed="M" n="0.0291" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0228" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0049" /> suvasanā, māladhārī <note>mālābhārī (sī.), mālabhārī (syā.)</note> vibhūsitā;
```

```
Alattakakatāpādā, pādukāruyha vesikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§460.</p>

```
‘‘Pādukā oruhitvāna, purato pañjalīkatā;
```

```
Sā maṃ saṇhena mudunā, mhitapubbaṃ <note>mihitapubbaṃ (sī.)</note> abhāsatha’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§461.</p>

```
‘‘Yuvāsi tvaṃ pabbajito, tiṭṭhāhi mama sāsane;
```

```
Bhuñja mānusake kāme, ahaṃ vittaṃ dadāmi te;
```

```
Saccaṃ te paṭijānāmi, aggiṃ vā te harāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§462.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā jiṇṇā bhavissāma, ubho daṇḍaparāyanā;
```

```
Ubhopi pabbajissāma, ubhayattha kaṭaggaho’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§463.</p>

```
‘‘Tañca disvāna yācantiṃ, vesikaṃ pañjalīkataṃ;
```

```
Alaṅkataṃ suvasanaṃ, maccupāsaṃva oḍḍitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§464.</p>

```
‘‘Tato me manasīkāro…pe… nibbidā samatiṭṭhatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§465.</p>

```
‘‘Tato cittaṃ vimucci me…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsana’’nti.
```

… Sundarasamuddo thero….

#### 2. Lakuṇḍakabhaddiyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§466.</p>

```
Pare ambāṭakārāme, vanasaṇḍamhi bhaddiyo;
```

```
Samūlaṃ taṇhamabbuyha, tattha bhaddova jhāyati <note>bhaddo’dhijhāyāyati (sī.), bhaddo jhiyāyati (syā. sī. aṭṭha.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§467.</p>

```
‘‘Ramanteke mudiṅgehi <note>mutiṅgehi (sī. aṭṭha.)</note>, vīṇāhi paṇavehi ca;
```

```
Ahañca <pb ed="T" n="0.0338" /> rukkhamūlasmiṃ, rato buddhassa sāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§468.</p>

```
‘‘Buddho ce <note>buddho ca (sabbattha)</note> me varaṃ dajjā, so ca labbhetha me varo;
```

```
Gaṇhehaṃ sabbalokassa, niccaṃ kāyagataṃ satiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§469.</p>

```
‘‘Ye <pb ed="M" n="0.0292" /> maṃ rūpena pāmiṃsu, ye ca ghosena anvagū;
```

```
Chandarāgavasūpetā, na maṃ jānanti te janā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§470.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjhattañca <pb ed="V" n="0.0229" /> na jānāti, bahiddhā ca na passati;
```

```
Samantāvaraṇo bālo, sa ve ghosena vuyhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§471.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjhattañca na jānāti, bahiddhā ca vipassati;
```

```
Bahiddhā phaladassāvī, sopi ghosena vuyhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§472.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjhattañca pajānāti, bahiddhā ca vipassati;
```

```
Anāvaraṇadassāvī, na so ghosena vuyhatī’’ti.
```

… Lakuṇḍakabhaddiyo thero….

#### 3. Bhaddattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§473.</p>

```
‘‘Ekaputto <pb ed="P" n="0.0050" /> ahaṃ āsiṃ, piyo mātu piyo pitu;
```

```
Bahūhi vatacariyāhi, laddho āyācanāhi ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§474.</p>

```
‘‘Te ca maṃ anukampāya, atthakāmā hitesino;
```

```
Ubho pitā ca mātā ca, buddhassa upanāmayuṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§475.</p>

```
‘‘Kicchā laddho ayaṃ putto, sukhumālo sukhedhito;
```

```
Imaṃ dadāma te nātha, jinassa paricārakaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§476.</p>

```
‘‘Satthā ca maṃ paṭiggayha, ānandaṃ etadabravi;
```

```
‘Pabbājehi imaṃ khippaṃ, hessatyājāniyo ayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§477.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbājetvāna <pb ed="T" n="0.0339" /> maṃ satthā, vihāraṃ pāvisī jino;
```

```
Anoggatasmiṃ sūriyasmiṃ, tato cittaṃ vimucci me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§478.</p>

```
‘‘Tato satthā nirākatvā, paṭisallānavuṭṭhito;
```

```
‘Ehi bhaddā’ti maṃ āha, sā me āsūpasampadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§479.</p>

```
‘‘Jātiyā sattavassena, laddhā me upasampadā;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, aho dhammasudhammatā’’ti.
```

… Bhaddo thero….

#### 4. Sopākattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§480.</p>

```
‘‘Disvā <pb ed="M" n="0.0293" /> pāsādachāyāyaṃ, caṅkamantaṃ naruttamaṃ;
```

```
Tattha naṃ upasaṅkamma, vandissaṃ <note>vandisaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> purisuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§481.</p>

```
‘‘Ekaṃsaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0230" /> cīvaraṃ katvā, saṃharitvāna pāṇayo;
```

```
Anucaṅkamissaṃ virajaṃ, sabbasattānamuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§482.</p>

```
‘‘Tato pañhe apucchi maṃ, pañhānaṃ kovido vidū;
```

```
Acchambhī ca abhīto ca, byākāsiṃ satthuno ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§483.</p>

```
‘‘Vissajjitesu pañhesu, anumodi tathāgato;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghaṃ viloketvā, imamatthaṃ abhāsatha’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§484.</p>

```
‘‘Lābhā aṅgānaṃ magadhānaṃ, yesāyaṃ paribhuñjati;
```

```
Cīvaraṃ piṇḍapātañca, paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ;
```

```
Paccuṭṭhānañca sāmīciṃ, tesaṃ lābhā’’ti cābravi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§485.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjatagge maṃ sopāka, dassanāyopasaṅkama;
```

```
Esā <pb ed="T" n="0.0340" /> ceva te sopāka, bhavatu upasampadā’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§486.</p>

```
‘‘Jātiyā sattavassohaṃ, laddhāna upasampadaṃ;
```

```
Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ, aho dhammasudhammatā’’ti.
```

… Sopāko thero….

#### 5. Sarabhaṅgattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§487.</p>

```
‘‘Sare hatthehi bhañjitvā, katvāna kuṭimacchisaṃ;
```

```
Tena me sarabhaṅgoti, nāmaṃ sammutiyā ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§488.</p>

```
‘‘Na <pb ed="P" n="0.0051" /> mayhaṃ kappate ajja, sare hatthehi bhañjituṃ;
```

```
Sikkhāpadā no paññattā, gotamena yasassinā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§489.</p>

```
‘‘Sakalaṃ samattaṃ rogaṃ, sarabhaṅgo nāddasaṃ pubbe;
```

```
Soyaṃ rogo diṭṭho, vacanakarenātidevassa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§490.</p>

```
‘‘Yeneva maggena gato vipassī, yeneva maggena sikhī ca vessabhū;
```

```
Kakusandhakoṇāgamano ca kassapo, tenañjasena agamāsi gotamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§491.</p>

```
‘‘Vītataṇhā <pb ed="M" n="0.0294" /> anādānā, satta buddhā khayogadhā;
```

```
Yehāyaṃ desito dhammo, dhammabhūtehi tādibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§492.</p>

```
‘‘Cattāri ariyasaccāni, anukampāya pāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Dukkhaṃ samudayo maggo, nirodho dukkhasaṅkhayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§493.</p>

```
‘‘Yasmiṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0231" /> nivattate <note>yasmiṃ na nibbattate (ka.)</note> dukkhaṃ, saṃsārasmiṃ anantakaṃ;
```

```
Bhedā <pb ed="T" n="0.0341" /> imassa kāyassa, jīvitassa ca saṅkhayā;
```

```
Añño punabbhavo natthi, suvimuttomhi sabbadhī’’ti.
```

… Sarabhaṅgo thero….

<trailer rend="centre">Sattakanipāto niṭṭhito.</trailer>

Tatruddānaṃ –

```
Sundarasamuddo thero, thero lakuṇḍabhaddiyo;
```

```
Bhaddo thero ca sopāko, sarabhaṅgo mahāisi;
```

```
Sattake pañcakā therā, gāthāyo pañcatiṃsatīti.
```

### 8. Aṭṭhakanipāto

#### 1. Mahākaccāyanattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§494.</p>

```
‘‘Kammaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0295" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0232" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0052" /> bahukaṃ na kāraye, parivajjeyya janaṃ na uyyame;
```

```
So ussukko rasānugiddho, atthaṃ riñcati yo sukhādhivāho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§495.</p>

```
‘‘Paṅkoti hi naṃ avedayuṃ, yāyaṃ vandanapūjanā kulesu;
```

```
Sukhumaṃ sallaṃ durubbahaṃ, sakkāro kāpurisena dujjaho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§496.</p>

```
‘‘Na parassupanidhāya, kammaṃ maccassa pāpakaṃ;
```

```
Attanā taṃ na seveyya, kammabandhūhi mātiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§497.</p>

```
‘‘Na pare vacanā coro, na pare vacanā muni;
```

```
Attā ca naṃ yathāvedi <note>yathā vetti (sī.)</note>, devāpi naṃ tathā vidū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§498.</p>

```
‘‘Pare ca na vijānanti, mayamettha yamāmase;
```

```
Ye <pb ed="T" n="0.0342" /> ca tattha vijānanti, tato sammanti medhagā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§499.</p>

```
‘‘Jīvate vāpi sappañño, api vittaparikkhayo;
```

```
Paññāya ca alābhena <note>abhāvena (sī. aṭṭha.)</note>, vittavāpi na jīvati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§500.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbaṃ suṇāti sotena, sabbaṃ passati cakkhunā;
```

```
Na ca diṭṭhaṃ sutaṃ dhīro, sabbaṃ ujjhitumarahati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§501.</p>

```
‘‘Cakkhumāssa yathā andho, sotavā badhiro yathā;
```

```
Paññavāssa yathā mūgo, balavā dubbaloriva;
```

```
Atha atthe samuppanne, sayetha <note>passetha (ka.)</note> matasāyika’’nti.
```

… Mahākaccāyano thero….

#### 2. Sirimittattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§502.</p>

```
‘‘Akkodhanonupanāhī, amāyo rittapesuṇo;
```

```
Sa ve tādisako bhikkhu, evaṃ pecca na socati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§503.</p>

```
‘‘Akkodhanonupanāhī, amāyo rittapesuṇo;
```

```
Guttadvāro sadā bhikkhu, evaṃ pecca na socati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§504.</p>

```
‘‘Akkodhanonupanāhī<pb ed="M" n="0.0296" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0233" />, amāyo rittapesuṇo;
```

```
Kalyāṇasīlo so <note>yo (syā.)</note> bhikkhu, evaṃ pecca na socati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§505.</p>

```
‘‘Akkodhanonupanāhī, amāyo rittapesuṇo;
```

```
Kalyāṇamitto so bhikkhu, evaṃ pecca na socati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§506.</p>

```
‘‘Akkodhanonupanāhī<pb ed="P" n="0.0053" />, amāyo rittapesuṇo;
```

```
Kalyāṇapañño so bhikkhu, evaṃ pecca na socati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§507.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa saddhā tathāgate, acalā suppatiṭṭhitā;
```

```
Sīlañca <pb ed="T" n="0.0343" /> yassa kalyāṇaṃ, ariyakantaṃ pasaṃsitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§508.</p>

```
‘‘Saṅghe pasādo yassatthi, ujubhūtañca dassanaṃ;
```

```
‘Adaliddo’ti taṃ āhu, amoghaṃ tassa jīvitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§509.</p>

```
‘‘Tasmā saddhañca sīlañca, pasādaṃ dhammadassanaṃ;
```

```
Anuyuñjetha medhāvī, saraṃ buddhāna sāsana’’nti.
```

… Sirimitto thero….

#### 3. Mahāpanthakattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§510.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā paṭhamamaddakkhiṃ, satthāramakutobhayaṃ;
```

```
Tato me ahu saṃvego, passitvā purisuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§511.</p>

```
‘‘Siriṃ hatthehi pādehi, yo paṇāmeyya āgataṃ;
```

```
Etādisaṃ so satthāraṃ, ārādhetvā virādhaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§512.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ puttadārañca, dhanadhaññañca chaḍḍayiṃ;
```

```
Kesamassūni chedetvā, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§513.</p>

```
‘‘Sikkhāsājīvasampanno, indriyesu susaṃvuto;
```

```
Namassamāno sambuddhaṃ, vihāsiṃ aparājito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§514.</p>

```
‘‘Tato me paṇidhī āsi, cetaso abhipatthito;
```

```
Na nisīde muhuttampi, taṇhāsalle anūhate.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§515.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa mevaṃ viharato, passa vīriyaparakkamaṃ;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§516.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0297" /> jānāmi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
```

```
Arahā dakkhiṇeyyomhi, vippamutto nirūpadhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§517.</p>

```
‘‘Tato <pb ed="T" n="0.0344" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0234" /> ratyā vivasāne <note>vivasane (sī. syā.)</note>, sūriyassuggamanaṃ pati;
```

```
Sabbaṃ taṇhaṃ visosetvā, pallaṅkena upāvisi’’nti.
```

… Mahāpanthako thero….

<trailer rend="centre">Aṭṭhakanipāto niṭṭhito.</trailer>

Tatruddānaṃ –

```
Mahākaccāyano thero, sirimitto mahāpanthako;
```

```
Ete aṭṭhanipātamhi, gāthāyo catuvīsatīti.
```

### 9. Navakanipāto

#### 1. Bhūtattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§518.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā <pb ed="M" n="0.0298" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0235" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0054" /> dukkhaṃ jarāmaraṇanti paṇḍito, aviddasū yattha sitā puthujjanā;
```

```
Dukkhaṃ pariññāya satova jhāyati, tato ratiṃ paramataraṃ na vindati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§519.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā dukkhassāvahaniṃ visattikaṃ, papañcasaṅghātadukhādhivāhiniṃ;
```

```
Taṇhaṃ pahantvāna satova jhāyati, tato ratiṃ paramataraṃ na vindati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§520.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā sivaṃ dvecaturaṅgagāminaṃ, magguttamaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0345" /> sabbakilesasodhanaṃ;
```

```
Paññāya passitva satova jhāyati, tato ratiṃ paramataraṃ na vindati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§521.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā asokaṃ virajaṃ asaṅkhataṃ, santaṃ padaṃ sabbakilesasodhanaṃ;
```

```
Bhāveti saññojanabandhanacchidaṃ, tato ratiṃ paramataraṃ na vindati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§522.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā nabhe gajjati meghadundubhi, dhārākulā vihagapathe samantato;
```

```
Bhikkhū ca pabbhāragatova jhāyati, tato ratiṃ paramataraṃ na vindati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§523.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā nadīnaṃ kusumākulānaṃ, vicitta-vāneyya-vaṭaṃsakānaṃ;
```

```
Tīre nisinno sumanova jhāyati, tato ratiṃ paramataraṃ na vindati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§524.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā <pb ed="M" n="0.0299" /> nisīthe rahitamhi kānane, deve gaḷantamhi nadanti dāṭhino;
```

```
Bhikkhū ca pabbhāragatova jhāyati, tato ratiṃ paramataraṃ na vindati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§525.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā <pb ed="T" n="0.0346" /> vitakke uparundhiyattano, nagantare nagavivaraṃ samassito;
```

```
Vītaddaro vītakhilova jhāyati, tato ratiṃ paramataraṃ na vindati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§526.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā <pb ed="P" n="0.0055" /> sukhī malakhilasokanāsano, niraggaḷo nibbanatho visallo;
```

```
Sabbāsave byantikatova jhāyati, tato ratiṃ paramataraṃ na vindatī’’ti.
```

… Bhūto thero….

<trailer rend="centre">Navakanipāto niṭṭhito.</trailer>

Tatruddānaṃ –

```
Bhūto tathaddaso thero, eko khaggavisāṇavā;
```

```
Navakamhi nipātamhi, gāthāyopi imā navāti.
```

### 10. Dasakanipāto

#### 1. Kāḷudāyittheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§527.</p>

```
‘‘Aṅgārino <pb ed="M" n="0.0300" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0236" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0056" /> dāni dumā bhadante, phalesino chadanaṃ vippahāya;
```

```
Te accimantova pabhāsayanti, samayo mahāvīra bhāgī rasānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§528.</p>

```
‘‘Dumāni <pb ed="T" n="0.0347" /> phullāni manoramāni, samantato sabbadisā pavanti;
```

```
Pattaṃ pahāya phalamāsasānā <note>phalamāsamāno (ka.)</note>, kālo ito pakkamanāya vīra.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§529.</p>

```
‘‘Nevātisītaṃ na panātiuṇhaṃ, sukhā utu addhaniyā bhadante;
```

```
Passantu taṃ sākiyā koḷiyā ca, pacchāmukhaṃ rohiniyaṃ tarantaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§530.</p>

```
‘‘Āsāya kasate khettaṃ, bījaṃ āsāya vappati;
```

```
Āsāya vāṇijā yanti, samuddaṃ dhanahārakā;
```

```
Yāya āsāya tiṭṭhāmi, sā me āsā samijjhatu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§531.</p>

```
<note>saṃ. ni. 1.198</note> ‘‘Punappunaṃ ceva vapanti bījaṃ, punappunaṃ vassati devarājā;
```

```
Punappunaṃ khettaṃ kasanti kassakā, punappunaṃ dhaññamupeti raṭṭhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§532.</p>

```
<note>saṃ. ni. 1.198</note> ‘‘Punappunaṃ yācanakā caranti, punappunaṃ dānapatī dadanti;
```

```
Punappunaṃ dānapatī daditvā, punappunaṃ saggamupenti ṭhānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§533.</p>

```
‘‘Vīro <pb ed="T" n="0.0348" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0057" /> have sattayugaṃ puneti, yasmiṃ kule jāyati bhūripañño;
```

```
Maññāmahaṃ sakkati devadevo, tayā hi jāto <note>tayābhijāto (sī.)</note> muni saccanāmo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§534.</p>

```
‘‘Suddhodano <pb ed="M" n="0.0301" /> nāma pitā mahesino, buddhassa mātā pana māyanāmā;
```

```
Yā bodhisattaṃ parihariya kucchinā, kāyassa bhedā tidivamhi modati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§535.</p>

```
‘‘Sā gotamī kālakatā ito cutā, dibbehi kāmehi samaṅgibhūtā;
```

```
Sā modati kāmaguṇehi pañcahi, parivāritā devagaṇehi tehi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§536.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhassa puttomhi asayhasāhino, aṅgīrasassappaṭimassa tādino;
```

```
Pitupitā mayhaṃ tuvaṃsi sakka, dhammena me gotama ayyakosī’’ti.
```

… Kāḷudāyī thero….

#### 2. Ekavihāriyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§537.</p>

```
‘‘Purato <pb ed="V" n="0.0237" /> pacchato vāpi, aparo ce na vijjati;
```

```
Atīva phāsu bhavati, ekassa vasato vane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§538.</p>

```
‘‘Handa <pb ed="T" n="0.0349" /> eko gamissāmi, araññaṃ buddhavaṇṇitaṃ;
```

```
Phāsu <note>phāsuṃ (syā. pī.)</note> ekavihārissa, pahitattassa bhikkhuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§539.</p>

```
‘‘Yogī-pītikaraṃ rammaṃ, mattakuñjarasevitaṃ;
```

```
Eko attavasī khippaṃ, pavisissāmi kānanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§540.</p>

```
‘‘Supupphite sītavane, sītale girikandare;
```

```
Gattāni parisiñcitvā, caṅkamissāmi ekako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§541.</p>

```
‘‘Ekākiyo adutiyo, ramaṇīye mahāvane;
```

```
Kadāhaṃ viharissāmi, katakicco anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§542.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ me kattukāmassa, adhippāyo samijjhatu;
```

```
Sādhiyissāmahaṃyeva, nāñño aññassa kārako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§543.</p>

```
‘‘Esa <pb ed="M" n="0.0302" /> bandhāmi sannāhaṃ, pavisissāmi kānanaṃ;
```

```
Na tato nikkhamissāmi, appatto āsavakkhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§544.</p>

```
‘‘Mālute upavāyante, sīte surabhigandhike <note>gandhake (syā. pī. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Avijjaṃ dālayissāmi, nisinno nagamuddhani.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§545.</p>

```
‘‘Vane kusumasañchanne, pabbhāre nūna sītale;
```

```
Vimuttisukhena sukhito, ramissāmi giribbaje.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§546.</p>

```
‘‘Sohaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0058" /> paripuṇṇasaṅkappo, cando pannaraso yathā;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇo, natthi dāni punabbhavo’’ti.
```

… Ekavihāriyo thero….

#### 3. Mahākappinattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§547.</p>

```
‘‘Anāgataṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0350" /> yo paṭikacca <note>paṭigacca (sī.)</note> passati, hitañca atthaṃ ahitañca taṃ dvayaṃ;
```

```
Viddesino tassa hitesino vā, randhaṃ na passanti samekkhamānā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§548.</p>

```
<note>paṭi. ma. 1.160 paṭisambhidāmagge</note> ‘‘Ānāpānasatī yassa, paripuṇṇā subhāvitā;
```

```
Anupubbaṃ paricitā, yathā buddhena desitā;
```

```
Somaṃ lokaṃ pabhāseti, abbhā muttova candimā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§549.</p>

```
‘‘Odātaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0238" /> vata me cittaṃ, appamāṇaṃ subhāvitaṃ;
```

```
Nibbiddhaṃ paggahītañca, sabbā obhāsate disā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§550.</p>

```
‘‘Jīvate vāpi sappañño, api vittaparikkhayo;
```

```
Paññāya ca alābhena, vittavāpi na jīvati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§551.</p>

```
‘‘Paññā sutavinicchinī, paññā kittisilokavaddhanī;
```

```
Paññāsahito naro idha, api dukkhesu sukhāni vindati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§552.</p>

```
‘‘Nāyaṃ ajjatano dhammo, nacchero napi abbhuto;
```

```
Yattha jāyetha mīyetha, tattha kiṃ viya abbhutaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§553.</p>

```
‘‘Anantaraṃ hi jātassa, jīvitā maraṇaṃ dhuvaṃ;
```

```
Jātā jātā marantīdha, evaṃdhammā hi pāṇino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§554.</p>

```
‘‘Na <pb ed="M" n="0.0303" /> hetadatthāya matassa hoti, yaṃ jīvitatthaṃ paraporisānaṃ;
```

```
Matamhi ruṇṇaṃ na yaso na lokyaṃ, na <pb ed="T" n="0.0351" /> vaṇṇitaṃ samaṇabrāhmaṇehi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§555.</p>

```
‘‘Cakkhuṃ sarīraṃ upahanti tena <note>upahanti ruṇṇaṃ (sī.), upahanti roṇṇaṃ (syā. pī.)</note>, nihīyati vaṇṇabalaṃ matī ca;
```

```
Ānandino tassa disā bhavanti, hitesino nāssa sukhī bhavanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§556.</p>

```
‘‘Tasmā hi iccheyya kule vasante, medhāvino ceva bahussute ca;
```

```
Yesaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0059" /> hi paññāvibhavena kiccaṃ, taranti nāvāya nadiṃva puṇṇa’’nti.
```

… Mahākappino thero….

#### 4. Cūḷapanthakattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§557.</p>

```
‘‘Dandhā mayhaṃ gatī āsi, paribhūto pure ahaṃ;
```

```
Bhātā ca maṃ paṇāmesi, ‘gaccha dāni tuvaṃ gharaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§558.</p>

```
‘‘Sohaṃ paṇāmito santo <note>bhātā (aṭṭha.)</note>, saṅghārāmassa koṭṭhake;
```

```
Dummano tattha aṭṭhāsiṃ, sāsanasmiṃ apekkhavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§559.</p>

```
‘‘Bhagavā tattha āgacchi <note>āgañchi (sī. pī.)</note>, sīsaṃ mayhaṃ parāmasi;
```

```
Bāhāya maṃ gahetvāna, saṅghārāmaṃ pavesayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§560.</p>

```
‘‘Anukampāya me satthā, pādāsi pādapuñchaniṃ;
```

```
‘Etaṃ suddhaṃ adhiṭṭhehi, ekamantaṃ svadhiṭṭhitaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§561.</p>

```
‘‘Tassāhaṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, vihāsiṃ sāsane rato;
```

```
Samādhiṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0352" /> paṭipādesiṃ, uttamatthassa pattiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§562.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0239" /> jānāmi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§563.</p>

```
‘‘Sahassakkhattumattānaṃ<pb ed="M" n="0.0304" />, nimminitvāna panthako;
```

```
Nisīdambavane ramme, yāva kālappavedanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§564.</p>

```
‘‘Tato me satthā pāhesi, dūtaṃ kālappavedakaṃ;
```

```
Paveditamhi kālamhi, vehāsādupasaṅkamiṃ <note>vehāsānupasaṅkamiṃ (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§565.</p>

```
‘‘Vanditvā satthuno pāde, ekamantaṃ nisīdahaṃ;
```

```
Nisinnaṃ maṃ viditvāna, atha satthā paṭiggahi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§566.</p>

```
‘‘Āyāgo sabbalokassa, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Puññakkhettaṃ manussānaṃ, paṭigaṇhittha dakkhiṇa’’nti.
```

… Cūḷapanthako thero….

#### 5. Kappattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§567.</p>

```
‘‘Nānākulamalasampuṇṇo, mahāukkārasambhavo;
```

```
Candanikaṃva paripakkaṃ, mahāgaṇḍo mahāvaṇo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§568.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbaruhirasampuṇṇo, gūthakūpena gāḷhito <note>gūthakūpe nigāḷhito (syā. pī. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Āpopaggharaṇo kāyo, sadā sandati pūtikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§569.</p>

```
‘‘Saṭṭhikaṇḍarasambandho<pb ed="P" n="0.0060" />, maṃsalepanalepito;
```

```
Cammakañcukasannaddho, pūtikāyo niratthako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§570.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhisaṅghātaghaṭito, nhārusuttanibandhano;
```

```
Nekesaṃ saṃgatībhāvā, kappeti iriyāpathaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§571.</p>

```
‘‘Dhuvappayāto <pb ed="T" n="0.0353" /> maraṇāya, maccurājassa santike;
```

```
Idheva chaḍḍayitvāna, yenakāmaṅgamo naro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§572.</p>

```
‘‘Avijjāya nivuto kāyo, catuganthena ganthito;
```

```
Oghasaṃsīdano kāyo, anusayajālamotthato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§573.</p>

```
‘‘Pañcanīvaraṇe yutto, vitakkena samappito;
```

```
Taṇhāmūlenānugato, mohacchādanachādito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§574.</p>

```
‘‘Evāyaṃ vattate kāyo, kammayantena yantito;
```

```
Sampatti ca vipatyantā, nānābhāvo vipajjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§575.</p>

```
‘‘Yemaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0305" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0240" /> kāyaṃ mamāyanti, andhabālā puthujjanā;
```

```
Vaḍḍhenti kaṭasiṃ ghoraṃ, ādiyanti punabbhavaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§576.</p>

```
‘‘Yemaṃ kāyaṃ vivajjenti, gūthalittaṃva pannagaṃ;
```

```
Bhavamūlaṃ vamitvāna, parinibbissantināsavā’’ti <note>parinibbantunāsavā (sī.)</note>.
```

… Kappo thero….

#### 6. Vaṅgantaputtaupasenattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§577.</p>

```
‘‘Vivittaṃ appanigghosaṃ, vāḷamiganisevitaṃ;
```

```
Seve senāsanaṃ bhikkhu, paṭisallānakāraṇā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§578.</p>

```
‘‘Saṅkārapuñjā āhatvā <note>āhitvā (ka.)</note>, susānā rathiyāhi ca;
```

```
Tato saṅghāṭikaṃ katvā, lūkhaṃ dhāreyya cīvaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§579.</p>

```
‘‘Nīcaṃ manaṃ karitvāna, sapadānaṃ kulā kulaṃ;
```

```
Piṇḍikāya care bhikkhu, guttadvāro susaṃvuto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§580.</p>

```
‘‘Lūkhenapi vā <note>lūkhenapi ca (bahūsu)</note> santusse, nāññaṃ patthe rasaṃ bahuṃ;
```

```
Rasesu <pb ed="T" n="0.0354" /> anugiddhassa, jhāne na ramatī mano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§581.</p>

```
‘‘Appiccho ceva santuṭṭho, pavivitto vase muni;
```

```
Asaṃsaṭṭho gahaṭṭhehi, anāgārehi cūbhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§582.</p>

```
‘‘Yathā jaḷo va mūgo va, attānaṃ dassaye tathā;
```

```
Nātivelaṃ sambhāseyya, saṅghamajjhamhi paṇḍito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§583.</p>

```
‘‘Na so upavade kañci, upaghātaṃ vivajjaye;
```

```
Saṃvuto pātimokkhasmiṃ, mattaññū cassa bhojane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§584.</p>

```
‘‘Suggahītanimittassa, cittassuppādakovido;
```

```
Samaṃ anuyuñjeyya, kālena ca vipassanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§585.</p>

```
‘‘Vīriyasātaccasampanno<pb ed="P" n="0.0061" />, yuttayogo sadā siyā;
```

```
Na ca appatvā dukkhantaṃ, vissāsaṃ eyya paṇḍito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§586.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ viharamānassa, suddhikāmassa bhikkhuno;
```

```
Khīyanti āsavā sabbe, nibbutiñcādhigacchatī’’ti.
```

… Upaseno vaṅgantaputto thero….

#### 7. (Apara)-gotamattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§587.</p>

```
‘‘Vijāneyya <pb ed="M" n="0.0306" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0241" /> sakaṃ atthaṃ, avalokeyyātha pāvacanaṃ;
```

```
Yañcettha assa patirūpaṃ, sāmaññaṃ ajjhupagatassa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§588.</p>

```
‘‘Mittaṃ idha ca kalyāṇaṃ, sikkhā vipulaṃ samādānaṃ;
```

```
Sussūsā ca garūnaṃ, etaṃ samaṇassa patirūpaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§589.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhesu sagāravatā, dhamme apaciti yathābhūtaṃ;
```

```
Saṅghe <pb ed="T" n="0.0355" /> ca cittikāro, etaṃ samaṇassa patirūpaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§590.</p>

```
‘‘Ācāragocare yutto, ājīvo sodhito agārayho;
```

```
Cittassa ca saṇṭhapanaṃ, etaṃ samaṇassa patirūpaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§591.</p>

```
‘‘Cārittaṃ atha vārittaṃ, iriyāpathiyaṃ pasādaniyaṃ;
```

```
Adhicitte ca āyogo, etaṃ samaṇassa patirūpaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§592.</p>

```
‘‘Āraññakāni senāsanāni, pantāni appasaddāni;
```

```
Bhajitabbāni muninā, etaṃ samaṇassa patirūpaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§593.</p>

```
‘‘Sīlañca bāhusaccañca, dhammānaṃ pavicayo yathābhūtaṃ;
```

```
Saccānaṃ abhisamayo, etaṃ samaṇassa patirūpaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§594.</p>

```
‘‘Bhāveyya ca aniccanti, anattasaññaṃ asubhasaññañca;
```

```
Lokamhi ca anabhiratiṃ, etaṃ samaṇassa patirūpaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§595.</p>

```
‘‘Bhāveyya ca bojjhaṅge, iddhipādāni indriyāni balāni;
```

```
Aṭṭhaṅgamaggamariyaṃ, etaṃ samaṇassa patirūpaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§596.</p>

```
‘‘Taṇhaṃ pajaheyya muni, samūlake āsave padāleyya;
```

```
Vihareyya vippamutto, etaṃ samaṇassa patirūpa’’nti.
```

… Gotamo thero….

<trailer rend="centre">Dasakanipāto niṭṭhito.</trailer>

Tatruddānaṃ –

```
Kāḷudāyī ca so thero, ekavihārī ca kappino;
```

```
Cūḷapanthako kappo ca, upaseno ca gotamo;
```

```
Sattime dasake therā, gāthāyo cettha sattatīti.
```

### 11. Ekādasanipāto

#### 1. Saṃkiccattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§597.</p>

```
‘‘Kiṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0356" /><pb ed="M" n="0.0307" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0242" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0062" /> tavattho vane tāta, ujjuhānova pāvuse;
```

```
Verambhā ramaṇīyā te, paviveko hi jhāyinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§598.</p>

```
‘‘Yathā abbhāni verambho, vāto nudati pāvuse;
```

```
Saññā me abhikiranti, vivekapaṭisaññutā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§599.</p>

```
‘‘Apaṇḍaro aṇḍasambhavo, sīvathikāya niketacāriko;
```

```
Uppādayateva me satiṃ, sandehasmiṃ virāganissitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§600.</p>

```
‘‘Yañca aññe na rakkhanti, yo ca aññe na rakkhati;
```

```
Sa ve bhikkhu sukhaṃ seti, kāmesu anapekkhavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§601.</p>

```
‘‘Acchodikā puthusilā, gonaṅgulamigāyutā;
```

```
Ambusevālasañchannā, te selā ramayanti maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§602.</p>

```
‘‘Vasitaṃ me araññesu, kandarāsu guhāsu ca;
```

```
Senāsanesu pantesu, vāḷamiganisevite.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§603.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ime haññantu vajjhantu, dukkhaṃ pappontu pāṇino’;
```

```
Saṅkappaṃ nābhijānāmi, anariyaṃ dosasaṃhitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§604.</p>

```
‘‘Pariciṇṇo mayā satthā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ;
```

```
Ohito garuko bhāro, bhavanetti samūhatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§605.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa catthāya <note>yassatthāya (sī.)</note> pabbajito, agārasmānagāriyaṃ;
```

```
So me attho anuppatto, sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§606.</p>

```
‘‘Nābhinandāmi <pb ed="T" n="0.0357" /> maraṇaṃ, nābhinandāmi jīvitaṃ;
```

```
Kālañca paṭikaṅkhāmi, nibbisaṃ bhatako yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§607.</p>

```
‘‘Nābhinandāmi <pb ed="M" n="0.0308" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0243" /> maraṇaṃ, nābhinandāmi jīvitaṃ;
```

```
Kālañca paṭikaṅkhāmi, sampajāno patissato’’ti.
```

… Saṃkicco thero….

<trailer rend="centre">Ekādasanipāto niṭṭhito.</trailer>

Tatruddānaṃ –

```
Saṃkiccathero ekova, katakicco anāsavo;
```

```
Ekādasanipātamhi, gāthā ekādaseva cāti.
```

### 12. Dvādasakanipāto

#### 1. Sīlavattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§608.</p>

```
‘‘Sīlamevidha <pb ed="M" n="0.0309" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0244" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0063" /> sikkhetha, asmiṃ loke susikkhitaṃ;
```

```
Sīlaṃ hi sabbasampattiṃ, upanāmeti sevitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§609.</p>

```
‘‘Sīlaṃ rakkheyya medhāvī, patthayāno tayo sukhe;
```

```
Pasaṃsaṃ vittilābhañca, pecca sagge pamodanaṃ <note>pecca sagge ca modanaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§610.</p>

```
‘‘Sīlavā hi bahū mitte, saññamenādhigacchati;
```

```
Dussīlo pana mittehi, dhaṃsate pāpamācaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§611.</p>

```
‘‘Avaṇṇañca akittiñca, dussīlo labhate naro;
```

```
Vaṇṇaṃ kittiṃ pasaṃsañca, sadā labhati sīlavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§612.</p>

```
‘‘Ādi <pb ed="T" n="0.0358" /> sīlaṃ patiṭṭhā ca, kalyāṇānañca mātukaṃ;
```

```
Pamukhaṃ sabbadhammānaṃ, tasmā sīlaṃ visodhaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§613.</p>

```
‘‘Velā ca saṃvaraṃ sīlaṃ <note>saṃvaro sīlaṃ (sī.), saṃvarasīlaṃ (sī. aṭṭha.)</note>, cittassa abhihāsanaṃ;
```

```
Titthañca sabbabuddhānaṃ, tasmā sīlaṃ visodhaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§614.</p>

```
‘‘Sīlaṃ balaṃ appaṭimaṃ, sīlaṃ āvudhamuttamaṃ;
```

```
Sīlamābharaṇaṃ seṭṭhaṃ, sīlaṃ kavacamabbhutaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§615.</p>

```
‘‘Sīlaṃ setu mahesakkho, sīlaṃ gandho anuttaro;
```

```
Sīlaṃ vilepanaṃ seṭṭhaṃ, yena vāti disodisaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§616.</p>

```
‘‘Sīlaṃ sambalamevaggaṃ, sīlaṃ pātheyyamuttamaṃ;
```

```
Sīlaṃ seṭṭho ativāho, yena yāti disodisaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§617.</p>

```
‘‘Idheva nindaṃ labhati, peccāpāye ca dummano;
```

```
Sabbattha dummano bālo, sīlesu asamāhito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§618.</p>

```
‘‘Idheva kittiṃ labhati, pecca sagge ca summano;
```

```
Sabbattha sumano dhīro, sīlesu susamāhito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§619.</p>

```
‘‘Sīlameva <pb ed="V" n="0.0245" /> idha aggaṃ, paññavā pana uttamo;
```

```
Manussesu ca devesu, sīlapaññāṇato jaya’’nti.
```

… Sīlavo thero….

#### 2. Sunītattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§620.</p>

```
‘‘Nīce <pb ed="M" n="0.0310" /> kulamhi jātohaṃ, daliddo appabhojano;
```

```
Hīnakammaṃ <note>hīnaṃ kammaṃ (syā.)</note> mamaṃ āsi, ahosiṃ pupphachaḍḍako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§621.</p>

```
‘‘Jigucchito <pb ed="T" n="0.0359" /> manussānaṃ, paribhūto ca vambhito;
```

```
Nīcaṃ manaṃ karitvāna, vandissaṃ bahukaṃ janaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§622.</p>

```
‘‘Athaddasāsiṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0064" /> sambuddhaṃ, bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhataṃ;
```

```
Pavisantaṃ mahāvīraṃ, magadhānaṃ puruttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§623.</p>

```
‘‘Nikkhipitvāna byābhaṅgiṃ, vandituṃ upasaṅkamiṃ;
```

```
Mameva anukampāya, aṭṭhāsi purisuttamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§624.</p>

```
‘‘Vanditvā satthuno pāde, ekamantaṃ ṭhito tadā;
```

```
Pabbajjaṃ ahamāyāciṃ, sabbasattānamuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§625.</p>

```
‘‘Tato kāruṇiko satthā, sabbalokānukampako;
```

```
‘Ehi bhikkhū’ti maṃ āha, sā me āsūpasampadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§626.</p>

```
‘‘Sohaṃ eko araññasmiṃ, viharanto atandito;
```

```
Akāsiṃ satthuvacanaṃ, yathā maṃ ovadī jino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§627.</p>

```
‘‘Rattiyā paṭhamaṃ yāmaṃ, pubbajātimanussariṃ;
```

```
Rattiyā majjhimaṃ yāmaṃ, dibbacakkhuṃ visodhayiṃ <note>dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Rattiyā pacchime yāme, tamokhandhaṃ padālayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§628.</p>

```
‘‘Tato ratyā vivasāne, sūriyassuggamanaṃ pati;
```

```
Indo brahmā ca āgantvā, maṃ namassiṃsu pañjalī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§629.</p>

```
‘‘‘Namo te purisājañña, namo te purisuttama;
```

```
Yassa te āsavā khīṇā, dakkhiṇeyyosi mārisa’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§630.</p>

```
‘‘Tato <pb ed="T" n="0.0360" /> disvāna maṃ satthā, devasaṅghapurakkhataṃ;
```

```
Sitaṃ pātukaritvāna, imamatthaṃ abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§631.</p>

```
<note>su. ni. 660 suttanipātepi</note> ‘‘‘Tapena <pb ed="M" n="0.0311" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0246" /> brahmacariyena, saṃyamena damena ca;
```

```
Etena brāhmaṇo hoti, etaṃ brāhmaṇamuttama’’’nti.
```

… Sunīto thero….

<trailer rend="centre">Dvādasakanipāto niṭṭhito.</trailer>

Tatruddānaṃ –

```
Sīlavā ca sunīto ca, therā dve te mahiddhikā;
```

```
Dvādasamhi nipātamhi, gāthāyo catuvīsatīti.
```

### 13. Terasanipāto

#### 1. Soṇakoḷivisattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§632.</p>

```
‘‘Yāhu <pb ed="M" n="0.0312" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0247" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0065" /> raṭṭhe samukkaṭṭho, rañño aṅgassa paddhagū <note>patthagū (syā.), paṭṭhagū (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Svājja dhammesu ukkaṭṭho, soṇo dukkhassa pāragū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§633.</p>

```
‘‘Pañca chinde pañca jahe, pañca cuttari bhāvaye;
```

```
Pañcasaṅgātigo bhikkhu, oghatiṇṇoti vuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§634.</p>

```
‘‘Unnaḷassa pamattassa, bāhirāsassa <note>bāhirāsayassa (ka.)</note> bhikkhuno;
```

```
Sīlaṃ samādhi paññā ca, pāripūriṃ na gacchati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§635.</p>

```
‘‘Yañhi kiccaṃ apaviddhaṃ <note>tadapaviddhaṃ (sī. syā.)</note>, akiccaṃ pana karīyati;
```

```
Unnaḷānaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0361" /> pamattānaṃ, tesaṃ vaḍḍhanti āsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§636.</p>

```
‘‘Yesañca susamāraddhā, niccaṃ kāyagatā sati;
```

```
Akiccaṃ te na sevanti, kicce sātaccakārino;
```

```
Satānaṃ sampajānānaṃ, atthaṃ gacchanti āsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§637.</p>

```
‘‘Ujumaggamhi akkhāte, gacchatha mā nivattatha;
```

```
Attanā codayattānaṃ, nibbānamabhihāraye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§638.</p>

```
‘‘Accāraddhamhi vīriyamhi, satthā loke anuttaro;
```

```
Vīṇopamaṃ karitvā me, dhammaṃ desesi cakkhumā;
```

```
Tassāhaṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, vihāsiṃ sāsane rato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§639.</p>

```
‘‘Samathaṃ paṭipādesiṃ, uttamatthassa pattiyā;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§640.</p>

```
‘‘Nekkhamme <note>nikkhame (ka.), nekkhammaṃ (mahāva. 244; a. ni. 6.55)</note> adhimuttassa, pavivekañca cetaso;
```

```
Abyāpajjhādhimuttassa <note>abyāpajjhādhimhattassa (ka.)</note>, upādānakkhayassa ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§641.</p>

```
‘‘Taṇhakkhayādhimuttassa, asammohañca cetaso;
```

```
Disvā āyatanuppādaṃ, sammā cittaṃ vimuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§642.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa <pb ed="P" n="0.0066" /> sammā vimuttassa, santacittassa bhikkhuno;
```

```
Katassa paṭicayo natthi, karaṇīyaṃ na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§643.</p>

```
‘‘Selo <pb ed="M" n="0.0313" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0248" /> yathā ekaghano <note>ekaghano (ka.)</note>, vātena na samīrati;
```

```
Evaṃ rūpā rasā saddā, gandhā phassā ca kevalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§644.</p>

```
‘‘Iṭṭhā <pb ed="T" n="0.0362" /> dhammā aniṭṭhā ca, nappavedhenti tādino;
```

```
Ṭhitaṃ cittaṃ visaññuttaṃ, vayañcassānupassatī’’ti.
```

… Soṇo koḷiviso thero….

<trailer rend="centre">Terasanipāto niṭṭhito.</trailer>

Tatruddānaṃ –

```
Soṇo koḷiviso thero, ekoyeva mahiddhiko;
```

```
Terasamhi nipātamhi, gāthāyo cettha terasāti.
```

### 14. Cuddasakanipāto

#### 1. Khadiravaniyarevatattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§645.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā <pb ed="M" n="0.0314" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0249" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0067" /> ahaṃ pabbajito, agārasmānagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Nābhijānāmi saṅkappaṃ, anariyaṃ dosasaṃhitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§646.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ime haññantu vajjhantu, dukkhaṃ pappontu pāṇino’;
```

```
Saṅkappaṃ nābhijānāmi, imasmiṃ dīghamantare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§647.</p>

```
‘‘Mettañca abhijānāmi, appamāṇaṃ subhāvitaṃ;
```

```
Anupubbaṃ paricitaṃ, yathā buddhena desitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§648.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbamitto sabbasakho, sabbabhūtānukampako;
```

```
Mettacittañca <note>mettaṃ cittaṃ (sī. syā.)</note> bhāvemi, abyāpajjarato <note>abyāpajjharato (sī. syā.)</note> sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§649.</p>

```
‘‘Asaṃhīraṃ asaṃkuppaṃ, cittaṃ āmodayāmahaṃ;
```

```
Brahmavihāraṃ bhāvemi, akāpurisasevitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§650.</p>

```
‘‘Avitakkaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0363" /> samāpanno, sammāsambuddhasāvako;
```

```
Ariyena tuṇhībhāvena, upeto hoti tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§651.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāpi pabbato selo, acalo suppatiṭṭhito;
```

```
Evaṃ mohakkhayā bhikkhu, pabbatova na vedhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§652.</p>

```
‘‘Anaṅgaṇassa posassa, niccaṃ sucigavesino;
```

```
Vālaggamattaṃ pāpassa, abbhamattaṃva khāyati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§653.</p>

```
‘‘Nagaraṃ yathā paccantaṃ, guttaṃ santarabāhiraṃ;
```

```
Evaṃ gopetha attānaṃ, khaṇo vo mā upaccagā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§654.</p>

```
‘‘Nābhinandāmi maraṇaṃ, nābhinandāmi jīvitaṃ;
```

```
Kālañca paṭikaṅkhāmi, nibbisaṃ bhatako yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§655.</p>

```
‘‘Nābhinandāmi maraṇaṃ…pe… sampajāno patissato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§656.</p>

```
‘‘Pariciṇṇo mayā satthā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ;
```

```
Ohito garuko bhāro, bhavanetti samūhatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§657.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa <pb ed="M" n="0.0315" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0250" /> catthāya pabbajito, agārasmānagāriyaṃ;
```

```
So me attho anuppatto, sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§658.</p>

```
‘‘Sampādethappamādena, esā me anusāsanī;
```

```
Handāhaṃ parinibbissaṃ, vippamuttomhi sabbadhī’’ti.
```

… Khadiravaniyarevato thero….

#### 2. Godattattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§659.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāpi bhaddo ājañño, dhure yutto dhurassaho <note>dhurāsaho (aṭṭha.)</note>;
```

```
Mathito <pb ed="T" n="0.0364" /> atibhārena, saṃyugaṃ nātivattati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§660.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ paññāya ye tittā, samuddo vārinā yathā;
```

```
Na pare atimaññanti, ariyadhammova pāṇinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§661.</p>

```
‘‘Kāle <pb ed="P" n="0.0068" /> kālavasaṃ pattā, bhavābhavavasaṃ gatā;
```

```
Narā dukkhaṃ nigacchanti, tedha socanti māṇavā <note>mānavā (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§662.</p>

```
‘‘Unnatā sukhadhammena, dukkhadhammena conatā;
```

```
Dvayena bālā haññanti, yathābhūtaṃ adassino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§663.</p>

```
‘‘Ye ca dukkhe sukhasmiñca, majjhe sibbinimaccagū;
```

```
Ṭhitā te indakhīlova, na te unnataonatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§664.</p>

```
‘‘Na heva lābhe nālābhe, na yase na ca kittiyā;
```

```
Na nindāyaṃ pasaṃsāya, na te dukkhe sukhamhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§665.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbattha te na limpanti, udabinduva pokkhare;
```

```
Sabbattha sukhitā dhīrā, sabbattha aparājitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§666.</p>

```
‘‘Dhammena ca alābho yo, yo ca lābho adhammiko;
```

```
Alābho dhammiko seyyo, yaṃ ce lābho adhammiko.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§667.</p>

```
‘‘Yaso ca appabuddhīnaṃ, viññūnaṃ ayaso ca yo;
```

```
Ayasova seyyo viññūnaṃ, na yaso appabuddhinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§668.</p>

```
‘‘Dummedhehi <pb ed="M" n="0.0316" /> pasaṃsā ca, viññūhi garahā ca yā;
```

```
Garahāva seyyo viññūhi, yaṃ ce bālappasaṃsanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§669.</p>

```
‘‘Sukhañca <pb ed="T" n="0.0365" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0251" /> kāmamayikaṃ, dukkhañca pavivekiyaṃ;
```

```
Pavivekadukkhaṃ seyyo, yaṃ ce kāmamayaṃ sukhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§670.</p>

```
‘‘Jīvitañca adhammena, dhammena maraṇañca yaṃ;
```

```
Maraṇaṃ dhammikaṃ seyyo, yaṃ ce jīve adhammikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§671.</p>

```
‘‘Kāmakopappahīnā ye, santacittā bhavābhave;
```

```
Caranti loke asitā, natthi tesaṃ piyāpiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§672.</p>

```
‘‘Bhāvayitvāna bojjhaṅge, indriyāni balāni ca;
```

```
Pappuyya paramaṃ santiṃ, parinibbantināsavā’’ti.
```

… Godatto thero….

<trailer rend="centre">Cuddasakanipāto niṭṭhito.</trailer>

Tatruddānaṃ –

```
Revato ceva godatto, therā dve te mahiddhikā;
```

```
Cuddasamhi nipātamhi, gāthāyo aṭṭhavīsatīti.
```

### 15. Soḷasakanipāto

#### 1. Aññāsikoṇḍaññattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§673.</p>

```
‘‘Esa <pb ed="M" n="0.0317" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0252" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0069" /> bhiyyo pasīdāmi, sutvā dhammaṃ mahārasaṃ;
```

```
Virāgo desito dhammo, anupādāya sabbaso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§674.</p>

```
‘‘Bahūni loke citrāni, asmiṃ pathavimaṇḍale;
```

```
Mathenti <pb ed="T" n="0.0366" /> maññe saṅkappaṃ, subhaṃ rāgūpasaṃhitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§675.</p>

```
‘‘Rajamuhatañca vātena, yathā meghopasammaye;
```

```
Evaṃ sammanti saṅkappā, yadā paññāya passati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§676.</p>

```
<note>dha. pa. 277 dhammapade</note> ‘‘Sabbe saṅkhārā aniccāti, yadā paññāya passati;
```

```
Atha nibbindati dukkhe, esa maggo visuddhiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§677 .</p>

```
<note>dha. pa. 278 dhammapade</note> ‘‘Sabbe saṅkhārā dukkhāti, yadā paññāya passati
```

```
Atha nibbindati dukkhe, esa maggo visuddhiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§678.</p>

```
<note>dha. pa. 279 dhammapade</note> ‘‘Sabbe dhammā anattāti, yadā paññāya passati;
```

```
Atha nibbindati dukkhe, esa maggo visuddhiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§679.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhānubuddho yo thero, koṇḍañño tibbanikkamo;
```

```
Pahīnajātimaraṇo, brahmacariyassa kevalī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§680.</p>

```
‘‘Oghapāso daḷhakhilo <note>daḷho khilo (syā. ka.)</note>, pabbato duppadālayo;
```

```
Chetvā khilañca pāsañca, selaṃ bhetvāna <note>chetvāna (ka.)</note> dubbhidaṃ;
```

```
Tiṇṇo pāraṅgato jhāyī, mutto so mārabandhanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§681.</p>

```
‘‘Uddhato capalo bhikkhu, mitte āgamma pāpake;
```

```
Saṃsīdati mahoghasmiṃ, ūmiyā paṭikujjito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§682.</p>

```
‘‘Anuddhato acapalo, nipako saṃvutindriyo;
```

```
Kalyāṇamitto medhāvī, dukkhassantakaro siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§683.</p>

```
‘‘Kālapabbaṅgasaṅkāso, kiso dhamanisanthato;
```

```
Mattaññū <pb ed="T" n="0.0367" /> annapānasmiṃ, adīnamanaso naro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§684.</p>

```
‘‘Phuṭṭho <pb ed="V" n="0.0253" /> ḍaṃsehi makasehi, araññasmiṃ brahāvane;
```

```
Nāgo saṅgāmasīseva, sato tatrādhivāsaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§685.</p>

```
‘‘Nābhinandāmi <pb ed="M" n="0.0318" /> maraṇaṃ…pe… nibbisaṃ bhatako yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§686.</p>

```
‘‘Nābhinandāmi maraṇaṃ…pe… sampajāno patissato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§687.</p>

```
‘‘Pariciṇṇo mayā satthā…pe… bhavanetti samūhatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§688.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa catthāya pabbajito, agārasmānagāriyaṃ;
```

```
So me attho anuppatto, kiṃ me saddhivihārinā’’ti.
```

… Aññāsikoṇḍañño <note>aññākoṇḍañño (sī. syā.)</note> thero….

#### 2. Udāyittheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§689.</p>

```
<note>a. ni. 6.43</note> ‘‘Manussabhūtaṃ sambuddhaṃ, attadantaṃ samāhitaṃ;
```

```
Iriyamānaṃ brahmapathe, cittassūpasame rataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§690.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ manussā namassanti, sabbadhammāna pāraguṃ;
```

```
Devāpi taṃ namassanti, iti me arahato sutaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§691.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbasaṃyojanātītaṃ<pb ed="P" n="0.0070" />, vanā nibbanamāgataṃ;
```

```
Kāmehi nekkhammarataṃ <note>nikkhammarataṃ (ka.)</note>, muttaṃ selāva kañcanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§692.</p>

```
‘‘Sa ve accaruci nāgo, himavāvaññe siluccaye;
```

```
Sabbesaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0368" /> nāganāmānaṃ, saccanāmo anuttaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§693.</p>

```
‘‘Nāgaṃ vo kittayissāmi, na hi āguṃ karoti so;
```

```
Soraccaṃ avihiṃsā ca, pādā nāgassa te duve.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§694.</p>

```
‘‘Sati ca sampajaññañca, caraṇā nāgassa tepare;
```

```
Saddhāhattho mahānāgo, upekkhāsetadantavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§695.</p>

```
‘‘Sati gīvā siro paññā, vīmaṃsā dhammacintanā;
```

```
Dhammakucchisamāvāso, viveko tassa vāladhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§696.</p>

```
‘‘So jhāyī assāsarato, ajjhattaṃ susamāhito;
```

```
Gacchaṃ samāhito nāgo, ṭhito nāgo samāhito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§697.</p>

```
‘‘Sayaṃ samāhito nāgo, nisinnopi samāhito;
```

```
Sabbattha saṃvuto nāgo, esā nāgassa sampadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§698.</p>

```
‘‘Bhuñjati <pb ed="M" n="0.0319" /> anavajjāni, sāvajjāni na bhuñjati;
```

```
Ghāsamacchādanaṃ laddhā, sannidhiṃ parivajjayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§699.</p>

```
‘‘Saṃyojanaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0254" /> aṇuṃ thūlaṃ, sabbaṃ chetvāna bandhanaṃ;
```

```
Yena yeneva gacchati, anapakkhova gacchati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§700.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāpi udake jātaṃ, puṇḍarīkaṃ pavaḍḍhati;
```

```
Nopalippati toyena, sucigandhaṃ manoramaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§701.</p>

```
‘‘Tatheva ca loke jāto, buddho loke viharati;
```

```
Nopalippati lokena, toyena padumaṃ yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§702.</p>

```
‘‘Mahāgini pajjalito, anāhāropasammati;
```

```
Aṅgāresu <pb ed="T" n="0.0369" /> ca santesu, nibbutoti pavuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§703.</p>

```
‘‘Atthassāyaṃ viññāpanī, upamā viññūhi desitā;
```

```
Viññissanti mahānāgā, nāgaṃ nāgena desitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§704.</p>

```
‘‘Vītarāgo vītadoso, vītamoho anāsavo;
```

```
Sarīraṃ vijahaṃ nāgo, parinibbissatyanāsavo’’ti.
```

… Udāyī thero….

<trailer rend="centre">Soḷasakanipāto niṭṭhito.</trailer>

Tatruddānaṃ –

```
Koṇḍañño ca udāyī ca, therā dve te mahiddhikā;
```

```
Soḷasamhi nipātamhi, gāthāyo dve ca tiṃsa cāti.
```

### 16. Vīsatinipāto

#### 1. Adhimuttattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§705.</p>

```
‘‘Yaññatthaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0320" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0255" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0071" /> vā dhanatthaṃ vā, ye hanāma mayaṃ pure;
```

```
Avasesaṃ <note>avase taṃ (sī. aṭṭha. mūlapāṭho), avasesānaṃ (aṭṭha.?)</note> bhayaṃ hoti, vedhanti vilapanti ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§706.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa te natthi bhītattaṃ, bhiyyo vaṇṇo pasīdati;
```

```
Kasmā na paridevesi, evarūpe mahabbhaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§707.</p>

```
‘‘Natthi cetasikaṃ dukkhaṃ, anapekkhassa gāmaṇi;
```

```
Atikkantā bhayā sabbe, khīṇasaṃyojanassa ve.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§708.</p>

```
‘‘Khīṇāya bhavanettiyā, diṭṭhe dhamme yathātathe;
```

```
Na <pb ed="T" n="0.0370" /> bhayaṃ maraṇe hoti, bhāranikkhepane yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§709.</p>

```
‘‘Suciṇṇaṃ brahmacariyaṃ me, maggo cāpi subhāvito;
```

```
Maraṇe me bhayaṃ natthi, rogānamiva saṅkhaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§710.</p>

```
‘‘Suciṇṇaṃ brahmacariyaṃ me, maggo cāpi subhāvito;
```

```
Nirassādā bhavā diṭṭhā, visaṃ pitvāva <note>pītvāva (sī.)</note> chaḍḍitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§711.</p>

```
‘‘Pāragū anupādāno, katakicco anāsavo;
```

```
Tuṭṭho āyukkhayā hoti, mutto āghātanā yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§712.</p>

```
‘‘Uttamaṃ dhammataṃ patto, sabbaloke anatthiko;
```

```
Ādittāva gharā mutto, maraṇasmiṃ na socati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§713.</p>

```
‘‘Yadatthi saṅgataṃ kiñci, bhavo vā yattha labbhati;
```

```
Sabbaṃ anissaraṃ etaṃ, iti vuttaṃ mahesinā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§714.</p>

```
‘‘Yo taṃ tathā pajānāti, yathā buddhena desitaṃ;
```

```
Na gaṇhāti bhavaṃ kiñci, sutattaṃva ayoguḷaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§715.</p>

```
‘‘Na me hoti ‘ahosi’nti, ‘bhavissa’nti na hoti me;
```

```
Saṅkhārā vigamissanti, tattha kā paridevanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§716.</p>

```
‘‘Suddhaṃ dhammasamuppādaṃ, suddhaṃ saṅkhārasantatiṃ;
```

```
Passantassa yathābhūtaṃ, na bhayaṃ hoti gāmaṇi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§717.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṇakaṭṭhasamaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0321" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0256" /> lokaṃ, yadā paññāya passati;
```

```
Mamattaṃ so asaṃvindaṃ, ‘natthi me’ti na socati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§718.</p>

```
‘‘Ukkaṇṭhāmi <pb ed="P" n="0.0072" /> sarīrena, bhavenamhi anatthiko;
```

```
Soyaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0371" /> bhijjissati kāyo, añño ca na bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§719.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ vo kiccaṃ sarīrena, taṃ karotha yadicchatha;
```

```
Na me tappaccayā tattha, doso pemañca hehiti’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§720.</p>

```
Tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, abbhutaṃ lomahaṃsanaṃ;
```

```
Satthāni nikkhipitvāna, māṇavā etadabravuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§721.</p>

```
‘‘Kiṃ bhadante karitvāna, ko vā ācariyo tava;
```

```
Kassa sāsanamāgamma, labbhate taṃ asokatā’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§722.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbaññū sabbadassāvī, jino ācariyo mama;
```

```
Mahākāruṇiko satthā, sabbalokatikicchako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§723.</p>

```
‘‘Tenāyaṃ desito dhammo, khayagāmī anuttaro;
```

```
Tassa sāsanamāgamma, labbhate taṃ asokatā’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§724.</p>

```
Sutvāna corā isino subhāsitaṃ, nikkhippa satthāni ca āvudhāni ca;
```

```
Tamhā ca kammā viramiṃsu eke, eke ca pabbajjamarocayiṃsu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§725.</p>

```
Te pabbajitvā sugatassa sāsane, bhāvetva bojjhaṅgabalāni paṇḍitā;
```

```
Udaggacittā sumanā katindriyā, phusiṃsu nibbānapadaṃ asaṅkhatanti.
```

…Adhimutto thero….

#### 2. Pārāpariyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§726.</p>

```
‘‘Samaṇassa <pb ed="T" n="0.0372" /> ahu cintā, pārāpariyassa bhikkhuno;
```

```
Ekakassa nisinnassa, pavivittassa jhāyino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§727.</p>

```
‘‘Kimānupubbaṃ puriso, kiṃ vataṃ kiṃ samācāraṃ;
```

```
Attano kiccakārīssa, na ca kañci viheṭhaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§728.</p>

```
‘‘Indriyāni <pb ed="M" n="0.0322" /> manussānaṃ, hitāya ahitāya ca;
```

```
Arakkhitāni ahitāya, rakkhitāni hitāya ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§729.</p>

```
‘‘Indriyāneva sārakkhaṃ, indriyāni ca gopayaṃ;
```

```
Attano kiccakārīssa, na ca kañci viheṭhaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§730.</p>

```
‘‘Cakkhundriyaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0257" /> ce rūpesu, gacchantaṃ anivārayaṃ;
```

```
Anādīnavadassāvī, so dukkhā na hi muccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§731.</p>

```
‘‘Sotindriyaṃ ce saddesu, gacchantaṃ anivārayaṃ;
```

```
Anādīnavadassāvī, so dukkhā na hi muccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§732.</p>

```
‘‘Anissaraṇadassāvī<pb ed="P" n="0.0073" />, gandhe ce paṭisevati;
```

```
Na so muccati dukkhamhā, gandhesu adhimucchito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§733.</p>

```
‘‘Ambilaṃ madhuraggañca, tittakaggamanussaraṃ;
```

```
Rasataṇhāya gadhito, hadayaṃ nāvabujjhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§734.</p>

```
‘‘Subhānyappaṭikūlāni, phoṭṭhabbāni anussaraṃ;
```

```
Ratto rāgādhikaraṇaṃ, vividhaṃ vindate dukhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§735.</p>

```
‘‘Manaṃ cetehi dhammehi, yo na sakkoti rakkhituṃ;
```

```
Tato <pb ed="T" n="0.0373" /> naṃ dukkhamanveti, sabbehetehi pañcahi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§736.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbalohitasampuṇṇaṃ, bahussa kuṇapassa ca;
```

```
Naravīrakataṃ vagguṃ, samuggamiva cittitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§737.</p>

```
‘‘Kaṭukaṃ madhurassādaṃ, piyanibandhanaṃ dukhaṃ;
```

```
Khuraṃva madhunā littaṃ, ullihaṃ nāvabujjhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§738.</p>

```
‘‘Itthirūpe itthisare, phoṭṭhabbepi ca itthiyā;
```

```
Itthigandhesu sāratto, vividhaṃ vindate dukhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§739.</p>

```
‘‘Itthisotāni sabbāni, sandanti pañca pañcasu;
```

```
Tesamāvaraṇaṃ kātuṃ, yo sakkoti vīriyavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§740.</p>

```
‘‘So atthavā so dhammaṭṭho, so dakkho so vicakkhaṇo;
```

```
Kareyya ramamānopi, kiccaṃ dhammatthasaṃhitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§741.</p>

```
‘‘Atho <pb ed="M" n="0.0323" /> sīdati saññuttaṃ, vajje kiccaṃ niratthakaṃ;
```

```
‘Na taṃ kicca’nti maññitvā, appamatto vicakkhaṇo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§742.</p>

```
‘‘Yañca atthena saññuttaṃ, yā ca dhammagatā rati;
```

```
Taṃ samādāya vattetha, sā hi ve uttamā rati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§743.</p>

```
‘‘Uccāvacehupāyehi, paresamabhijigīsati;
```

```
Hantvā vadhitvā atha socayitvā, ālopati sāhasā yo paresaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§744.</p>

```
‘‘Tacchanto āṇiyā āṇiṃ, nihanti balavā yathā;
```

```
Indriyānindriyeheva<pb ed="T" n="0.0374" />, nihanti kusalo tathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§745.</p>

```
‘‘Saddhaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0258" /> vīriyaṃ samādhiñca, satipaññañca bhāvayaṃ;
```

```
Pañca pañcahi hantvāna, anīgho yāti brāhmaṇo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§746.</p>

```
‘‘So atthavā so dhammaṭṭho, katvā vākyānusāsaniṃ;
```

```
Sabbena sabbaṃ buddhassa, so naro sukhamedhatī’’ti.
```

…Pārāpariyo thero….

#### 3. Telakānittheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§747.</p>

```
‘‘Cirarattaṃ vatātāpī, dhammaṃ anuvicintayaṃ;
```

```
Samaṃ cittassa nālatthaṃ, pucchaṃ samaṇabrāhmaṇe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§748.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ko <pb ed="P" n="0.0074" /> so pāraṅgato loke, ko patto amatogadhaṃ;
```

```
Kassa dhammaṃ paṭicchāmi, paramatthavijānanaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§749.</p>

```
‘‘Antovaṅkagato āsi, macchova ghasamāmisaṃ;
```

```
Baddho mahindapāsena, vepacityasuro yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§750.</p>

```
‘‘Añchāmi naṃ na muñcāmi, asmā sokapariddavā;
```

```
Ko me bandhaṃ muñcaṃ loke, sambodhiṃ vedayissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§751.</p>

```
‘‘Samaṇaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ vā kaṃ, ādisantaṃ pabhaṅgunaṃ.
```

```
Kassa dhammaṃ paṭicchāmi, jarāmaccupavāhanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§752.</p>

```
‘‘Vicikicchākaṅkhāganthitaṃ, sārambhabalasaññutaṃ;
```

```
Kodhappattamanatthaddhaṃ, abhijappappadāraṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§753.</p>

```
‘‘Taṇhādhanusamuṭṭhānaṃ<pb ed="M" n="0.0324" />, dve ca pannarasāyutaṃ <note>dvedhāpannarasāyutaṃ (?)</note>;
```

```
Passa <pb ed="T" n="0.0375" /> orasikaṃ bāḷhaṃ, bhetvāna yadi <note>yada (sī. aṭṭha.) hadi (?) ‘‘hadaye’’ti taṃsaṃvaṇṇanā</note> tiṭṭhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§754.</p>

```
‘‘Anudiṭṭhīnaṃ appahānaṃ, saṅkappaparatejitaṃ;
```

```
Tena viddho pavedhāmi, pattaṃva māluteritaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§755.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjhattaṃ me samuṭṭhāya, khippaṃ paccati māmakaṃ;
```

```
Chaphassāyatanī kāyo, yattha sarati sabbadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§756.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ na passāmi tekicchaṃ, yo metaṃ sallamuddhare;
```

```
Nānārajjena satthena <note>nāraggena na satthena (?)</note>, nāññena vicikicchitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§757.</p>

```
‘‘Ko me asattho avaṇo, sallamabbhantarapassayaṃ;
```

```
Ahiṃsaṃ sabbagattāni, sallaṃ me uddharissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§758.</p>

```
‘‘Dhammappati <pb ed="V" n="0.0259" /> hi so seṭṭho, visadosappavāhako;
```

```
Gambhīre patitassa me, thalaṃ pāṇiñca dassaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§759.</p>

```
‘‘Rahadehamasmi ogāḷho, ahāriyarajamattike;
```

```
Māyāusūyasārambha, thinamiddhamapatthaṭe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§760.</p>

```
‘‘Uddhaccameghathanitaṃ, saṃyojanavalāhakaṃ;
```

```
Vāhā vahanti kuddiṭṭhiṃ <note>duddiṭṭhiṃ (sī. dha. pa. 339)</note>, saṅkappā rāganissitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§761.</p>

```
‘‘Savanti sabbadhi sotā, latā ubbhijja tiṭṭhati;
```

```
Te sote ko nivāreyya, taṃ lataṃ ko hi checchati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§762.</p>

```
‘‘Velaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0075" /> karotha bhaddante, sotānaṃ sannivāraṇaṃ;
```

```
Mā te manomayo soto, rukkhaṃva sahasā luve.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§763.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0376" /> me bhayajātassa, apārā pāramesato;
```

```
Tāṇo paññāvudho satthā, isisaṅghanisevito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§764.</p>

```
‘‘Sopāṇaṃ sugataṃ suddhaṃ, dhammasāramayaṃ daḷhaṃ;
```

```
Pādāsi vuyhamānassa, ‘mā bhāyī’ti ca mabravi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§765.</p>

```
‘‘Satipaṭṭhānapāsādaṃ, āruyha paccavekkhisaṃ;
```

```
Yaṃ taṃ pubbe amaññissaṃ, sakkāyābhirataṃ pajaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§766.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā <pb ed="M" n="0.0325" /> ca maggamaddakkhiṃ, nāvāya abhirūhanaṃ;
```

```
Anadhiṭṭhāya attānaṃ, titthamaddakkhimuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§767.</p>

```
‘‘Sallaṃ attasamuṭṭhānaṃ, bhavanettippabhāvitaṃ;
```

```
Etesaṃ appavattāya <note>appavattiyā (?)</note>, desesi maggamuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§768.</p>

```
‘‘Dīgharattānusayitaṃ, cirarattamadhiṭṭhitaṃ;
```

```
Buddho mepānudī ganthaṃ, visadosappavāhano’’ti.
```

…Telakāni thero….

#### 4. Raṭṭhapālattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§769.</p>

```
<note>ma. ni. 2.302</note> ‘‘Passa cittakataṃ bimbaṃ, arukāyaṃ samussitaṃ;
```

```
Āturaṃ bahusaṅkappaṃ, yassa natthi dhuvaṃ ṭhiti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§770.</p>

```
‘‘Passa cittakataṃ rūpaṃ, maṇinā kuṇḍalena ca;
```

```
Aṭṭhiṃ tacena onaddhaṃ, saha vatthehi sobhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§771.</p>

```
‘‘Alattakakatā <pb ed="V" n="0.0260" /> pādā, mukhaṃ cuṇṇakamakkhitaṃ;
```

```
Alaṃ bālassa mohāya, no ca pāragavesino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§772.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhapadakatā <pb ed="T" n="0.0377" /> kesā, nettā añjanamakkhitā;
```

```
Alaṃ bālassa mohāya, no ca pāragavesino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§773.</p>

```
‘‘Añjanīva navā cittā, pūtikāyo alaṅkato;
```

```
Alaṃ bālassa mohāya, no ca pāragavesino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§774.</p>

```
‘‘Odahi migavo pāsaṃ, nāsadā vāguraṃ migo;
```

```
Bhutvā nivāpaṃ gacchāma, kandante migabandhake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§775.</p>

```
‘‘Chinno pāso migavassa, nāsadā vāguraṃ migo;
```

```
Bhutvā nivāpaṃ gacchāma, socante migaluddake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§776.</p>

```
‘‘Passāmi loke sadhane manusse, laddhāna vittaṃ na dadanti mohā;
```

```
Luddhā <pb ed="P" n="0.0076" /> dhanaṃ sannicayaṃ karonti, bhiyyova kāme abhipatthayanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§777.</p>

```
‘‘Rājā <pb ed="M" n="0.0326" /> pasayhappathaviṃ vijetvā, sasāgarantaṃ mahimāvasanto;
```

```
Oraṃ samuddassa atittarūpo, pāraṃ samuddassapi patthayetha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§778.</p>

```
‘‘Rājā ca aññe ca bahū manussā, avītataṇhā maraṇaṃ upenti;
```

```
Ūnāva hutvāna jahanti dehaṃ, kāmehi lokamhi na hatthi titti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§779.</p>

```
‘‘Kandanti <pb ed="T" n="0.0378" /> naṃ ñātī pakiriya kese, aho vatā no amarāti cāhu;
```

```
Vatthena naṃ pārutaṃ nīharitvā, citaṃ samodhāya tato ḍahanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§780.</p>

```
‘‘So ḍayhati sūlehi tujjamāno, ekena vatthena <note>etena gatthena (ka.)</note> pahāya bhoge;
```

```
Na mīyamānassa bhavanti tāṇā, ñātī ca mittā atha vā sahāyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§781.</p>

```
‘‘Dāyādakā tassa dhanaṃ haranti, satto pana gacchati yena kammaṃ;
```

```
Na mīyamānaṃ dhanamanveti <note>manviti (ka.)</note> kiñci, puttā ca dārā ca dhanañca raṭṭhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§782.</p>

```
‘‘Na dīghamāyuṃ labhate dhanena, na cāpi vittena jaraṃ vihanti;
```

```
Appappaṃ hidaṃ jīvitamāhu dhīrā, asassataṃ vippariṇāmadhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§783.</p>

```
‘‘Aḍḍhā daliddā ca phusanti phassaṃ, bālo ca dhīro ca tatheva phuṭṭho;
```

```
Bālo hi bālyā vadhitova seti, dhīro <pb ed="T" n="0.0379" /> ca no vedhati phassaphuṭṭho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§784.</p>

```
‘‘Tasmā <pb ed="M" n="0.0327" /> hi paññāva dhanena seyyā, yāya vosānamidhādhigacchati;
```

```
Abyositattā hi bhavābhavesu, pāpāni kammāni karoti mohā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§785.</p>

```
‘‘Upeti <pb ed="P" n="0.0077" /> gabbhañca parañca lokaṃ, saṃsāramāpajja paramparāya;
```

```
Tassappapañño abhisaddahanto, upeti gabbhañca parañca lokaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§786.</p>

```
‘‘Coro <pb ed="V" n="0.0261" /> yathā sandhimukhe gahīto, sakammunā haññati pāpadhammo;
```

```
Evaṃ pajā pecca paramhi loke, sakammunā haññati pāpadhammo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§787.</p>

```
‘‘Kāmā hi citrā madhurā manoramā, virūparūpena mathenti cittaṃ;
```

```
Ādīnavaṃ kāmaguṇesu disvā, tasmā ahaṃ pabbajitomhi rāja.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§788.</p>

```
‘‘Dumapphalānīva patanti māṇavā, daharā ca vuḍḍhā ca sarīrabhedā;
```

```
Etampi <pb ed="T" n="0.0380" /> disvā pabbajitomhi rāja, apaṇṇakaṃ sāmaññameva seyyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§789.</p>

```
‘‘Saddhāyāhaṃ pabbajito, upeto jinasāsane;
```

```
Avajjhā mayhaṃ pabbajjā, anaṇo bhuñjāmi bhojanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§790.</p>

```
‘‘Kāme ādittato disvā, jātarūpāni satthato;
```

```
Gabbhavokkantito dukkhaṃ, nirayesu mahabbhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§791.</p>

```
‘‘Etamādīnavaṃ ñatvā, saṃvegaṃ alabhiṃ tadā;
```

```
Sohaṃ viddho tadā santo, sampatto āsavakkhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§792.</p>

```
‘‘Pariciṇṇo mayā satthā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ;
```

```
Ohito garuko bhāro, bhavanetti samūhatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§793.</p>

```
‘‘Yassatthāya pabbajito, agārasmānagāriyaṃ;
```

```
So me attho anuppatto, sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo’’ti.
```

… Raṭṭhapālo thero….

#### 5. Mālukyaputtattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§794.</p>

```
<note>saṃ. ni. 4.95</note> ‘‘Rūpaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0328" /> disvā sati muṭṭhā, piyaṃ nimittaṃ manasi karoto;
```

```
Sārattacitto vedeti, tañca ajjhossa tiṭṭhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§795.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa <pb ed="T" n="0.0381" /> vaḍḍhanti vedanā, anekā rūpasambhavā;
```

```
Abhijjhā ca vihesā ca, cittamassūpahaññati;
```

```
Evamācinato dukkhaṃ, ārā nibbāna <note>nibbānaṃ (sī.)</note> vuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§796.</p>

```
‘‘Saddaṃ sutvā sati muṭṭhā, piyaṃ nimittaṃ manasi karoto;
```

```
Sārattacitto vedeti, tañca ajjhossa tiṭṭhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§797.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa vaḍḍhanti vedanā, anekā saddasambhavā;
```

```
Abhijjhā ca vihesā ca, cittamassūpahaññati;
```

```
Evamācinato dukkhaṃ, ārā nibbāna vuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§798.</p>

```
‘‘Gandhaṃ ghatvā sati muṭṭhā, piyaṃ nimittaṃ manasi karoto;
```

```
Sārattacitto vedeti, tañca ajjhossa tiṭṭhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§799.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa <pb ed="V" n="0.0262" /> vaḍḍhanti vedanā, anekā gandhasambhavā;
```

```
Abhijjhā ca vihesā ca, cittamassūpahaññati;
```

```
Evamācinato dukkhaṃ, ārā nibbāna vuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§800.</p>

```
‘‘Rasaṃ bhotvā sati muṭṭhā, piyaṃ nimittaṃ manasi karoto;
```

```
Sārattacitto vedeti, tañca ajjhossa tiṭṭhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§801.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa <pb ed="T" n="0.0382" /> vaḍḍhanti vedanā, anekā rasasambhavā;
```

```
Abhijjhā ca vihesā ca, cittamassūpahaññati;
```

```
Evamācinato dukkhaṃ, ārā nibbāna vuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§802.</p>

```
‘‘Phassaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0078" /> phussa sati muṭṭhā, piyaṃ nimittaṃ manasi karoto;
```

```
Sārattacitto vedeti, tañca ajjhossa tiṭṭhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§803.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa vaḍḍhanti vedanā, anekā phassasambhavā;
```

```
Abhijjhā ca vihesā ca, cittamassūpahaññati;
```

```
Evamācinato dukkhaṃ, ārā nibbāna vuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§804.</p>

```
‘‘Dhammaṃ ñatvā sati muṭṭhā, piyaṃ nimittaṃ manasi karoto;
```

```
Sārattacitto vedeti, tañca ajjhossa tiṭṭhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§805.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa <pb ed="M" n="0.0329" /> vaḍḍhanti vedanā, anekā dhammasambhavā;
```

```
Abhijjhā ca vihesā ca, cittamassūpahaññati;
```

```
Evamācinato dukkhaṃ, ārā nibbāna vuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§806.</p>

```
‘‘Na so rajjati rūpesu, rūpaṃ disvā patissato;
```

```
Virattacitto vedeti, tañca nājjhossa tiṭṭhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§807.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāssa passato rūpaṃ, sevato cāpi vedanaṃ;
```

```
Khīyati nopacīyati, evaṃ so caratī sato;
```

```
Evaṃ apacinato dukkhaṃ, santike nibbāna vuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§808.</p>

```
‘‘Na so rajjati saddesu, saddaṃ sutvā patissato;
```

```
Virattacitto vedeti, tañca nājjhossa tiṭṭhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§809.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāssa suṇato saddaṃ, sevato cāpi vedanaṃ;
```

```
Khīyati nopacīyati, evaṃ so caratī sato;
```

```
Evaṃ apacinato dukkhaṃ, santike nibbāna vuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§810.</p>

```
‘‘Na so rajjati gandhesu, gandhaṃ ghatvā patissato;
```

```
Virattacitto vedeti, tañca nājjhossa tiṭṭhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§811.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāssa <pb ed="V" n="0.0263" /> ghāyato gandhaṃ, sevato cāpi vedanaṃ;
```

```
Khīyati nopacīyati, evaṃ so caratī sato;
```

```
Evaṃ apacinato dukkhaṃ, santike nibbāna vuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§812.</p>

```
‘‘Na <pb ed="T" n="0.0383" /> so rajjati rasesu, rasaṃ bhotvā patissato;
```

```
Virattacitto vedeti, tañca nājjhossa tiṭṭhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§813.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāssa sāyarato rasaṃ, sevato cāpi vedanaṃ;
```

```
Khīyati nopacīyati, evaṃ so caratī sato;
```

```
Evaṃ apacinato dukkhaṃ, santike nibbāna vuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§814.</p>

```
‘‘Na so rajjati phassesu, phassaṃ phussa patissato;
```

```
Virattacitto vedeti, tañca nājjhossa tiṭṭhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§815.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāssa phusato phassaṃ, sevato cāpi vedanaṃ;
```

```
Khīyati nopacīyati, evaṃ so caratī sato;
```

```
Evaṃ apacinato dukkhaṃ, santike nibbāna vuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§816.</p>

```
‘‘Na so rajjati dhammesu, dhammaṃ ñatvā patissato;
```

```
Virattacitto vedeti, tañca nājjhossa tiṭṭhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§817.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāssa <pb ed="M" n="0.0330" /> vijānato dhammaṃ, sevato cāpi vedanaṃ;
```

```
Khīyati nopacīyati, evaṃ so caratī sato;
```

```
Evaṃ apacinato dukkhaṃ, santike nibbāna vuccati’’.
```

… Mālukyaputto thero….

#### 6. Selattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§818.</p>

```
‘‘Paripuṇṇakāyo suruci, sujāto cārudassano;
```

```
Suvaṇṇavaṇṇosi bhagavā, susukkadāṭhosi vīriyavā <note>susukkadāṭho virīyavā (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§819.</p>

```
‘‘Narassa hi sujātassa, ye bhavanti viyañjanā;
```

```
Sabbe <pb ed="T" n="0.0384" /> te tava kāyasmiṃ, mahāpurisalakkhaṇā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§820.</p>

```
‘‘Pasannanetto sumukho, brahā uju patāpavā;
```

```
Majjhe samaṇasaṅghassa, ādiccova virocasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§821.</p>

```
‘‘Kalyāṇadassano bhikkhu, kañcanasannibhattaco;
```

```
Kiṃ te samaṇabhāvena, evaṃ uttamavaṇṇino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§822.</p>

```
‘‘Rājā <pb ed="V" n="0.0264" /> arahasi bhavituṃ, cakkavattī rathesabho;
```

```
Cāturanto vijitāvī, jambusaṇḍassa <note>jambumaṇḍassa (ka.)</note> issaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§823.</p>

```
‘‘Khattiyā bhogī rājāno <note>bhogā rājāno (sī. ka.), bhojarājāno (syā.)</note>, anuyantā bhavanti te;
