```

```
Rājābhirājā <note>rājādhirājā (sī. ka.)</note> manujindo, rajjaṃ kārehi gotama’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§824.</p>

```
‘‘Rājāhamasmi <pb ed="P" n="0.0079" /> sela, (selāti bhagavā) dhammarājā anuttaro;
```

```
Dhammena cakkaṃ vattemi, cakkaṃ appaṭivattiyaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§825.</p>

```
‘‘Sambuddho paṭijānāsi, (iti selo brāhmaṇo) dhammarājā anuttaro;
```

```
‘Dhammena cakkaṃ vattemi’, iti bhāsatha gotama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§826.</p>

```
‘‘Ko nu senāpati bhoto, sāvako satthuranvayo <note>anvayo (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Ko tetamanuvatteti, dhammacakkaṃ pavattitaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§827.</p>

```
‘‘Mayā <pb ed="M" n="0.0331" /> pavattitaṃ cakkaṃ, (selāti bhagavā) dhammacakkaṃ anuttaraṃ;
```

```
Sāriputto anuvatteti, anujāto tathāgataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§828.</p>

```
‘‘Abhiññeyyaṃ abhiññātaṃ, bhāvetabbañca bhāvitaṃ;
```

```
Pahātabbaṃ pahīnaṃ me, tasmā buddhosmi brāhmaṇa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§829.</p>

```
‘‘Vinayassu <pb ed="T" n="0.0385" /> mayi kaṅkhaṃ, adhimuñcassu brāhmaṇa;
```

```
Dullabhaṃ dassanaṃ hoti, sambuddhānaṃ abhiṇhaso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§830.</p>

```
‘‘Yesaṃ ve dullabho loke, pātubhāvo abhiṇhaso;
```

```
Sohaṃ brāhmaṇa buddhosmi, sallakatto <note>sallakanto (sī.)</note> anuttaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§831.</p>

```
‘‘Brahmabhūto atitulo, mārasenappamaddano;
```

```
Sabbāmitte vase <note>vasī (syā. ka., ma. ni. 2.399; su. ni. 966)</note> katvā, modāmi akutobhayo’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§832.</p>

```
‘‘Idaṃ bhonto nisāmetha, yathā bhāsati cakkhumā;
```

```
Sallakatto mahāvīro, sīhova nadatī vane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§833.</p>

```
‘‘Brahmabhūtaṃ atitulaṃ, mārasenappamaddanaṃ;
```

```
Ko disvā nappasīdeyya, api kaṇhābhijātiko.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§834.</p>

```
‘‘Yo maṃ icchati anvetu, yo vā nicchati gacchatu;
```

```
Idhāhaṃ pabbajissāmi, varapaññassa santike’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§835.</p>

```
‘‘Etaṃ ce ruccati bhoto, sammāsambuddhasāsanaṃ;
```

```
Mayampi pabbajissāma, varapaññassa santike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§836.</p>

```
‘‘Brāhmaṇā tisatā ime, yācanti pañjalīkatā;
```

```
‘Brahmacariyaṃ carissāma, bhagavā tava santike’’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§837.</p>

```
‘‘Svākhātaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0265" /> brahmacariyaṃ, (selāti bhagavā) sandiṭṭhikamakālikaṃ;
```

```
Yattha amoghā pabbajjā, appamattassa sikkhato’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§838.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0080" /> taṃ saraṇamāgamha <note>saraṇamāgamma (sabbattha)</note>, ito aṭṭhame <note>aṭṭhami (syā. ka.)</note> cakkhuma;
```

```
Sattarattena bhagavā, dantāmha tava sāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§839.</p>

```
‘‘Tuvaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0386" /><pb ed="M" n="0.0332" /> buddho tuvaṃ satthā, tuvaṃ mārābhibhū muni;
```

```
Tuvaṃ anusaye chetvā, tiṇṇo tāresimaṃ pajaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§840.</p>

```
‘‘Upadhī te samatikkantā, āsavā te padālitā;
```

```
Sīhova anupādāno, pahīnabhayabheravo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§841.</p>

```
‘‘Bhikkhavo tisatā ime, tiṭṭhanti pañjalīkatā;
```

```
Pāde vīra pasārehi, nāgā vandantu satthuno’’ti.
```

… Selo thero….

#### 7. Kāḷigodhāputtabhaddiyattheragāthā

```
Sālīnaṃ odano bhutto, sucimaṃsūpasecano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§843.</p>

```
‘‘Sojja bhaddo sātatiko, uñchāpattāgate rato;
```

```
Jhāyati anupādāno, putto godhāya bhaddiyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§844.</p>

```
‘‘Paṃsukūlī sātatiko, uñchāpattāgate rato;
```

```
Jhāyati anupādāno, putto godhāya bhaddiyo.

<p rend="hangnum">§863.</p>

‘‘Ucce maṇḍalipākāre, daḷhamaṭṭālakoṭṭhake;

Pāpuṇiṃ anupubbena, sabbasaṃyojanakkhaya’’nti.

#### 8. Aṅgulimālattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§866.</p>

```
‘‘Gacchaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0388" /> vadesi samaṇa ‘ṭṭhitomhi’, mamañca brūsi ṭhitamaṭṭhitoti;
```

```
Pucchāmi <pb ed="P" n="0.0081" /> taṃ samaṇa etamatthaṃ, ‘kathaṃ ṭhito tvaṃ ahamaṭṭhitomhi’’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§867.</p>

```
‘‘Ṭhito ahaṃ aṅgulimāla sabbadā, sabbesu bhūtesu nidhāya daṇḍaṃ;
```

```
Tuvañca pāṇesu asaññatosi, tasmā ṭhitohaṃ tuvamaṭṭhitosi’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§868.</p>

```
‘‘Cirassaṃ vata me mahito mahesī, mahāvanaṃ samaṇo paccapādi <note>paccupādi (sabbattha)</note>;
```

```
Sohaṃ cajissāmi sahassapāpaṃ, sutvāna gāthaṃ tava dhammayuttaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§869.</p>

```
Icceva <pb ed="M" n="0.0334" /> coro asimāvudhañca, sobbhe papāte narake anvakāsi <note>akiri (ma. ni. 2.349)</note>;
```

```
Avandi coro sugatassa pāde, tattheva pabbajjamayāci buddhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§870.</p>

```
Buddho ca kho kāruṇiko mahesi, yo satthā lokassa sadevakassa;
```

```
‘Tamehi bhikkhū’ti tadā avoca, eseva tassa ahu bhikkhubhāvo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§871.</p>

```
‘‘Yo <pb ed="T" n="0.0389" /> ca pubbe pamajjitvā, pacchā so nappamajjati;
```

```
Somaṃ lokaṃ pabhāseti, abbhā muttova candimā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§872.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa <pb ed="V" n="0.0267" /> pāpaṃ kataṃ kammaṃ, kusalena pidhīyati <note>pithīyati (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Somaṃ lokaṃ pabhāseti, abbhā muttova candimā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§873.</p>

```
‘‘Yo have daharo bhikkhu, yuñjati buddhasāsane;
```

```
Somaṃ lokaṃ pabhāseti, abbhā muttova candimā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§874.</p>

```
<note>disā hi (syā. ka., ma. ni. 2.352)</note> ‘‘Disāpi me dhammakathaṃ suṇantu, disāpi me yuñjantu buddhasāsane;
```

```
Disāpi me te manuje bhajantu, ye dhammamevādapayanti santo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§875.</p>

```
‘‘Disā hi me khantivādānaṃ, avirodhappasaṃsinaṃ;
```

```
Suṇantu dhammaṃ kālena, tañca anuvidhīyantu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§876.</p>

```
‘‘Na hi jātu so mamaṃ hiṃse, aññaṃ vā pana kiñcanaṃ <note>kañcinaṃ (sī. syā.), kañcanaṃ (?)</note>;
```

```
Pappuyya paramaṃ santiṃ, rakkheyya tasathāvare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§877.</p>

```
<note>theragā. 19</note> ‘‘Udakañhi <pb ed="P" n="0.0082" /> nayanti nettikā, usukārā namayanti <note>damayanti (ka.)</note> tejanaṃ;
```

```
Dāruṃ namayanti <note>damayanti (ka.)</note> tacchakā, attānaṃ damayanti paṇḍitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§878.</p>

```
‘‘Daṇḍeneke <pb ed="M" n="0.0335" /> damayanti, aṅkusebhi kasāhi ca;
```

```
Adaṇḍena asatthena, ahaṃ dantomhi tādinā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§879.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ahiṃsako’ti <pb ed="T" n="0.0390" /> me nāmaṃ, hiṃsakassa pure sato;
```

```
Ajjāhaṃ saccanāmomhi, na naṃ hiṃsāmi kiñcanaṃ <note>kañcinaṃ (sī. syā.), kañcanaṃ (?)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§880.</p>

```
‘‘Coro ahaṃ pure āsiṃ, aṅgulimāloti vissuto;
```

```
Vuyhamāno mahoghena, buddhaṃ saraṇamāgamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§881.</p>

```
‘‘Lohitapāṇi pure āsiṃ, aṅgulimāloti vissuto;
```

```
Saraṇagamanaṃ passa, bhavanetti samūhatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§882.</p>

```
‘‘Tādisaṃ kammaṃ katvāna, bahuṃ duggatigāminaṃ;
```

```
Phuṭṭho kammavipākena, anaṇo bhuñjāmi bhojanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§883.</p>

```
‘‘Pamādamanuyuñjanti, bālā dummedhino janā;
```

```
Appamādañca medhāvī, dhanaṃ seṭṭhaṃva rakkhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§884.</p>

```
‘‘Mā pamādamanuyuñjetha, mā kāmaratisanthavaṃ <note>sandhavaṃ (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Appamatto hi jhāyanto, pappoti paramaṃ sukhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§885.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ nāpagataṃ, netaṃ dummantitaṃ mama;
```

```
Savibhattesu dhammesu, yaṃ seṭṭhaṃ tadupāgamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§886.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ nāpagataṃ, netaṃ dummantitaṃ mama;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§887.</p>

```
‘‘Araññe <pb ed="V" n="0.0268" /> rukkhamūle vā, pabbatesu guhāsu vā;
```

```
Tattha tattheva aṭṭhāsiṃ, ubbiggamanaso tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§888.</p>

```
‘‘Sukhaṃ sayāmi ṭhāyāmi, sukhaṃ kappemi jīvitaṃ;
```

```
Ahatthapāso mārassa, aho satthānukampito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§889.</p>

```
‘‘Brahmajacco <pb ed="T" n="0.0391" /> pure āsiṃ, udicco ubhato ahu;
```

```
Sojja putto sugatassa, dhammarājassa satthuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§890.</p>

```
‘‘Vītataṇho anādāno, guttadvāro susaṃvuto;
```

```
Aghamūlaṃ vadhitvāna, patto me āsavakkhayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§891.</p>

```
‘‘Pariciṇṇo <pb ed="M" n="0.0336" /> mayā satthā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ;
```

```
Ohito garuko bhāro, bhavanetti samūhatā’’ti.
```

… Aṅgulimālo thero….

#### 9. Anuruddhattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§892.</p>

```
‘‘Pahāya <pb ed="P" n="0.0083" /> mātāpitaro, bhaginī ñātibhātaro;
```

```
Pañca kāmaguṇe hitvā, anuruddhova jhāyatu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§893.</p>

```
‘‘Sameto naccagītehi, sammatāḷappabodhano;
```

```
Na tena suddhimajjhagaṃ <note>suddhamajjhagā (sī. ka.), suddhimajjhagamā (syā.)</note>, mārassa visaye rato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§894.</p>

```
‘‘Etañca samatikkamma, rato buddhassa sāsane;
```

```
Sabboghaṃ samatikkamma, anuruddhova jhāyati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§895.</p>

```
‘‘Rūpā saddā rasā gandhā, phoṭṭhabbā ca manoramā;
```

```
Ete ca samatikkamma, anuruddhova jhāyati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§896.</p>

```
‘‘Piṇḍapātapaṭikkanto, eko adutiyo muni;
```

```
Esati paṃsukūlāni, anuruddho anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§897.</p>

```
‘‘Vicinī aggahī dhovi, rajayī dhārayī muni;
```

```
Paṃsukūlāni matimā, anuruddho anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§898.</p>

```
‘‘Mahiccho <pb ed="T" n="0.0392" /> ca asantuṭṭho, saṃsaṭṭho yo ca uddhato;
```

```
Tassa dhammā ime honti, pāpakā saṃkilesikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§899.</p>

```
‘‘Sato ca hoti appiccho, santuṭṭho avighātavā;
```

```
Pavivekarato vitto, niccamāraddhavīriyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§900.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa <pb ed="V" n="0.0269" /> dhammā ime honti, kusalā bodhipakkhikā;
```

```
Anāsavo ca so hoti, iti vuttaṃ mahesinā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§901.</p>

```
‘‘Mama saṅkappamaññāya, satthā loke anuttaro;
```

```
Manomayena kāyena, iddhiyā upasaṅkami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§902.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā me ahu saṅkappo, tato uttari desayi;
```

```
Nippapañcarato buddho, nippapañcamadesayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§903.</p>

```
‘‘Tassāhaṃ dhammamaññāya, vihāsiṃ sāsane rato;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§904.</p>

```
‘‘Pañcapaññāsavassāni<pb ed="M" n="0.0337" />, yato nesajjiko ahaṃ;
```

```
Pañcavīsativassāni, yato middhaṃ samūhataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§905.</p>

```
<note>dī. ni. 2.222</note> ‘‘Nāhu assāsapassāsā, ṭhitacittassa tādino;
```

```
Anejo santimārabbha, cakkhumā parinibbuto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§906.</p>

```
<note>dī. ni. 2.222</note> ‘‘Asallīnena cittena, vedanaṃ ajjhavāsayi;
```

```
Pajjotasseva nibbānaṃ, vimokkho cetaso ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§907.</p>

```
‘‘Ete pacchimakā dāni, munino phassapañcamā;
```

```
Nāññe <pb ed="T" n="0.0393" /> dhammā bhavissanti, sambuddhe parinibbute.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§908.</p>

```
‘‘Natthi dāni punāvāso, devakāyasmi jālini;
```

```
Vikkhīṇo jātisaṃsāro, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§909.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa <pb ed="P" n="0.0084" /> muhuttena sahassadhā, loko saṃvidito sabrahmakappo;
```

```
Vasī iddhiguṇe cutūpapāte, kāle passati devatā sa bhikkhu <note>sabhikkhuno (sī. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§910.</p>

```
‘‘Annabhāro <note>annahāro (sī.)</note> pure āsiṃ, daliddo ghāsahārako;
```

```
Samaṇaṃ paṭipādesiṃ, upariṭṭhaṃ yasassinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§911.</p>

```
‘‘Somhi sakyakule jāto, anuruddhoti maṃ vidū;
```

```
Upeto naccagītehi, sammatāḷappabodhano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§912.</p>

```
‘‘Athaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ, satthāraṃ akutobhayaṃ;
```

```
Tasmiṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§913.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi, yattha me vusitaṃ pure;
```

```
Tāvatiṃsesu devesu, aṭṭhāsiṃ sakkajātiyā <note>satajātiyā (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§914.</p>

```
‘‘Sattakkhattuṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0270" /> manussindo, ahaṃ rajjamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Cāturanto vijitāvī, jambusaṇḍassa issaro;
```

```
Adaṇḍena asatthena, dhammena anusāsayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§915.</p>

```
‘‘Ito satta tato satta, saṃsārāni catuddasa;
```

```
Nivāsamabhijānissaṃ, devaloke ṭhitā tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§916.</p>

```
‘‘Pañcaṅgike <pb ed="T" n="0.0394" /><pb ed="M" n="0.0338" /> samādhimhi, sante ekodibhāvite;
```

```
Paṭippassaddhiladdhamhi, dibbacakkhu visujjhi me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§917.</p>

```
‘‘Cutūpapātaṃ jānāmi, sattānaṃ āgatiṃ gatiṃ;
```

```
Itthabhāvaññathābhāvaṃ, jhāne pañcaṅgike ṭhito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§918.</p>

```
‘‘Pariciṇṇo mayā satthā…pe… bhavanetti samūhatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§919.</p>

```
‘‘Vajjīnaṃ veḷuvagāme, ahaṃ jīvitasaṅkhayā;
```

```
Heṭṭhato veḷugumbasmiṃ, nibbāyissaṃ anāsavo’’ti.
```

… Anuruddho thero….

#### 10. Pārāpariyattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§920.</p>

```
Samaṇassa ahu cintā, pupphitamhi mahāvane;
```

```
Ekaggassa nisinnassa, pavivittassa jhāyino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§921.</p>

```
‘‘Aññathā lokanāthamhi, tiṭṭhante purisuttame;
```

```
Iriyaṃ āsi bhikkhūnaṃ, aññathā dāni dissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§922.</p>

```
‘‘Sītavātaparittānaṃ, hirikopīnachādanaṃ;
```

```
Mattaṭṭhiyaṃ abhuñjiṃsu, santuṭṭhā itarītare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§923.</p>

```
‘‘Paṇītaṃ yadi vā lūkhaṃ, appaṃ vā yadi vā bahuṃ;
```

```
Yāpanatthaṃ abhuñjiṃsu, agiddhā nādhimucchitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§924.</p>

```
‘‘Jīvitānaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0085" /> parikkhāre, bhesajje atha paccaye;
```

```
Na bāḷhaṃ ussukā āsuṃ, yathā te āsavakkhaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§925.</p>

```
‘‘Araññe rukkhamūlesu, kandarāsu guhāsu ca;
```

```
Vivekamanubrūhantā, vihaṃsu tapparāyanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§926.</p>

```
‘‘Nīcā <pb ed="T" n="0.0395" /> niviṭṭhā subharā, mudū atthaddhamānasā;
```

```
Abyāsekā amukharā, atthacintā vasānugā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§927.</p>

```
‘‘Tato <pb ed="V" n="0.0271" /> pāsādikaṃ āsi, gataṃ bhuttaṃ nisevitaṃ;
```

```
Siniddhā teladhārāva, ahosi iriyāpatho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§928.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā, mahājhāyī mahāhitā;
```

```
Nibbutā dāni te therā, parittā dāni tādisā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§929.</p>

```
‘‘Kusalānañca <pb ed="M" n="0.0339" /> dhammānaṃ, paññāya ca parikkhayā;
```

```
Sabbākāravarūpetaṃ, lujjate jinasāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§930.</p>

```
‘‘Pāpakānañca dhammānaṃ, kilesānañca yo utu;
```

```
Upaṭṭhitā vivekāya, ye ca saddhammasesakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§931.</p>

```
‘‘Te kilesā pavaḍḍhantā, āvisanti bahuṃ janaṃ;
```

```
Kīḷanti maññe bālehi, ummattehiva rakkhasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§932.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesehābhibhūtā te, tena tena vidhāvitā;
```

```
Narā kilesavatthūsu, sasaṅgāmeva ghosite.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§933.</p>

```
‘‘Pariccajitvā saddhammaṃ, aññamaññehi bhaṇḍare;
```

```
Diṭṭhigatāni anventā, idaṃ seyyoti maññare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§934.</p>

```
‘‘Dhanañca puttaṃ bhariyañca, chaḍḍayitvāna niggatā;
```

```
Kaṭacchubhikkhahetūpi, akicchāni nisevare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§935.</p>

```
‘‘Udarāvadehakaṃ bhutvā, sayantuttānaseyyakā;
```

```
Kathaṃ vattenti <note>kathā vaḍḍhenti (sī. ka.)</note> paṭibuddhā, yā kathā satthugarahitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§936.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbakārukasippāni<pb ed="T" n="0.0396" />, cittiṃ katvāna <note>cittīkatvāna (sī.), cittaṃ katvāna (syā.)</note> sikkhare;
```

```
Avūpasantā ajjhattaṃ, sāmaññatthoti acchati <note>tiriñcati (?)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§937.</p>

```
‘‘Mattikaṃ telacuṇṇañca, udakāsanabhojanaṃ;
```

```
Gihīnaṃ upanāmenti, ākaṅkhantā bahuttaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§938.</p>

```
‘‘Dantaponaṃ kapitthañca, pupphaṃ khādaniyāni ca;
```

```
Piṇḍapāte ca sampanne, ambe āmalakāni ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§939.</p>

```
‘‘Bhesajjesu yathā vejjā, kiccākicce yathā gihī;
```

```
Gaṇikāva vibhūsāyaṃ, issare khattiyā yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§940.</p>

```
‘‘Nekatikā <pb ed="P" n="0.0086" /> vañcanikā, kūṭasakkhī apāṭukā;
```

```
Bahūhi parikappehi, āmisaṃ paribhuñjare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§941.</p>

```
‘‘Lesakappe pariyāye, parikappenudhāvitā;
```

```
Jīvikatthā upāyena, saṅkaḍḍhanti bahuṃ dhanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§942.</p>

```
‘‘Upaṭṭhāpenti <pb ed="M" n="0.0340" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0272" /> parisaṃ, kammato no ca dhammato;
```

```
Dhammaṃ paresaṃ desenti, lābhato no ca atthato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§943.</p>

```
‘‘Saṅghalābhassa bhaṇḍanti, saṅghato paribāhirā;
```

```
Paralābhopajīvantā, ahirīkā na lajjare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§944.</p>

```
‘‘Nānuyuttā tathā eke, muṇḍā saṅghāṭipārutā;
```

```
Sambhāvanaṃyevicchanti, lābhasakkāramucchitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§945.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ nānappayātamhi, na dāni sukaraṃ tathā;
```

```
Aphusitaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0397" /> vā phusituṃ, phusitaṃ vānurakkhituṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§946.</p>

```
‘‘Yathā kaṇṭakaṭṭhānamhi, careyya anupāhano;
```

```
Satiṃ upaṭṭhapetvāna, evaṃ gāme munī care.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§947.</p>

```
‘‘Saritvā pubbake yogī, tesaṃ vattamanussaraṃ;
```

```
Kiñcāpi pacchimo kālo, phuseyya amataṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§948.</p>

```
‘‘Idaṃ vatvā sālavane, samaṇo bhāvitindriyo;
```

```
Brāhmaṇo parinibbāyī, isi khīṇapunabbhavo’’ti.
```

… Pārāpariyo <note>pārāsariyo (syā.)</note> thero….

<trailer rend="centre">Vīsatinipāto niṭṭhito.</trailer>

Tatruddānaṃ –

```
Adhimutto pārāpariyo, telakāni raṭṭhapālo;
```

```
Mālukyaselo bhaddiyo, aṅguli dibbacakkhuko.
```

```
Pārāpariyo dasete, vīsamhi parikittitā;
```

```
Gāthāyo dve satā honti, pañcatālīsa <note>244 gāthāyoyeva dissanti</note> uttarinti.
```

### 17. Tiṃsanipāto

#### 1. Phussattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§949.</p>

```
Pāsādike <pb ed="M" n="0.0341" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0273" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0087" /> bahū disvā, bhāvitatte susaṃvute;
```

```
Isi paṇḍarasagotto <note>paṇḍarassa gotto (sī.)</note>, apucchi phussasavhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§950.</p>

```
‘‘Kiṃchandā <pb ed="T" n="0.0398" /> kimadhippāyā, kimākappā bhavissare;
```

```
Anāgatamhi kālamhi, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§951.</p>

```
‘‘Suṇohi vacanaṃ mayhaṃ, isipaṇḍarasavhaya;
```

```
Sakkaccaṃ upadhārehi, ācikkhissāmyanāgataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§952.</p>

```
‘‘Kodhanā upanāhī ca, makkhī thambhī saṭhā bahū;
```

```
Ussukī nānāvādā ca, bhavissanti anāgate.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§953.</p>

```
‘‘Aññātamānino dhamme, gambhīre tīragocarā;
```

```
Lahukā agaru dhamme, aññamaññamagāravā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§954.</p>

```
‘‘Bahū ādīnavā loke, uppajjissantyanāgate;
```

```
Sudesitaṃ imaṃ dhammaṃ, kilesessanti <note>kilesissanti (sī.), kilisissanti (syā. ka.)</note> dummatī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§955.</p>

```
‘‘Guṇahīnāpi saṅghamhi, voharantā visāradā;
```

```
Balavanto bhavissanti, mukharā assutāvino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§956.</p>

```
‘‘Guṇavantopi saṅghamhi, voharantā yathātthato;
```

```
Dubbalā te bhavissanti, hirīmanā anatthikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§957.</p>

```
‘‘Rajataṃ jātarūpañca, khettaṃ vatthumajeḷakaṃ;
```

```
Dāsidāsañca dummedhā, sādiyissantyanāgate.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§958.</p>

```
‘‘Ujjhānasaññino bālā, sīlesu asamāhitā;
```

```
Unnaḷā vicarissanti, kalahābhiratā magā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§959.</p>

```
‘‘Uddhatā ca bhavissanti, nīlacīvarapārutā;
```

```
Kuhā <pb ed="T" n="0.0399" /> thaddhā lapā siṅgī, carissantyariyā viya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§960.</p>

```
‘‘Telasaṇṭhehi kesehi, capalā añjanakkhikā;
```

```
Rathiyāya gamissanti, dantavaṇṇikapārutā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§961.</p>

```
‘‘Ajegucchaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0342" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0274" /> vimuttehi, surattaṃ arahaddhajaṃ;
```

```
Jigucchissanti kāsāvaṃ, odātesu samucchitā <note>odāte susamucchitā (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§962.</p>

```
‘‘Lābhakāmā bhavissanti, kusītā hīnavīriyā;
```

```
Kicchantā vanapatthāni, gāmantesu vasissare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§963.</p>

```
‘‘Ye <pb ed="P" n="0.0088" /> ye lābhaṃ labhissanti, micchājīvaratā sadā;
```

```
Te teva anusikkhantā, bhajissanti asaṃyatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§964.</p>

```
‘‘Ye ye alābhino lābhaṃ, na te pujjā bhavissare;
```

```
Supesalepi te dhīre, sevissanti na te tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§965.</p>

```
‘‘Milakkhurajanaṃ rattaṃ <note>pilakkharajanaṃ rattaṃ (?)</note>, garahantā sakaṃ dhajaṃ;
```

```
Titthiyānaṃ dhajaṃ keci, dhārissantyavadātakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§966.</p>

```
‘‘Agāravo ca kāsāve, tadā tesaṃ bhavissati;
```

```
Paṭisaṅkhā ca kāsāve, bhikkhūnaṃ na bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§967.</p>

```
‘‘Abhibhūtassa dukkhena, sallaviddhassa ruppato;
```

```
Paṭisaṅkhā mahāghorā, nāgassāsi acintiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§968.</p>

```
‘‘Chaddanto hi tadā disvā, surattaṃ arahaddhajaṃ;
```

```
Tāvadeva bhaṇī gāthā, gajo atthopasaṃhitā’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§969.</p>

```
<note>dha. pa. 9; jā. 1.2.141; 1.16.122</note> ‘‘Anikkasāvo <pb ed="T" n="0.0400" /> kāsāvaṃ, yo vatthaṃ paridhassati <note>paridahissati (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Apeto damasaccena, na so kāsāvamarahati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§970.</p>

```
‘‘Yo ca vantakāsāvassa, sīlesu susamāhito;
```

```
Upeto damasaccena, sa ve kāsāvamarahati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§971.</p>

```
‘‘Vipannasīlo dummedho, pākaṭo kāmakāriyo;
```

```
Vibbhantacitto nissukko, na so kāsāvamarahati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§972.</p>

```
‘‘Yo ca sīlena sampanno, vītarāgo samāhito;
```

```
Odātamanasaṅkappo, sa ve kāsāvamarahati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§973.</p>

```
‘‘Uddhato unnaḷo bālo, sīlaṃ yassa na vijjati;
```

```
Odātakaṃ arahati, kāsāvaṃ kiṃ karissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§974.</p>

```
‘‘Bhikkhū <pb ed="M" n="0.0343" /> ca bhikkhuniyo ca, duṭṭhacittā anādarā;
```

```
Tādīnaṃ mettacittānaṃ, niggaṇhissantyanāgate.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§975.</p>

```
‘‘Sikkhāpentāpi therehi, bālā cīvaradhāraṇaṃ;
```

```
Na suṇissanti dummedhā, pākaṭā kāmakāriyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§976.</p>

```
‘‘Te <pb ed="V" n="0.0275" /> tathā sikkhitā bālā, aññamaññaṃ agāravā;
```

```
Nādiyissantupajjhāye, khaḷuṅko viya sārathiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§977.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ anāgataddhānaṃ, paṭipatti bhavissati;
```

```
Bhikkhūnaṃ bhikkhunīnañca, patte kālamhi pacchime.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§978.</p>

```
‘‘Purā āgacchate etaṃ, anāgataṃ mahabbhayaṃ;
```

```
Subbacā hotha sakhilā, aññamaññaṃ sagāravā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§979.</p>

```
‘‘Mettacittā <pb ed="T" n="0.0401" /> kāruṇikā, hotha sīlesu saṃvutā;
```

```
Āraddhavīriyā pahitattā, niccaṃ daḷhaparakkamā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§980.</p>

```
‘‘Pamādaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0089" /> bhayato disvā, appamādañca khemato;
```

```
Bhāvethaṭṭhaṅgikaṃ maggaṃ, phusantā amataṃ pada’’nti.
```

… Phusso thero….

#### 2. Sāriputtattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§981.</p>

```
‘‘Yathācārī yathāsato satīmā, yatasaṅkappajjhāyi appamatto;
```

```
Ajjhattarato samāhitatto, eko santusito tamāhu bhikkhuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§982.</p>

```
‘‘Allaṃ sukkhaṃ vā bhuñjanto, na bāḷhaṃ suhito siyā;
```

```
Ūnūdaro mitāhāro, sato bhikkhu paribbaje.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§983.</p>

```
‘‘Cattāro pañca ālope, abhutvā udakaṃ pive;
```

```
Alaṃ phāsuvihārāya, pahitattassa bhikkhuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§984.</p>

```
‘‘Kappiyaṃ taṃ ce chādeti, cīvaraṃ idamatthikaṃ <note>idamatthitaṃ (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Alaṃ phāsuvihārāya, pahitattassa bhikkhuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§985.</p>

```
‘‘Pallaṅkena <pb ed="M" n="0.0344" /> nisinnassa, jaṇṇuke nābhivassati;
```

```
Alaṃ phāsuvihārāya, pahitattassa bhikkhuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§986.</p>

```
<note>saṃ. ni. 4.253; itivu. 53</note> ‘‘Yo sukhaṃ dukkhato adda, dukkhamaddakkhi sallato;
```

```
Ubhayantarena <pb ed="T" n="0.0402" /> <note>ubhayamantare (sī.)</note> nāhosi, kena lokasmi kiṃ siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§987.</p>

```
‘‘Mā me kadāci pāpiccho, kusīto hīnavīriyo;
```

```
Appassuto anādaro, kena lokasmi kiṃ siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§988.</p>

```
‘‘Bahussuto <pb ed="V" n="0.0276" /> ca medhāvī, sīlesu susamāhito;
```

```
Cetosamathamanuyutto, api muddhani tiṭṭhatu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§989.</p>

```
‘‘Yo papañcamanuyutto, papañcābhirato mago;
```

```
Virādhayī so nibbānaṃ, yogakkhemaṃ anuttaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§990.</p>

```
‘‘Yo ca papañcaṃ hitvāna, nippapañcapathe rato;
```

```
Ārādhayī so nibbānaṃ, yogakkhemaṃ anuttaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§991.</p>

```
<note>dha. pa. 98</note> ‘‘Gāme vā yadi vāraññe, ninne vā yadi vā thale;
```

```
Yattha arahanto viharanti, taṃ bhūmirāmaṇeyyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§992.</p>

```
‘‘Ramaṇīyāni araññāni, yattha na ramatī jano;
```

```
Vītarāgā ramissanti, na te kāmagavesino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§993.</p>

```
<note>dha. pa. 76</note> ‘‘Nidhīnaṃva pavattāraṃ, yaṃ passe vajjadassinaṃ;
```

```
Niggayhavādiṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0090" /> medhāviṃ, tādisaṃ paṇḍitaṃ bhaje;
```

```
Tādisaṃ bhajamānassa, seyyo hoti na pāpiyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§994.</p>

```
<note>dha. pa. 77</note> ‘‘Ovadeyyānusāseyya, asabbhā ca nivāraye;
```

```
Satañhi so piyo hoti, asataṃ hoti appiyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§995.</p>

```
‘‘Aññassa bhagavā buddho, dhammaṃ desesi cakkhumā;
```

```
Dhamme <pb ed="T" n="0.0403" /> desiyamānamhi, sotamodhesimatthiko;
```

```
Taṃ me amoghaṃ savanaṃ, vimuttomhi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§996.</p>

```
‘‘Neva pubbenivāsāya, napi dibbassa cakkhuno;
```

```
Cetopariyāya iddhiyā, cutiyā upapattiyā;
```

```
Sotadhātuvisuddhiyā, paṇidhī me na vijjati <note>kathā. 378</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§997.</p>

```
‘‘Rukkhamūlaṃva <pb ed="M" n="0.0345" /> nissāya, muṇḍo saṅghāṭipāruto;
```

```
Paññāya uttamo thero, upatissova <note>upatisso ca (sī. ka.)</note> jhāyati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§998.</p>

```
‘‘Avitakkaṃ samāpanno, sammāsambuddhasāvako;
```

```
Ariyena tuṇhībhāvena, upeto hoti tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§999.</p>

```
<note>udā. 24</note> ‘‘Yathāpi pabbato selo, acalo suppatiṭṭhito;
```

```
Evaṃ mohakkhayā bhikkhu, pabbatova na vedhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1000.</p>

```
‘‘Anaṅgaṇassa posassa, niccaṃ sucigavesino;
```

```
Vālaggamattaṃ pāpassa, abbhamattaṃva khāyati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1001.</p>

```
‘‘Nābhinandāmi <pb ed="V" n="0.0277" /> maraṇaṃ, nābhinandāmi jīvitaṃ;
```

```
Nikkhipissaṃ imaṃ kāyaṃ, sampajāno patissato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1002.</p>

```
‘‘Nābhinandāmi maraṇaṃ, nābhinandāmi jīvitaṃ;
```

```
Kālañca paṭikaṅkhāmi, nibbisaṃ bhatako yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1003.</p>

```
‘‘Ubhayena midaṃ maraṇameva, nāmaraṇaṃ pacchā vā pure vā;
```

```
Paṭipajjatha mā vinassatha, khaṇo vo mā upaccagā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1004.</p>

```
‘‘Nagaraṃ yathā paccantaṃ, guttaṃ santarabāhiraṃ;
```

```
Evaṃ gopetha attānaṃ, khaṇo vo mā upaccagā;
```

```
Khaṇātītā <pb ed="T" n="0.0404" /> hi socanti, nirayamhi samappitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1005.</p>

```
‘‘Upasanto uparato, mantabhāṇī <note>mattabhāṇī (sī.)</note> anuddhato;
```

```
Dhunāti pāpake dhamme, dumapattaṃva māluto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1006.</p>

```
‘‘Upasanto uparato, mantabhāṇī anuddhato;
```

```
Appāsi <note>abbahi (syā.), abhāsi (?)</note> pāpake dhamme, dumapattaṃva māluto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1007.</p>

```
‘‘Upasanto <pb ed="P" n="0.0091" /> anāyāso, vippasanno anāvilo;
```

```
Kalyāṇasīlo medhāvī, dukkhassantakaro siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1008.</p>

```
‘‘Na vissase ekatiyesu evaṃ, agārisu pabbajitesu cāpi;
```

```
Sādhūpi hutvā na asādhu honti, asādhu hutvā puna sādhu honti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1009.</p>

```
‘‘Kāmacchando <pb ed="M" n="0.0346" /> ca byāpādo, thinamiddhañca bhikkhuno;
```

```
Uddhaccaṃ vicikicchā ca, pañcete cittakelisā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1010.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa sakkariyamānassa, asakkārena cūbhayaṃ;
```

```
Samādhi na vikampati, appamādavihārino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1011.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ jhāyinaṃ sātatikaṃ, sukhumadiṭṭhivipassakaṃ;
```

```
Upādānakkhayārāmaṃ, āhu sappuriso iti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1012.</p>

```
‘‘Mahāsamuddo pathavī, pabbato anilopi ca;
```

```
Upamāya na yujjanti, satthu varavimuttiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1013.</p>

```
‘‘Cakkānuvattako <pb ed="T" n="0.0405" /> thero, mahāñāṇī samāhito;
```

```
Pathavāpaggisamāno, na rajjati na dussati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1014.</p>

```
‘‘Paññāpāramitaṃ patto, mahābuddhi mahāmati;
```

```
Ajaḷo jaḷasamāno, sadā carati nibbuto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1015.</p>

```
‘‘Pariciṇṇo mayā satthā…pe… bhavanetti samūhatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1016.</p>

```
‘‘Sampādethappamādena<pb ed="V" n="0.0278" />, esā me anusāsanī;
```

```
Handāhaṃ parinibbissaṃ, vippamuttomhi sabbadhī’’ti.
```

… Sāriputto thero….

#### 3. Ānandattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§1017.</p>

```
‘‘Pisuṇena ca kodhanena ca, maccharinā ca vibhūtanandinā;
```

```
Sakhitaṃ na kareyya paṇḍito, pāpo kāpurisena saṅgamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1018.</p>

```
‘‘Saddhena ca pesalena ca, paññavatā bahussutena ca;
```

```
Sakhitaṃ kareyya paṇḍito, bhaddo sappurisena saṅgamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1019.</p>

```
‘‘Passa cittakataṃ bimbaṃ…pe… yassa natthi dhuvaṃ ṭhiti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1020.</p>

```
‘‘Passa cittakataṃ bimbaṃ…pe… vatthehi sobhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1021.</p>

```
‘‘Alattakakatā <pb ed="M" n="0.0347" /> …pe… no ca pāragavesino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1022.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhapadakatā…pe… no ca pāragavesino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1023.</p>

```
‘‘Añjanīva navā…pe… no ca pāragavesino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1024.</p>

```
‘‘Bahussuto cittakathī, buddhassa paricārako;
```

```
Pannabhāro visaññutto, seyyaṃ kappeti gotamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1025.</p>

```
‘‘Khīṇāsavo visaññutto, saṅgātīto sunibbuto;
```

```
Dhāreti antimaṃ dehaṃ, jātimaraṇapāragū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1026.</p>

```
‘‘Yasmiṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0092" /> patiṭṭhitā dhammā, buddhassādiccabandhuno;
```

```
Nibbānagamane magge, soyaṃ tiṭṭhati gotamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1027.</p>

```
‘‘Dvāsīti <pb ed="T" n="0.0406" /> buddhato gaṇhiṃ, dve sahassāni bhikkhuto;
```

```
Caturāsītisahassāni, ye me dhammā pavattino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1028.</p>

```
‘‘Appassutāyaṃ puriso, balibaddova jīrati;
```

```
Maṃsāni tassa vaḍḍhanti, paññā tassa na vaḍḍhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1029.</p>

```
‘‘Bahussuto appassutaṃ, yo sutenātimaññati;
```

```
Andho padīpadhārova, tatheva paṭibhāti maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1030.</p>

```
‘‘Bahussutaṃ upāseyya, sutañca na vināsaye;
```

```
Taṃ mūlaṃ brahmacariyassa, tasmā dhammadharo siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1031.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbāparaññū atthaññū, niruttipadakovido;
```

```
Suggahītañca gaṇhāti, atthañcopaparikkhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1032.</p>

```
‘‘Khantyā <pb ed="V" n="0.0279" /> chandikato <note>khantiyā chandito (?)</note> hoti, ussahitvā tuleti taṃ;
```

```
Samaye so padahati, ajjhattaṃ susamāhito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1033.</p>

```
‘‘Bahussutaṃ dhammadharaṃ, sappaññaṃ buddhasāvakaṃ;
```

```
Dhammaviññāṇamākaṅkhaṃ, taṃ bhajetha tathāvidhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1034.</p>

```
‘‘Bahussuto dhammadharo, kosārakkho mahesino;
```

```
Cakkhu sabbassa lokassa, pūjanīyo bahussuto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1035.</p>

```
‘‘Dhammārāmo dhammarato, dhammaṃ anuvicintayaṃ;
```

```
Dhammaṃ anussaraṃ bhikkhu, saddhammā na parihāyati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1036.</p>

```
‘‘Kāyamaccheragaruno <pb ed="M" n="0.0348" /> <note>garuko (sī.)</note>, hiyyamāne <note>hiyyamāno (sī.)</note> anuṭṭhahe;
```

```
Sarīrasukhagiddhassa, kuto samaṇaphāsutā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1037.</p>

```
‘‘Na <pb ed="T" n="0.0407" /> pakkhanti disā sabbā, dhammā na paṭibhanti maṃ;
```

```
Gate kalyāṇamittamhi, andhakāraṃva khāyati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1038.</p>

```
‘‘Abbhatītasahāyassa, atītagatasatthuno;
```

```
Natthi etādisaṃ mittaṃ, yathā kāyagatā sati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1039.</p>

```
‘‘Ye purāṇā atītā te, navehi na sameti me;
```

```
Svajja ekova jhāyāmi, vassupetova pakkhimā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1040.</p>

```
‘‘Dassanāya abhikkante, nānāverajjake bahū;
```

```
Mā vārayittha sotāro, passantu samayo mamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1041.</p>

```
‘‘Dassanāya <pb ed="P" n="0.0093" /> abhikkante, nānāverajjake puthu;
```

```
Karoti satthā okāsaṃ, na nivāreti cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1042.</p>

```
‘‘Paṇṇavīsativassāni, sekhabhūtassa me sato;
```

```
Na kāmasaññā uppajji, passa dhammasudhammataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1043.</p>

```
‘‘Paṇṇavīsativassāni, sekhabhūtassa me sato;
```

```
Na dosasaññā uppajji, passa dhammasudhammataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1044.</p>

```
‘‘Paṇṇavīsativassāni, bhagavantaṃ upaṭṭhahiṃ;
```

```
Mettena kāyakammena, chāyāva anapāyinī <note>anupāyinī (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1045.</p>

```
‘‘Paṇṇavīsativassāni, bhagavantaṃ upaṭṭhahiṃ;
```

```
Mettena vacīkammena, chāyāva anapāyinī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1046.</p>

```
‘‘Paṇṇavīsativassāni, bhagavantaṃ upaṭṭhahiṃ;
```

```
Mettena manokammena, chāyāva anapāyinī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1047.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhassa <pb ed="T" n="0.0408" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0280" /> caṅkamantassa, piṭṭhito anucaṅkamiṃ;
```

```
Dhamme desiyamānamhi, ñāṇaṃ me udapajjatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1048.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ sakaraṇīyomhi, sekho appattamānaso;
```

```
Satthu ca parinibbānaṃ, yo amhaṃ anukampako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1049.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāsi <pb ed="M" n="0.0349" /> yaṃ bhiṃsanakaṃ, tadāsi lomahaṃsanaṃ;
```

```
Sabbākāravarūpete, sambuddhe parinibbute.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1050.</p>

```
‘‘Bahussuto dhammadharo, kosārakkho mahesino;
```

```
Cakkhu sabbassa lokassa, ānando parinibbuto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1051.</p>

```
‘‘Bahussuto dhammadharo, kosārakkho mahesino;
```

```
Cakkhu sabbassa lokassa, andhakāre tamonudo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1052.</p>

```
‘‘Gatimanto satimanto, dhitimanto ca yo isi;
```

```
Saddhammadhārako thero, ānando ratanākaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1053.</p>

```
‘‘Pariciṇṇo mayā satthā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ;
```

```
Ohito garuko bhāro, natthi dāni punabbhavo’’ti.
```

… Ānando thero….

<trailer rend="centre">Tiṃsanipāto niṭṭhito.</trailer>

Tatruddānaṃ –

```
Phussopatisso ānando, tayotime pakittitā;
```

```
Gāthāyo tattha saṅkhātā, sataṃ pañca ca uttarīti;
```

### 18. Cattālīsanipāto

#### 1. Mahākassapattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§1054.</p>

```
‘‘Na <pb ed="T" n="0.0409" /><pb ed="M" n="0.0350" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0281" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0094" /> gaṇena purakkhato care, vimano hoti samādhi dullabho;
```

```
Nānājanasaṅgaho dukho, iti disvāna gaṇaṃ na rocaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1055.</p>

```
‘‘Na kulāni upabbaje muni, vimano hoti samādhi dullabho;
```

```
So ussukko rasānugiddho, atthaṃ riñcati yo sukhāvaho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1056.</p>

```
‘‘Paṅkoti hi naṃ avedayuṃ, yāyaṃ vandanapūjanā kulesu;
```

```
Sukhumaṃ salla durubbahaṃ, sakkāro kāpurisena dujjaho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1057.</p>

```
‘‘Senāsanamhā oruyha, nagaraṃ piṇḍāya pāvisiṃ;
```

```
Bhuñjantaṃ purisaṃ kuṭṭhiṃ, sakkaccaṃ taṃ upaṭṭhahiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1058.</p>

```
‘‘So me <note>taṃ (sī. ka.)</note> pakkena hatthena, ālopaṃ upanāmayi;
```

```
Ālopaṃ pakkhipantassa, aṅguli cettha <note>pettha (sī. ka.)</note> chijjatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1059.</p>

```
‘‘Kuṭṭamūlañca <note>kuḍḍamūlañca (sī. syā.)</note> nissāya, ālopaṃ taṃ abhuñjisaṃ;
```

```
Bhuñjamāne vā bhutte vā, jegucchaṃ me na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1060.</p>

```
‘‘Uttiṭṭhapiṇḍo āhāro, pūtimuttañca osadhaṃ;
```

```
Senāsanaṃ rukkhamūlaṃ, paṃsukūlañca cīvaraṃ;
```

```
Yassete abhisambhutvā <note>abhibhuñjati (?)</note>, sa ve cātuddiso naro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1061.</p>

```
‘‘Yattha eke vihaññanti, āruhantā siluccayaṃ;
```

```
Tassa buddhassa dāyādo, sampajāno patissato;
```

```
Iddhibalenupatthaddho<pb ed="T" n="0.0410" />, kassapo abhirūhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1062.</p>

```
‘‘Piṇḍapātapaṭikkanto<pb ed="M" n="0.0351" />, selamāruyha kassapo;
```

```
Jhāyati anupādāno, pahīnabhayabheravo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1063.</p>

```
‘‘Piṇḍapātapaṭikkanto, selamāruyha kassapo;
```

```
Jhāyati anupādāno, ḍayhamānesu nibbuto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1064.</p>

```
‘‘Piṇḍapātapaṭikkanto, selamāruyha kassapo;
```

```
Jhāyati anupādāno, katakicco anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1065.</p>

```
‘‘Karerimālāvitatā<pb ed="V" n="0.0282" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0095" />, bhūmibhāgā manoramā;
```

```
Kuñjarābhirudā rammā, te selā ramayanti maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1066.</p>

```
‘‘Nīlabbhavaṇṇā rucirā, vārisītā sucindharā;
```

```
Indagopakasañchannā, te selā ramayanti maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1067.</p>

```
‘‘Nīlabbhakūṭasadisā, kūṭāgāravarūpamā;
```

```
Vāraṇābhirudā rammā, te selā ramayanti maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1068.</p>

```
‘‘Abhivuṭṭhā rammatalā, nagā isibhi sevitā;
```

```
Abbhunnaditā sikhīhi, te selā ramayanti maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1069.</p>

```
‘‘Alaṃ jhāyitukāmassa, pahitattassa me sato;
```

```
Alaṃ me atthakāmassa <note>attakāmassa (?)</note>, pahitattassa bhikkhuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1070.</p>

```
‘‘Alaṃ me phāsukāmassa, pahitattassa bhikkhuno;
```

```
Alaṃ me yogakāmassa, pahitattassa tādino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1071.</p>

```
‘‘Umāpupphena samānā, gaganāvabbhachāditā;
```

```
Nānādijagaṇākiṇṇā<pb ed="T" n="0.0411" />, te selā ramayanti maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1072.</p>

```
‘‘Anākiṇṇā gahaṭṭhehi, migasaṅghanisevitā;
```

```
Nānādijagaṇākiṇṇā, te selā ramayanti maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1073.</p>

```
‘‘Acchodikā puthusilā, gonaṅgulamigāyutā;
```

```
Ambusevālasañchannā, te selā ramayanti maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1074.</p>

```
‘‘Na pañcaṅgikena turiyena, rati me hoti tādisī;
```

```
Yathā ekaggacittassa, sammā dhammaṃ vipassato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1075.</p>

```
‘‘Kammaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0352" /> bahukaṃ na kāraye, parivajjeyya janaṃ na uyyame;
```

```
Ussukko so rasānugiddho, atthaṃ riñcati yo sukhāvaho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1076.</p>

```
‘‘Kammaṃ bahukaṃ na kāraye, parivajjeyya anattaneyyametaṃ;
```

```
Kicchati kāyo kilamati, dukkhito so samathaṃ na vindati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1077.</p>

```
‘‘Oṭṭhappahatamattena, attānampi na passati;
```

```
Patthaddhagīvo carati, ahaṃ seyyoti maññati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1078.</p>

```
‘‘Aseyyo seyyasamānaṃ, bālo maññati attānaṃ;
```

```
Na taṃ viññū pasaṃsanti, patthaddhamānasaṃ naraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1079.</p>

```
‘‘Yo <pb ed="V" n="0.0283" /> ca seyyohamasmīti, nāhaṃ seyyoti vā pana;
```

```
Hīno taṃsadiso <note>tīnohaṃ sadiso (syā.)</note> vāti, vidhāsu na vikampati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1080.</p>

```
‘‘Paññavantaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0096" /> tathā tādiṃ, sīlesu susamāhitaṃ;
```

```
Cetosamathamanuttaṃ, tañce viññū pasaṃsare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1081.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa <pb ed="T" n="0.0412" /> sabrahmacārīsu, gāravo nūpalabbhati;
```

```
Ārakā hoti saddhammā, nabhato puthavī yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1082.</p>

```
‘‘Yesañca hiri ottappaṃ, sadā sammā upaṭṭhitaṃ;
```

```
Virūḷhabrahmacariyā te, tesaṃ khīṇā punabbhavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1083.</p>

```
‘‘Uddhato capalo bhikkhu, paṃsukūlena pāruto;
```

```
Kapīva sīhacammena, na so tenupasobhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1084.</p>

```
‘‘Anuddhato acapalo, nipako saṃvutindriyo;
```

```
Sobhati paṃsukūlena, sīhova girigabbhare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1085.</p>

```
‘‘Ete sambahulā devā, iddhimanto yasassino;
```

```
Dasadevasahassāni, sabbe te brahmakāyikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1086.</p>

```
‘‘Dhammasenāpatiṃ vīraṃ, mahājhāyiṃ samāhitaṃ;
```

```
Sāriputtaṃ namassantā, tiṭṭhanti pañjalīkatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1087.</p>

```
‘‘‘Namo <pb ed="M" n="0.0353" /> te purisājañña, namo te purisuttama;
```

```
Yassa te nābhijānāma, yampi nissāya jhāyati <note>jhāyasi (ka. aṭṭha.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1088.</p>

```
‘‘‘Accheraṃ vata buddhānaṃ, gambhīro gocaro sako;
```

```
Ye mayaṃ nābhijānāma, vālavedhisamāgatā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1089.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ tathā devakāyehi, pūjitaṃ pūjanārahaṃ;
```

```
Sāriputtaṃ tadā disvā, kappinassa sitaṃ ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1090.</p>

```
‘‘Yāvatā buddhakhettamhi, ṭhapayitvā mahāmuniṃ;
```

```
Dhutaguṇe visiṭṭhohaṃ, sadiso me na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1091.</p>

```
‘‘Pariciṇṇo <pb ed="T" n="0.0413" /> mayā satthā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ;
```

```
Ohito garuko bhāro, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1092.</p>

```
‘‘Na <pb ed="V" n="0.0284" /> cīvare na sayane, bhojane nupalimpati;
```

```
Gotamo anappameyyo, muḷālapupphaṃ vimalaṃva;
```

```
Ambunā nekkhammaninno, tibhavābhinissaṭo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1093.</p>

```
‘‘Satipaṭṭhānagīvo so, saddhāhattho mahāmuni;
```

```
Paññāsīso mahāñāṇī, sadā carati nibbuto’’ti.
```

… Mahākassapo thero….

<trailer rend="centre">Cattālīsanipāto niṭṭhito.</trailer>

Tatruddānaṃ –

```
Cattālīsanipātamhi, mahākassapasavhayo;
```

```
Ekova thero gāthāyo, cattāsīla duvepi cāti.
```

### 19. Paññāsanipāto

#### 1. Tālapuṭattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§1094.</p>

```
‘‘Kadā <pb ed="M" n="0.0354" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0285" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0097" /> nuhaṃ pabbatakandarāsu, ekākiyo addutiyo vihassaṃ;
```

```
Aniccato sabbabhavaṃ vipassaṃ, taṃ me idaṃ taṃ nu kadā bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1095.</p>

```
‘‘Kadā nuhaṃ bhinnapaṭandharo muni, kāsāvavattho <pb ed="T" n="0.0414" /> amamo nirāso;
```

```
Rāgañca dosañca tatheva mohaṃ, hantvā sukhī pavanagato vihassaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1096.</p>

```
‘‘Kadā aniccaṃ vadharoganīḷaṃ, kāyaṃ imaṃ maccujarāyupaddutaṃ;
```

```
Vipassamāno vītabhayo vihassaṃ, eko vane taṃ nu kadā bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1097.</p>

```
‘‘Kadā nuhaṃ bhayajananiṃ dukhāvahaṃ, taṇhālataṃ bahuvidhānuvattaniṃ;
```

```
Paññāmayaṃ tikhiṇamasiṃ gahetvā, chetvā vase tampi kadā bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1098.</p>

```
‘‘Kadā nu paññāmayamuggatejaṃ, satthaṃ isīnaṃ sahasādiyitvā;
```

```
Māraṃ sasenaṃ sahasā bhañjissaṃ, sīhāsane taṃ nu kadā bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1099.</p>

```
‘‘Kadā nuhaṃ sabbhi samāgamesu, diṭṭho bhave dhammagarūhi tādibhi;
```

```
Yāthāvadassīhi jitindriyehi, padhāniyo <pb ed="T" n="0.0415" /> taṃ nu kadā bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1100.</p>

```
‘‘Kadā nu maṃ tandi khudā pipāsā, vātātapā kīṭasarīsapā vā;
```

```
Na bādhayissanti na taṃ giribbaje, atthatthiyaṃ taṃ nu kadā bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1101.</p>

```
‘‘Kadā <pb ed="M" n="0.0355" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0098" /> nu kho yaṃ viditaṃ mahesinā, cattāri saccāni sududdasāni;
```

```
Samāhitatto satimā agacchaṃ, paññāya taṃ taṃ nu kadā bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1102.</p>

```
‘‘Kadā nu rūpe amite ca sadde, gandhe rase phusitabbe ca dhamme;
```

```
Ādittatohaṃ samathehi yutto, paññāya dacchaṃ tadidaṃ kadā me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1103.</p>

```
‘‘Kadā nuhaṃ dubbacanena vutto, tatonimittaṃ vimano na hessaṃ;
```

```
Atho pasatthopi tatonimittaṃ, tuṭṭho na hessaṃ tadidaṃ kadā me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1104.</p>

```
‘‘Kadā nu kaṭṭhe ca tiṇe latā ca, khandhe imehaṃ amite ca dhamme;
```

```
Ajjhattikāneva ca bāhirāni ca, samaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0416" /> tuleyyaṃ tadidaṃ kadā me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1105.</p>

```
‘‘Kadā nu maṃ pāvusakālamegho, navena toyena sacīvaraṃ vane;
```

```
Isippayātamhi pathe vajantaṃ, ovassate taṃ nu kadā bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1106.</p>

```
‘‘Kadā <pb ed="V" n="0.0286" /> mayūrassa sikhaṇḍino vane, dijassa sutvā girigabbhare rutaṃ;
```

```
Paccuṭṭhahitvā amatassa pattiyā, saṃcintaye taṃ nu kadā bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1107.</p>

```
‘‘Kadā nu gaṅgaṃ yamunaṃ sarassatiṃ, pātālakhittaṃ vaḷavāmukhañca <note>balavāmukhañca (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Asajjamāno patareyyamiddhiyā, vibhiṃsanaṃ taṃ nu kadā bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1108.</p>

```
‘‘Kadā <pb ed="M" n="0.0356" /> nu nāgova asaṅgacārī, padālaye kāmaguṇesu chandaṃ;
```

```
Nibbajjayaṃ sabbasubhaṃ nimittaṃ, jhāne yuto taṃ nu kadā bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1109.</p>

```
‘‘Kadā <pb ed="P" n="0.0099" /> iṇaṭṭova daliddako <note>daḷiddako (sī.)</note> nidhiṃ, ārādhayitvā dhanikehi pīḷito;
```

```
Tuṭṭho bhavissaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0417" /> adhigamma sāsanaṃ, mahesino taṃ nu kadā bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1110.</p>

```
‘‘Bahūni vassāni tayāmhi yācito, ‘agāravāsena alaṃ nu te idaṃ’;
```

```
Taṃ dāni maṃ pabbajitaṃ samānaṃ, kiṃkāraṇā citta tuvaṃ na yuñjasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1111.</p>

```
‘‘Nanu ahaṃ citta tayāmhi yācito, ‘giribbaje citrachadā vihaṅgamā’;
```

```
Mahindaghosatthanitābhigajjino, te taṃ ramessanti vanamhi jhāyinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1112.</p>

```
‘‘Kulamhi mitte ca piye ca ñātake, khiḍḍāratiṃ kāmaguṇañca loke;
```

```
Sabbaṃ pahāya imamajjhupāgato, athopi tvaṃ citta na mayha tussasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1113.</p>

```
‘‘Mameva etaṃ na hi tvaṃ paresaṃ, sannāhakāle paridevitena kiṃ;
```

```
Sabbaṃ idaṃ calamiti pekkhamāno, abhinikkhamiṃ amatapadaṃ jigīsaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1114.</p>

```
‘‘Suyuttavādī dvipadānamuttamo, mahābhisakko naradammasārathi <note>sārathī (sī.)</note>;
```

```
‘Cittaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0418" /> calaṃ makkaṭasannibhaṃ iti, avītarāgena sudunnivārayaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1115.</p>

```
‘‘Kāmā <pb ed="M" n="0.0357" /> hi citrā madhurā manoramā, aviddasū yattha sitā puthujjanā;
```

```
Te dukkhamicchanti punabbhavesino, cittena nītā niraye nirākatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1116.</p>

```
‘‘‘Mayūrakoñcābhirutamhi kānane, dīpīhi byagghehi purakkhato vasaṃ;
```

```
Kāye apekkhaṃ jaha mā virādhaya’, itissu maṃ citta pure niyuñjasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1117.</p>

```
‘‘‘Bhāvehi <pb ed="P" n="0.0100" /> jhānāni ca indriyāni ca, balāni bojjhaṅgasamādhibhāvanā;
```

```
Tisso ca vijjā phusa buddhasāsane’, itissu maṃ citta pure niyuñjasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1118.</p>

```
‘‘‘Bhāvehi maggaṃ amatassa pattiyā, niyyānikaṃ sabbadukhakkhayogadhaṃ;
```

```
Aṭṭhaṅgikaṃ sabbakilesasodhanaṃ’, itissu maṃ citta pure niyuñjasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1119.</p>

```
‘‘‘Dukkhanti khandhe paṭipassa yoniso, yato <pb ed="T" n="0.0419" /> ca dukkhaṃ samudeti taṃ jaha;
```

```
Idheva dukkhassa karohi antaṃ’, itissu maṃ citta pure niyuñjasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1120.</p>

```
‘‘‘Aniccaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0287" /> dukkhanti vipassa yoniso, suññaṃ anattāti aghaṃ vadhanti ca;
```

```
Manovicāre uparundha cetaso’, itissu maṃ citta pure niyuñjasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1121.</p>

```
‘‘‘Muṇḍo virūpo abhisāpamāgato, kapālahatthova kulesu bhikkhasu;
```

```
Yuñjassu satthuvacane mahesino’, itissu maṃ citta pure niyuñjasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1122.</p>

```
‘‘‘Susaṃvutatto <pb ed="M" n="0.0358" /> visikhantare caraṃ, kulesu kāmesu asaṅgamānaso;
```

```
Cando yathā dosinapuṇṇamāsiyā’, itissu maṃ citta pure niyuñjasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1123.</p>

```
‘‘‘Āraññiko hohi ca piṇḍapātiko, sosāniko hohi ca paṃsukūliko;
```

```
Nesajjiko hohi sadā dhute rato’, itissu maṃ citta pure niyuñjasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1124.</p>

```
‘‘Ropetva <pb ed="T" n="0.0420" /> rukkhāni yathā phalesī, mūle taruṃ chettu tameva icchasi;
```

```
Tathūpamaṃ cittamidaṃ karosi, yaṃ maṃ aniccamhi cale niyuñjasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1125.</p>

```
‘‘Arūpa dūraṅgama ekacāri, na te karissaṃ vacanaṃ idānihaṃ;
```

```
Dukkhā hi kāmā kaṭukā mahabbhayā, nibbānamevābhimano carissaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1126.</p>

```
‘‘Nāhaṃ alakkhyā ahirikkatāya vā, na cittahetū na ca dūrakantanā;
```

```
Ājīvahetū ca ahaṃ na nikkhamiṃ, kato ca te citta paṭissavo mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1127.</p>

```
‘‘‘Appicchatā sappurisehi vaṇṇitā, makkhappahānaṃ vūpasamo dukhassa’;
```

```
Itissu <pb ed="P" n="0.0101" /> maṃ citta tadā niyuñjasi, idāni tvaṃ gacchasi pubbaciṇṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1128.</p>

```
‘‘Taṇhā avijjā ca piyāpiyañca, subhāni rūpāni sukhā ca vedanā;
```

```
Manāpiyā kāmaguṇā ca vantā, vante ahaṃ āvamituṃ na ussahe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1129.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbattha <pb ed="T" n="0.0421" /><pb ed="M" n="0.0359" /> te citta vaco kataṃ mayā, bahūsu jātīsu na mesi kopito;
```

```
Ajjhattasambhavo kataññutāya te, dukkhe ciraṃ saṃsaritaṃ tayā kate.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1130.</p>

```
‘‘Tvaññeva no citta karosi brāhmaṇo <note>brāhmaṇe (sī.), brāhmaṇaṃ (?) bhāvalopa-tappadhānatā gahetabbā</note>, tvaṃ khattiyo rājadasī <note>rājadisī (syā. ka.)</note> karosi;
```

```
Vessā ca suddā ca bhavāma ekadā, devattanaṃ vāpi taveva vāhasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1131.</p>

```
‘‘Taveva hetū asurā bhavāmase, tvaṃmūlakaṃ nerayikā bhavāmase;
```

```
Atho tiracchānagatāpi ekadā, petattanaṃ vāpi taveva vāhasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1132.</p>

```
‘‘Nanu dubbhissasi maṃ punappunaṃ, muhuṃ muhuṃ cāraṇikaṃva dassayaṃ;
```

```
Ummattakeneva mayā palobhasi, kiñcāpi te citta virādhitaṃ mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1133.</p>

```
‘‘Idaṃ pure cittamacāri cārikaṃ, yenicchakaṃ yatthakāmaṃ yathāsukhaṃ;
```

```
Tadajjahaṃ niggahessāmi yoniso, hatthippabhinnaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0422" /> viya aṅkusaggaho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1134.</p>

```
‘‘Satthā <pb ed="V" n="0.0288" /> ca me lokamimaṃ adhiṭṭhahi, aniccato addhuvato asārato;
```

```
Pakkhanda maṃ citta jinassa sāsane, tārehi oghā mahatā suduttarā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1135.</p>

```
‘‘Na te idaṃ citta yathā purāṇakaṃ, nāhaṃ alaṃ tuyha vase nivattituṃ <note>vasena vattituṃ (?)</note>;
```

```
Mahesino pabbajitomhi sāsane, na mādisā honti vināsadhārino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1136.</p>

```
‘‘Nagā <pb ed="M" n="0.0360" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0102" /> samuddā saritā vasundharā, disā catasso vidisā adho divā;
```

```
Sabbe aniccā tibhavā upaddutā, kuhiṃ gato citta sukhaṃ ramissasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1137.</p>

```
‘‘Dhitipparaṃ kiṃ mama citta kāhisi, na te alaṃ citta vasānuvattako;
```

```
Na jātu bhastaṃ ubhatomukhaṃ chupe, dhiratthu pūraṃ nava sotasandaniṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1138.</p>

```
‘‘Varāhaeṇeyyavigāḷhasevite, pabbhārakuṭṭe pakateva sundare;
```

```
Navambunā pāvusasitthakānane, tahiṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0423" /> guhāgehagato ramissasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1139.</p>

```
‘‘Sunīlagīvā susikhā supekhunā, sucittapattacchadanā vihaṅgamā;
```

```
Sumañjughosatthanitābhigajjino, te taṃ ramessanti vanamhi jhāyinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1140.</p>

```
‘‘Vuṭṭhamhi deve caturaṅgule tiṇe, saṃpupphite meghanibhamhi kānane;
```

```
Nagantare viṭapisamo sayissaṃ, taṃ me mudū hehiti tūlasannibhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1141.</p>

```
‘‘Tathā tu kassāmi yathāpi issaro, yaṃ labbhati tenapi hotu me alaṃ;
```

```
Na tāhaṃ kassāmi yathā atandito, biḷārabhastaṃva yathā sumadditaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1142.</p>

```
‘‘Tathā tu kassāmi yathāpi issaro, yaṃ labbhati tenapi hotu me alaṃ;
```

```
Vīriyena taṃ mayha vasānayissaṃ, gajaṃva mattaṃ kusalaṅkusaggaho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1143.</p>

```
‘‘Tayā <pb ed="M" n="0.0361" /> sudantena avaṭṭhitena hi, hayena <pb ed="T" n="0.0424" /> yoggācariyova ujjunā;
```

```
Pahomi maggaṃ paṭipajjituṃ sivaṃ, cittānurakkhīhi sadā nisevitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1144.</p>

```
‘‘Ārammaṇe <pb ed="P" n="0.0103" /> taṃ balasā nibandhisaṃ, nāgaṃva thambhamhi daḷhāya rajjuyā;
```

```
Taṃ me suguttaṃ satiyā subhāvitaṃ, anissitaṃ sabbabhavesu hehisi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1145.</p>

```
‘‘Paññāya chetvā vipathānusārinaṃ, yogena niggayha pathe nivesiya;
```

```
Disvā samudayaṃ vibhavañca sambhavaṃ, dāyādako hehisi aggavādino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1146.</p>

```
‘‘Catubbipallāsavasaṃ adhiṭṭhitaṃ, gāmaṇḍalaṃva parinesi citta maṃ;
```

```
Nanu <note>nūna (sī.)</note> saṃyojanabandhanacchidaṃ, saṃsevase kāruṇikaṃ mahāmuniṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1147.</p>

```
‘‘Migo yathā seri sucittakānane, rammaṃ giriṃ pāvusaabbhamāliniṃ <note>māliṃ (?)</note>;
```

```
Anākule tattha nage ramissaṃ <note>ramissasi (syā. ka.)</note>, asaṃsayaṃ citta parā bhavissasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1148.</p>

```
‘‘Ye <pb ed="T" n="0.0425" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0289" /> tuyha chandena vasena vattino, narā ca nārī ca anubhonti yaṃ sukhaṃ;
```

```
Aviddasū māravasānuvattino, bhavābhinandī tava citta sāvakā’’ti.
```

… Tālapuṭo thero….

<trailer rend="centre">Paññāsanipāto niṭṭhito.</trailer>

Tatruddānaṃ –

```
Paññāsamhi nipātamhi, eko tālapuṭo suci;
```

```
Gāthāyo tattha paññāsa, puna pañca ca uttarīti.
```

### 20. Saṭṭhinipāto

#### 1. Mahāmoggallānattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§1149.</p>

```
‘‘Āraññikā <pb ed="M" n="0.0362" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0290" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0104" /> piṇḍapātikā, uñchāpattāgate ratā;
```

```
Dālemu maccuno senaṃ, ajjhattaṃ susamāhitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1150.</p>

```
‘‘Āraññikā piṇḍapātikā, uñchāpattāgate ratā;
```

```
Dhunāma <pb ed="T" n="0.0426" /> maccuno senaṃ, naḷāgāraṃva kuñjaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1151.</p>

```
‘‘Rukkhamūlikā sātatikā, uñchāpattāgate ratā;
```

```
Dālemu maccuno senaṃ, ajjhattaṃ susamāhitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1152.</p>

```
‘‘Rukkhamūlikā sātatikā, uñchāpattāgate ratā;
```

```
Dhunāma maccuno senaṃ, naḷāgāraṃva kuñjaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1153.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhikaṅkalakuṭike, maṃsanhārupasibbite;
```

```
Dhiratthu pure duggandhe, paragatte mamāyase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1154.</p>

```
‘‘Gūthabhaste taconaddhe, uragaṇḍipisācini;
```

```
Nava sotāni te kāye, yāni sandanti sabbadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1155.</p>

```
‘‘Tava sarīraṃ navasotaṃ, duggandhakaraṃ paribandhaṃ;
```

```
Bhikkhu parivajjayate taṃ, mīḷhaṃ ca yathā sucikāmo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1156.</p>

```
‘‘Evañce taṃ jano jaññā, yathā jānāmi taṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Ārakā parivajjeyya, gūthaṭṭhānaṃva pāvuse’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1157.</p>

```
‘‘Evametaṃ mahāvīra, yathā samaṇa bhāsasi;
```

```
Ettha ceke visīdanti, paṅkamhiva jaraggavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1158.</p>

```
‘‘Ākāsamhi haliddiyā, yo maññetha rajetave;
```

```
Aññena vāpi raṅgena, vighātudayameva taṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1159.</p>

```
‘‘Tadākāsasamaṃ cittaṃ, ajjhattaṃ susamāhitaṃ;
```

```
Mā pāpacitte āsādi, aggikhandhaṃva pakkhimā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1160.</p>

```
‘‘Passa cittakataṃ bimbaṃ, arukāyaṃ samussitaṃ;
```

```
Āturaṃ bahusaṅkappaṃ, yassa natthi dhuvaṃ ṭhiti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1161.</p>

```
‘‘Passa <pb ed="V" n="0.0291" /> cittakataṃ rūpaṃ, maṇinā kuṇḍalena ca;
```

```
Aṭṭhiṃ tacena onaddhaṃ, saha vatthehi sobhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1162.</p>

```
‘‘Alattakakatā <pb ed="M" n="0.0363" /> pādā, mukhaṃ cuṇṇakamakkhitaṃ;
```

```
Alaṃ bālassa mohāya, no ca pāragavesino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1163.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhapadakatā kesā, nettā añjanamakkhitā;
```

```
Alaṃ bālassa mohāya, no ca pāragavesino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1164.</p>

```
‘‘Añjanīva navā cittā, pūtikāyo alaṅkato;
```

```
Alaṃ bālassa mohāya, no ca pāragavesino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1165.</p>

```
‘‘Odahi migavo pāsaṃ, nāsadā vāguraṃ migo;
```

```
Bhutvā nivāpaṃ gacchāma, kaddante migabandhake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1166.</p>

```
‘‘Chinno pāso migavassa, nāsadā vāguraṃ migo;
```

```
Bhutvā nivāpaṃ gacchāma, socante migaluddake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1167.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāsi yaṃ bhiṃsanakaṃ, tadāsi lomahaṃsanaṃ;
```

```
Anekākārasampanne, sāriputtamhi nibbute.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1168.</p>

```
<note>dī. ni. 2.221, 272; saṃ. ni. 1.186; 2.143; apa. thera 1.2.115; jā. 1.1.95</note> ‘‘Aniccā <pb ed="T" n="0.0427" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0105" /> vata saṅkhārā uppādavaya dhammino.
```

```
Upajjitvā nirujjhanti, tesaṃ vūpasamo sukho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1169.</p>

```
‘‘Sukhumaṃ te paṭivijjhanti, vālaggaṃ usunā yathā;
```

```
Ye pañcakkhandhe passanti, parato no ca attato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1170.</p>

```
‘‘Ye ca passanti saṅkhāre, parato no ca attato;
```

```
Paccabyādhiṃsu nipuṇaṃ, vālaggaṃ usunā yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1171.</p>

```
<note>saṃ. ni. 1.21, 97</note> ‘‘Sattiyā viya omaṭṭho, ḍayhamānova matthake;
```

```
Kāmarāgappahānāya, sato bhikkhu paribbaje.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1172.</p>

```
<note>saṃ. ni. 1.21, 97</note>‘‘Sattiyā viya omaṭṭho, ḍayhamānova matthake;
```

```
Bhavarāgappahānāya, sato bhikkhu paribbaje’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1173.</p>

```
‘‘Codito bhāvitattena, sarīrantimadhārinā;
```

```
Migāramātupāsādaṃ, pādaṅguṭṭhena kampayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1174.</p>

```
‘‘Nayidaṃ sithilamārabbha, nayidaṃ appena thāmasā;
```

```
Nibbānamadhigantabbaṃ, sabbagantha-pamocanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1175.</p>

```
‘‘Ayañca <pb ed="V" n="0.0292" /> daharo bhikkhu, ayamuttamaporiso;
```

```
Dhāreti antimaṃ dehaṃ, jetvā māraṃ savāhiniṃ <note>savāhanaṃ (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1176.</p>

```
‘‘Vivaramanupabhanti <pb ed="M" n="0.0364" /> vijjutā, vebhārassa ca paṇḍavassa ca;
```

```
Nagavivaragato jhāyati, putto appaṭimassa tādino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1177.</p>

```
‘‘Upasanto uparato, pantasenāsano muni;
```

```
Dāyādo <pb ed="T" n="0.0428" /> buddhaseṭṭhassa, brahmunā abhivandito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1178.</p>

```
‘‘Upasantaṃ uparataṃ, pantasenāsanaṃ muniṃ;
```

```
Dāyādaṃ buddhaseṭṭhassa, vanda brāhmaṇa kassapaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1179.</p>

```
‘‘Yo ca jātisataṃ gacche, sabbā brāhmaṇajātiyo;
```

```
Sottiyo vedasampanno, manussesu punappunaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1180.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjhāyakopi ce assa, tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragū;
```

```
Etassa vandanāyetaṃ, kalaṃ nāgghati soḷasiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1181.</p>

```
‘‘Yo so aṭṭha vimokkhāni, purebhattaṃ aphassayi <note>apassayi (sī. ka.), aphussayi (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Anulomaṃ paṭilomaṃ, tato piṇḍāya gacchati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1182.</p>

```
‘‘Tādisaṃ bhikkhuṃ māsādi <note>mā hani (sī.)</note>, māttānaṃ khaṇi brāhmaṇa;
```

```
Abhippasādehi manaṃ, arahantamhi tādine;
```

```
Khippaṃ pañjaliko vanda, mā te vijaṭi matthakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1183.</p>

```
‘‘Neso passati saddhammaṃ, saṃsārena purakkhato;
```

```
Adhogamaṃ jimhapathaṃ, kummaggamanudhāvati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1184.</p>

```
‘‘Kimīva mīḷhasallitto, saṅkhāre adhimucchito;
```

```
Pagāḷho lābhasakkāre, tuccho gacchati poṭṭhilo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1185.</p>

```
‘‘Imañca passa āyantaṃ, sāriputtaṃ sudassanaṃ;
```

```
Vimuttaṃ ubhatobhāge, ajjhattaṃ susamāhitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1186.</p>

```
‘‘Visallaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0106" /> khīṇasaṃyogaṃ, tevijjaṃ maccuhāyinaṃ;
```

```
Dakkhiṇeyyaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0429" /> manussānaṃ, puññakkhettaṃ anuttaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1187.</p>

```
‘‘Ete sambahulā devā, iddhimanto yasassino;
```

```
Dasa devasahassāni, sabbe brahmapurohitā;
```

```
Moggallānaṃ namassantā, tiṭṭhanti pañjalīkatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1188.</p>

```
‘‘‘Namo <pb ed="V" n="0.0293" /> te purisājañña, namo te purisuttama;
```

```
Yassa te āsavā khīṇā, dakkhiṇeyyosi mārisa’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1189.</p>

```
‘‘Pūjito <pb ed="M" n="0.0365" /> naradevena, uppanno maraṇābhibhū;
```

```
Puṇḍarīkaṃva toyena, saṅkhārenupalippati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1190.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa muhuttena sahassadhā loko, saṃvidito sabrahmakappo vasi;
```

```
Iddhiguṇe cutupapāte kāle, passati devatā sa bhikkhu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1191.</p>

```
‘‘Sāriputtova paññāya, sīlena upasamena ca;
```

```
Yopi pāraṅgato bhikkhu, etāvaparamo siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1192.</p>

```
‘‘Koṭisatasahassassa, attabhāvaṃ khaṇena nimmine;
```

```
Ahaṃ vikubbanāsu kusalo, vasībhūtomhi iddhiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1193.</p>

```
‘‘Samādhivijjāvasipāramīgato, moggallānagotto asitassa sāsane;
```

```
Dhīro samucchindi samāhitindriyo, nāgo <pb ed="T" n="0.0430" /> yathā pūtilataṃva bandhanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1194.</p>

```
‘‘Pariciṇṇo mayā satthā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ;
```

```
Ohito garuko bhāro, bhavanetti samūhatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1195.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa catthāya pabbajito, agārasmānagāriyaṃ;
```

```
So me attho anuppatto, sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1196.</p>

```
<note>ma. ni. 1.513</note> ‘‘Kīdiso nirayo āsi, yattha dussī apaccatha;
```

```
Vidhuraṃ sāvakamāsajja, kakusandhañca brāhmaṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1197.</p>

```
‘‘Sataṃ āsi ayosaṅkū, sabbe paccattavedanā;
```

```
Īdiso nirayo āsi, yattha dussī apaccatha;
```

```
Vidhuraṃ sāvakamāsajja, kakusandhañca brāhmaṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1198.</p>

```
‘‘Yo etamabhijānāti, bhikkhu buddhassa sāvako;
```

```
Tādisaṃ bhikkhumāsajja, kaṇha dukkhaṃ nigacchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1199.</p>

```
‘‘Majjhesarasmiṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0107" /> <note>sarassa (sī.), sāgarasmiṃ (ka.)</note> tiṭṭhanti, vimānā kappaṭhāyino;
```

```
Veḷuriyavaṇṇā rucirā, accimanto pabhassarā;
```

```
Accharā tattha naccanti, puthu nānattavaṇṇiyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1200.</p>

```
‘‘Yo <pb ed="T" n="0.0431" /><pb ed="M" n="0.0366" /> etamabhijānāti…pe… kaṇha dukkhaṃ nigacchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1201.</p>

```
‘‘Yo ve buddhena codito, bhikkhusaṅghassa pekkhato;
```

```
Migāramātupāsādaṃ, pādaṅguṭṭhena kampayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1202.</p>

```
‘‘Yo etamabhijānāti…pe… kaṇha dukkhaṃ nigacchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1203.</p>

```
‘‘Yo <pb ed="V" n="0.0294" /> vejayantapāsādaṃ, pādaṅguṭṭhena kampayi;
```

```
Iddhibalenupatthaddho, saṃvejesi ca devatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1204.</p>

```
‘‘Yo etamabhijānāti…pe… kaṇha dukkhaṃ nigacchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1204.</p>

```
‘‘Yo etamabhijānāti…pe… kaṇha dukkhaṃ nigacchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1205.</p>

```
‘‘Yo vejayantapāsāde, sakkaṃ so paripucchati;
```

```
Api āvuso jānāsi, taṇhakkhayavimuttiyo;
```

```
Tassa sakko viyākāsi, pañhaṃ puṭṭho yathātathaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1206.</p>

```
‘‘Yo etamabhijānāti…pe… kaṇha dukkhaṃ nigacchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1207.</p>

```
‘‘Yo brahmānaṃ paripucchati, sudhammāyaṃ ṭhito <note>sudhammāyā’bhito (syā.)</note> sabhaṃ;
```

```
Ajjāpi tyāvuso sā diṭṭhi, yā te diṭṭhi pure ahu;
```

```
Passasi vītivattantaṃ, brahmaloke pabhassaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1208.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa brahmā viyākāsi, pañhaṃ puṭṭho yathātathaṃ;
```

```
Na me mārisa sā diṭṭhi, yā me diṭṭhi pure ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1209.</p>

```
‘‘Passāmi vītivattantaṃ, brahmaloke pabhassaraṃ;
```

```
Sohaṃ ajja kathaṃ vajjaṃ, ahaṃ niccomhi sassato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1210.</p>

```
‘‘Yo etamabhijānāti…pe… kaṇha dukkhaṃ nigacchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1211.</p>

```
‘‘Yo mahāneruno kūṭaṃ, vimokkhena aphassayi <note>apassayi (sī. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Vanaṃ pubbavidehānaṃ, ye ca bhūmisayā narā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1212.</p>

```
‘‘Yo etamabhijānāti, bhikkhu buddhassa sāvako;
```

```
Tādisaṃ bhikkhumāsajja, kaṇha dukkhaṃ nigacchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1213.</p>

```
‘‘Na ve aggi cetayati, ahaṃ bālaṃ ḍahāmīti;
```

```
Bālova jalitaṃ aggiṃ, āsajja naṃ paḍayhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1214.</p>

```
‘‘Evameva tuvaṃ māra, āsajja naṃ tathāgataṃ;
```

```
Sayaṃ ḍahissasi attānaṃ, bālo aggiṃva samphusaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1215.</p>

```
‘‘Apuññaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0432" /><pb ed="M" n="0.0367" /> pasavī māro, āsajja naṃ tathāgataṃ;
```

```
Kiṃ nu maññasi pāpima, na me pāpaṃ vipaccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1216.</p>

```
‘‘Karato te cīyate <note>miyyate (sabbattha) ma. ni. 1.513 passitabbaṃ</note> pāpaṃ, cirarattāya antaka;
```

```
Māra nibbinda buddhamhā, āsaṃ mākāsi bhikkhusu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1217.</p>

```
‘‘Iti <pb ed="V" n="0.0295" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0108" /> māraṃ atajjesi, bhikkhu bhesakaḷāvane;
```

```
Tato so dummano yakkho, tatthevantaradhāyathā’’ti.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mahāmoggallāno <note>mahāmoggalāno (ka.)</note> thero gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

<trailer rend="centre">Saṭṭhinipāto niṭṭhito.</trailer>

Tatruddānaṃ –

```
Saṭṭhikamhi nipātamhi, moggallāno mahiddhiko;
```

```
Ekova theragāthāyo, aṭṭhasaṭṭhi bhavanti tāti.
```

### 21. Mahānipāto

#### 1. Vaṅgīsattheragāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§1218.</p>

```
‘‘Nikkhantaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0368" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0296" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0109" /> vata maṃ santaṃ, agārasmānagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Vitakkā upadhāvanti, pagabbhā kaṇhato ime.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1219.</p>

```
‘‘Uggaputtā mahissāsā, sikkhitā daḷhadhammino <note>daḷhadhanvino (sī. aṭṭha.)</note>;
```

```
Samantā parikireyyuṃ, sahassaṃ apalāyinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1220.</p>

```
‘‘Sacepi ettakā <note>etato (saṃ. ni. 1.209)</note> bhiyyo, āgamissanti itthiyo;
```

```
Neva maṃ byādhayissanti <note>byāthayissanti (?)</note>, dhamme samhi <note>dhammesvamhi (syā. ka.)</note> patiṭṭhito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1221.</p>

```
‘‘Sakkhī <pb ed="T" n="0.0433" /> hi me sutaṃ etaṃ, buddhassādiccabandhuno;
```

```
Nibbānagamanaṃ maggaṃ, tattha me nirato mano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1222.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ ce maṃ viharantaṃ, pāpima upagacchasi;
```

```
Tathā maccu karissāmi, na me maggampi dakkhasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1223.</p>

```
‘‘Aratiñca <note>aratiṃ (bahūsu)</note> ratiñca pahāya, sabbaso gehasitañca vitakkaṃ;
```

```
Vanathaṃ na kareyya kuhiñci, nibbanatho avanatho sa <note>nibbanatho arato sa hi (saṃ. ni. 1.210)</note> bhikkhu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1224.</p>

```
‘‘Yamidha pathaviñca vehāsaṃ, rūpagataṃ jagatogadhaṃ kiñci;
```

```
Parijīyati sabbamaniccaṃ, evaṃ samecca caranti mutattā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1225.</p>

```
‘‘Upadhīsu janā gadhitāse, diṭṭhasute <note>diṭṭhe sute (sī.)</note> paṭighe ca mute ca;
```

```
Ettha vinodaya chandamanejo, yo hettha na limpati muni tamāhu <note>taṃ munimāhu (saṃ. ni. 1.210)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1226.</p>

```
‘‘Atha <pb ed="M" n="0.0369" /> saṭṭhisitā savitakkā, puthujjanatāya <note>puthū janatāya (saṃ. ni. 1.210)</note> adhammā niviṭṭhā;
```

```
Na ca vaggagatassa kuhiñci, no pana duṭṭhullagāhī <note>duṭṭhullabhāṇī (saṃ. ni. 1.210)</note> sa bhikkhu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1227.</p>

```
‘‘Dabbo <pb ed="P" n="0.0110" /> cirarattasamāhito, akuhako nipako apihālu;
```

```
Santaṃ padaṃ ajjhagamā muni, paṭicca parinibbuto kaṅkhati kālaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1228.</p>

```
‘‘Mānaṃ pajahassu gotama, mānapathañca jahassu asesaṃ;
```

```
Mānapathamhi sa mucchito, vippaṭisārīhuvā cirarattaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1229.</p>

```
‘‘Makkhena makkhitā pajā, mānahatā nirayaṃ papatanti;
```

```
Socanti janā cirarattaṃ, mānahatā nirayaṃ upapannā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1230.</p>

```
‘‘Na <pb ed="V" n="0.0297" /> hi socati bhikkhu kadāci, maggajino sammā paṭipanno;
```

```
Kittiñca <pb ed="T" n="0.0434" /> sukhañcānubhoti, dhammadasoti tamāhu tathattaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1231.</p>

```
‘‘Tasmā akhilo idha <note>akhilo (sī.), akhilodha (saṃ. ni. 1.211)</note> padhānavā, nīvaraṇāni pahāya visuddho;
```

```
Mānañca pahāya asesaṃ, vijjāyantakaro samitāvī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1232.</p>

```
‘‘Kāmarāgena ḍayhāmi, cittaṃ me pariḍayhati;
```

```
Sādhu nibbāpanaṃ brūhi, anukampāya gotama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1233.</p>

```
‘‘Saññāya <pb ed="M" n="0.0370" /> vipariyesā, cittaṃ te pariḍayhati;
```

```
Nimittaṃ parivajjehi, subhaṃ rāgūpasaṃhitaṃ ( ) <note>(saṅkhāre parato passa, dukkhato mā ca attato; nibbāpehi mahārāgaṃ, mā dayhittho punappunaṃ;) (sī. saṃ. ni. 1.212) uddānagāthāyaṃ ekasattatītisaṅkhyā ca, theragāthāṭṭhakathā ca passitabbā</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1234.</p>

```
‘‘Asubhāya cittaṃ bhāvehi, ekaggaṃ susamāhitaṃ;
```

```
Sati kāyagatā tyatthu, nibbidābahulo bhava.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1235.</p>

```
‘‘Animittañca bhāvehi, mānānusayamujjaha;
```

```
Tato mānābhisamayā, upasanto carissasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1236.</p>

```
‘‘Tameva vācaṃ bhāseyya, yāyattānaṃ na tāpaye;
```

```
Pare ca na vihiṃseyya, sā ve vācā subhāsitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1237.</p>

```
‘‘Piyavācameva bhāseyya, yā vācā paṭinanditā;
```

```
Yaṃ anādāya pāpāni, paresaṃ bhāsate piyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1238.</p>

```
‘‘Saccaṃ ve amatā vācā, esa dhammo sanantano;
```

```
Sacce atthe ca dhamme ca, āhu santo patiṭṭhitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1239.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ buddho bhāsati vācaṃ, khemaṃ nibbānapattiyā;
```

```
Dukkhassantakiriyāya, sā ve vācānamuttamā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1240.</p>

```
‘‘Gambhīrapañño medhāvī, maggāmaggassa kovido;
```

```
Sāriputto <pb ed="T" n="0.0435" /> mahāpañño, dhammaṃ deseti bhikkhunaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1241.</p>

```
‘‘Saṅkhittenapi deseti, vitthārenapi bhāsati;
```

```
Sālikāyiva nigghoso, paṭibhānaṃ udiyyati <note>udīrayi (sī.), udīyyati (syā.), udayyati (?) uṭṭhahatīti taṃsaṃvaṇṇanā</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1242.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa <pb ed="P" n="0.0111" /> taṃ desayantassa, suṇanti madhuraṃ giraṃ;
```

```
Sarena rajanīyena, savanīyena vaggunā;
```

```
Udaggacittā muditā, sotaṃ odhenti bhikkhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1243.</p>

```
‘‘Ajja pannarase visuddhiyā, bhikkhū pañcasatā samāgatā;
```

```
Saṃyojanabandhanacchidā, anīghā khīṇapunabbhavā isī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1244.</p>

```
‘‘Cakkavattī <pb ed="V" n="0.0298" /> yathā rājā, amaccaparivārito;
```

```
Samantā anupariyeti, sāgarantaṃ mahiṃ imaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1245.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0371" /> vijitasaṅgāmaṃ, satthavāhaṃ anuttaraṃ;
```

```
Sāvakā payirupāsanti, tevijjā maccuhāyino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1246.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbe bhagavato puttā, palāpettha na vijjati;
```

```
Taṇhāsallassa hantāraṃ, vande ādiccabandhunaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1247.</p>

```
‘‘Parosahassaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ, sugataṃ payirupāsati;
```

```
Desentaṃ virajaṃ dhammaṃ, nibbānaṃ akutobhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1248.</p>

```
‘‘Suṇanti dhammaṃ vimalaṃ, sammāsambuddhadesitaṃ;
```

```
Sobhati vata sambuddho, bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1249.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nāganāmo’si bhagavā, isīnaṃ isisattamo;
```

```
Mahāmeghova hutvāna, sāvake abhivassasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1250.</p>

```
‘‘Divā <pb ed="T" n="0.0436" /> vihārā nikkhamma, satthudassanakamyatā;
```

```
Sāvako te mahāvīra, pāde vandati vaṅgiso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1251.</p>

```
‘‘Ummaggapathaṃ mārassa, abhibhuyya carati pabhijja khīlāni;
```

```
Taṃ passatha bandhapamuñcakaraṃ, asitaṃva bhāgaso pavibhajja.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1252.</p>

```
‘‘Oghassa hi nitaraṇatthaṃ, anekavihitaṃ maggaṃ akkhāsi;
```

```
Tasmiñca amate akkhāte, dhammadasā ṭhitā asaṃhīrā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1253.</p>

```
‘‘Pajjotakaro ativijjha <note>ativijjha dhammaṃ (sī.)</note>, sabbaṭhitīnaṃ atikkamamaddasa <note>atikkamamadda (sī. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Ñatvā ca sacchikatvā ca, aggaṃ so desayi dasaddhānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1254.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ sudesite dhamme, ko pamādo vijānataṃ dhammaṃ;
```

```
Tasmā hi tassa bhagavato sāsane, appamatto sadā namassamanusikkhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1255.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhānubuddho yo thero, koṇḍañño tibbanikkamo;
```

```
Lābhī sukhavihārānaṃ, vivekānaṃ abhiṇhaso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1256.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0372" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0112" /> sāvakena pattabbaṃ, satthu sāsanakārinā;
```

```
Sabbassa taṃ anuppattaṃ, appamattassa sikkhato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1257.</p>

```
‘‘Mahānubhāvo tevijjo, cetopariyakovido;
```

```
Koṇḍañño buddhadāyādo, pāde vandati satthuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1258.</p>

```
‘‘Nagassa <pb ed="V" n="0.0299" /> passe āsīnaṃ, muniṃ dukkhassa pāraguṃ;
```

```
Sāvakā payirupāsanti, tevijjā maccuhāyino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1259.</p>

```
‘‘Cetasā <note>te cetasā (saṃ. ni. 1.218)</note> anupariyeti, moggallāno mahiddhiko;
```

```
Cittaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0437" /> nesaṃ samanvesaṃ <note>samannesaṃ (saṃ. ni. 1.218)</note>, vippamuttaṃ nirūpadhiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1260.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ sabbaṅgasampannaṃ, muniṃ dukkhassa pāraguṃ;
```

```
Anekākārasampannaṃ, payirupāsanti gotamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1261.</p>

```
‘‘Cando yathā vigatavalāhake nabhe, virocati vītamalova bhāṇumā;
```

```
Evampi aṅgīrasa tvaṃ mahāmuni, atirocasi yasasā sabbalokaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1262.</p>

```
‘‘Kāveyyamattā vicarimha pubbe, gāmā gāmaṃ purā puraṃ;
```

```
Athaddasāma sambuddhaṃ, sabbadhammāna pāraguṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1263.</p>

```
‘‘So me dhammamadesesi, muni dukkhassa pāragū;
```

```
Dhammaṃ sutvā pasīdimha, saddhā <note>addhā (sī. aṭṭha.)</note> no udapajjatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1264.</p>

```
‘‘Tassāhaṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, khandhe āyatanāni ca;
```

```
Dhātuyo ca viditvāna, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1265.</p>

```
‘‘Bahūnaṃ vata atthāya, uppajjanti tathāgatā;
```

```
Itthīnaṃ purisānañca, ye te sāsanakārakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1266.</p>

```
‘‘Tesaṃ kho vata atthāya, bodhimajjhagamā muni;
```

```
Bhikkhūnaṃ bhikkhunīnañca, ye nirāmagataddasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1267.</p>

```
‘‘Sudesitā cakkhumatā, buddhenādiccabandhunā;
```

```
Cattāri ariyasaccāni, anukampāya pāṇinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1268.</p>

```
‘‘Dukkhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0373" /> dukkhasamuppādaṃ, dukkhassa ca atikkamaṃ;
```

```
Ariyaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0438" /> caṭṭhaṅgikaṃ maggaṃ, dukkhūpasamagāminaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1269.</p>

```
‘‘Evamete tathā vuttā, diṭṭhā me te yathā tathā;
```

```
Sadattho me anuppatto, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1270.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
```

```
Suvibhattesu <note>savibhattesu (sī. ka.)</note> dhammesu, yaṃ seṭṭhaṃ tadupāgamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1271.</p>

```
‘‘Abhiññāpāramippatto, sotadhātu visodhitā;
```

```
Tevijjo iddhipattomhi, cetopariyakovido.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1272.</p>

```
‘‘Pucchāmi <pb ed="P" n="0.0113" /> satthāramanomapaññaṃ, diṭṭheva dhamme yo vicikicchānaṃ chettā;
```

```
Aggāḷave kālamakāsi bhikkhu, ñāto yasassī abhinibbutatto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1273.</p>

```
‘‘Nigrodhakappo <pb ed="V" n="0.0300" /> iti tassa nāmaṃ, tayā kataṃ bhagavā brāhmaṇassa;
```

```
So taṃ namassaṃ acari mutyapekho, āraddhavīriyo daḷhadhammadassī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1274.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ sāvakaṃ sakka mayampi sabbe, aññātumicchāma samantacakkhu;
```

```
Samavaṭṭhitā no savanāya sotā <note>hetuṃ (sī. syā.) suttanipātaṭṭhakathā passitabbā</note>, tuvaṃ no satthā tvamanuttarosi’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1275.</p>

```
Chinda <pb ed="T" n="0.0439" /> no vicikicchaṃ brūhi metaṃ, parinibbutaṃ vedaya bhūripañña;
```

```
Majjheva no bhāsa samantacakkhu, sakkova devāna sahassanetto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1276.</p>

```
‘‘Ye keci ganthā idha mohamaggā, aññāṇapakkhā vicikicchaṭhānā;
```

```
Tathāgataṃ patvā na te bhavanti, cakkhuñhi etaṃ paramaṃ narānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1277.</p>

```
‘‘No <pb ed="M" n="0.0374" /> ce hi jātu puriso kilese, vāto yathā abbhaghanaṃ vihāne;
```

```
Tamovassa nivuto sabbaloko, jotimantopi na pabhāseyyuṃ <note>na jotimantopi narā tapeyyuṃ (su. ni. 350)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1278.</p>

```
‘‘Dhīrā ca pajjotakarā bhavanti, taṃ taṃ ahaṃ vīra tatheva maññe;
```

```
Vipassinaṃ jānamupāgamimha, parisāsu no āvikarohi kappaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1279.</p>

```
‘‘Khippaṃ giraṃ eraya vaggu vagguṃ, haṃsova paggayha saṇikaṃ nikūja;
```

```
Bindussarena <pb ed="P" n="0.0114" /> suvikappitena, sabbeva te ujjugatā suṇoma.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1280.</p>

```
‘‘Pahīnajātimaraṇaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0440" /> asesaṃ, niggayha dhonaṃ vadessāmi <note>paṭivediyāmi (sī. ka.)</note> dhammaṃ;
```

```
Na kāmakāro hi <note>hoti (sī. ka.)</note> puthujjanānaṃ, saṅkheyyakāro ca <note>va (bahūsu)</note> tathāgatānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1281.</p>

```
‘‘Sampannaveyyākaraṇaṃ tavedaṃ, samujjupaññassa samuggahītaṃ;
```

```
Ayamañjali pacchimo suppaṇāmito, mā mohayī jānamanomapañña.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1282.</p>

```
‘‘Paroparaṃ ariyadhammaṃ viditvā, mā mohayī jānamanomavīriya;
```

```
Vāriṃ yathā ghammani ghammatatto, vācābhikaṅkhāmi sutaṃ pavassa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1283.</p>

```
‘‘Yadatthikaṃ brahmacariyaṃ acarī, kappāyano kaccissataṃ amoghaṃ;
```

```
Nibbāyi so ādu saupādiseso <note>anupādisesā (sī.), anupādiseso (ka.)</note>, yathā vimutto ahu taṃ suṇoma.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1284.</p>

```
‘‘‘Acchecchi <pb ed="M" n="0.0375" /> taṇhaṃ idha nāmarūpe,
```

```
(Iti bhagavā) kaṇhassa sotaṃ dīgharattānusayitaṃ;
```

```
Atāri jātiṃ maraṇaṃ asesaṃ’, iccabravi <pb ed="T" n="0.0441" /> bhagavā pañcaseṭṭho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1285.</p>

```
‘‘Esa sutvā pasīdāmi, vaco te isisattama;
```

```
Amoghaṃ kira me puṭṭhaṃ, na maṃ vañcesi brāhmaṇo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1286.</p>

```
‘‘Yathā vādī tathā kārī, ahu buddhassa sāvako;
```

```
Acchecchi maccuno jālaṃ, tataṃ māyāvino daḷhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1287.</p>

```
‘‘Addasa <pb ed="V" n="0.0301" /> bhagavā ādiṃ, upādānassa kappiyo;
```

```
Accagā <pb ed="P" n="0.0115" /> vata kappāno, maccudheyyaṃ suduttaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1288.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ devadevaṃ vandāmi, puttaṃ te dvipaduttama;
```

```
Anujātaṃ mahāvīraṃ, nāgaṃ nāgassa orasa’’nti.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vaṅgīso thero gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

<trailer rend="centre">Mahānipāto niṭṭhito.</trailer>

Tatruddānaṃ –

```
Sattatimhi nipātamhi, vaṅgīso paṭibhāṇavā;
```

```
Ekova thero natthañño, gāthāyo ekasattatīti.
```

Niṭṭhitā theragāthāyo.

Tatruddānaṃ –

```
Sahassaṃ honti tā gāthā, tīṇi saṭṭhisatāni ca;
```

```
Therā ca dve satā saṭṭhi, cattāro ca pakāsitā.
```

```
Sīhanādaṃ naditvāna, buddhaputtā anāsavā;
```

```
Khemantaṃ pāpuṇitvāna, aggikhandhāva nibbutāti.
```

<trailer rend="centre">Theragāthāpāḷi niṭṭhitā.</trailer>
